Solving Physics Olympiad via Reinforcement Learning on Physics Simulators
Authors: Mihir Prabhudesai, Aryan Satpathy, Yangmin Li, Zheyang Qin, Nikash Bhardwaj, Amir Zadeh, Chuan Li, Katerina Fragkiadaki, Deepak Pathak
First: 2026-04-13T17:59:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T17:59:40+00:00
Comments: Project Webpage - https://sim2reason.github.io/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
We have witnessed remarkable advances in LLM reasoning capabilities with the advent of DeepSeek-R1. However, much of this progress has been fueled by the abundance of internet question-answer (QA) pairs, a major bottleneck going forward, since such data is limited in scale and concentrated mainly in domains like mathematics. In contrast, other sciences such as physics lack large-scale QA datasets to effectively train reasoning-capable models. In this work, we show that physics simulators can serve as a powerful alternative source of supervision for training LLMs for physical reasoning. We generate random scenes in physics engines, create synthetic question-answer pairs from simulated interactions, and train LLMs using reinforcement learning on this synthetic data. Our models exhibit zero-shot sim-to-real transfer to real-world physics benchmarks: for example, training solely on synthetic simulated data improves performance on IPhO (International Physics Olympiad) problems by 5-10 percentage points across model sizes. These results demonstrate that physics simulators can act as scalable data generators, enabling LLMs to acquire deep physical reasoning skills beyond the limitations of internet-scale QA data. Code available at: https://sim2reason.github.io/.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于物理模拟器的强化学习解决物理奥林匹克竞赛问题
随着DeepSeek-R1的出现，我们见证了大型语言模型推理能力的显著进步。然而，这一进展主要得益于互联网问答对数据的丰富性，这将成为未来发展的主要瓶颈，因为此类数据规模有限且主要集中在数学等领域。相比之下，物理学等其他科学领域缺乏大规模问答数据集来有效训练具备推理能力的模型。本研究证明，物理模拟器可作为训练大型语言模型进行物理推理的强大监督源。我们在物理引擎中生成随机场景，根据模拟交互创建合成问答对，并利用强化学习在此合成数据上训练模型。我们的模型展现出对真实世界物理基准的零样本模拟到现实迁移能力：例如，仅使用合成模拟数据训练，即可在不同规模模型上将国际物理奥林匹克竞赛问题的解决准确率提升5-10个百分点。这些结果表明，物理模拟器可作为可扩展的数据生成器，使大型语言模型能够突破互联网规模问答数据的限制，获得深层次的物理推理能力。代码发布于：https://sim2reason.github.io/。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the scarcity of large-scale question-answer datasets for training reasoning-capable LLMs in physics compared to domains like mathematics, this work proposes using physics simulators as an alternative source of supervision. The method involves generating random scenes in physics engines to create synthetic question-answer pairs from simulated interactions and then training LLMs via reinforcement learning on this synthetic data. The main experimental results show that models trained solely on synthetic simulated data achieve zero-shot sim-to-real transfer, improving performance on real-world physics benchmarks such as the International Physics Olympiad (IPhO) by 5-10 percentage points across different model sizes, demonstrating that physics simulators can serve as scalable data generators for acquiring deep physical reasoning skills.
本研究旨在解决物理领域缺乏大规模问答数据集来训练具备推理能力的大语言模型的问题，而数学等领域则相对数据丰富。方法上，研究利用物理模拟器生成随机场景，从模拟交互中创建合成问答对，并基于此合成数据通过强化学习训练大语言模型。主要实验结果表明，仅使用合成模拟数据训练的模型实现了零样本的模拟到现实迁移，在国际物理奥林匹克（IPhO）等真实物理基准测试上的性能提升了5-10个百分点，且在不同模型规模下均有效，这证明了物理模拟器可作为可扩展的数据生成器，帮助模型获得超越互联网问答数据局限的深层物理推理能力。
Autonomous Diffractometry Enabled by Visual Reinforcement Learning
Authors: J. Oppliger, M. Stifter, A. Rüegg, I. Biało, L. Martinelli, P. G. Freeman, D. Prabhakaran, J. Zhao, Q. Wang, J. Chang
First: 2026-04-13T17:42:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T17:42:19+00:00
Comments: 20 pages, 16 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Automation underpins progress across scientific and industrial disciplines. Yet, automating tasks requiring interpretation of abstract visual information remain challenging. For example, crystal alignment strongly relies on humans with the ability to comprehend diffraction patterns. Here we introduce an autonomous system that aligns single crystals without access to crystallography and diffraction theory. Using a model-free reinforcement learning framework, an agent learns to identify and navigate towards high-symmetry orientations directly from Laue diffraction patterns. Despite the absence of human supervision, the agent develops human-like strategies to achieve time-efficient alignment across different crystal symmetry classes. With this, we provide a computational framework for intelligent diffractometers. As such, our approach advances the development of automated experimental workflows in materials science.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于视觉强化学习的自主衍射测量技术
自动化是推动科学与工业领域进步的核心动力，但对需要解读抽象视觉信息的任务实现自动化仍具挑战。例如，晶体定向高度依赖人类对衍射图案的理解能力。本研究提出一种无需晶体学与衍射理论知识的单晶自主定向系统。通过无模型强化学习框架，智能体直接从劳厄衍射图案中学习识别并导航至高对称性取向。在无人监督的情况下，该智能体形成了类人策略，能在不同晶体对称类别中实现高效定向。本工作为智能衍射仪提供了计算框架，从而推动了材料科学自动化实验流程的发展。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of automating tasks that require interpreting abstract visual information, such as crystal alignment which traditionally relies on human expertise in reading diffraction patterns, this paper introduces an autonomous system using a model-free reinforcement learning framework. The method enables an agent to learn directly from Laue diffraction patterns, identifying and navigating toward high-symmetry orientations without prior knowledge of crystallography or diffraction theory. Experimental results show that the agent develops human-like strategies, achieving time-efficient alignment across various crystal symmetry classes, thereby providing a computational framework for intelligent diffractometers and advancing automated workflows in materials science.
本文针对自动化处理需要解释抽象视觉信息的任务（如晶体对准，传统上依赖人类解读衍射图案）的挑战，提出了一种自主系统，采用无模型强化学习框架。该方法使智能体能够直接从劳厄衍射图案中学习，识别并导航至高对称性取向，无需晶体学或衍射理论先验知识。实验结果表明，该智能体发展出类人策略，在不同晶体对称性类别中实现了时间高效的对准，从而为智能衍射仪提供了计算框架，并推动了材料科学中自动化工作流程的发展。
Discourse Diversity in Multi-Turn Empathic Dialogue
Authors: Hongli Zhan, Emma S. Gueorguieva, Javier Hernandez, Jina Suh, Desmond C. Ong, Junyi Jessy Li
First: 2026-04-13T17:17:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T17:17:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) produce responses rated as highly empathic in single-turn settings (Ayers et al., 2023; Lee et al., 2024), yet they are also known to be formulaic generators that reuse the same lexical patterns, syntactic templates, and discourse structures across tasks (Jiang et al., 2025; Shaib et al., 2024; Namuduri et al., 2025). Less attention has been paid to whether this formulaicity extends to the level of discourse moves, i.e., what a response does for the person it is addressing. This question is especially consequential for empathic dialogue, where effective support demands not just a kind response at one moment but varied strategies as a conversation unfolds (Stiles et al., 1998). Indeed, prior work shows that LLMs reuse the same tactic sequences more than human supporters in single-turn settings (Gueorguieva et al., 2026). We extend this analysis to multi-turn conversations and find that the rigidity compounds: once a tactic appears in a supporter turn, LLMs reuse it in the next at nearly double the rate of humans (0.50-0.56 vs. 0.27). This pattern holds across LLMs serving as supporters in real emotional support conversations, and is invisible to standard similarity metrics. To address this gap, we introduce MINT (Multi-turn Inter-tactic Novelty Training), the first reinforcement learning framework to optimize discourse move diversity across multi-turn empathic dialogue. The best MINT variant combines an empathy quality reward with a cross-turn tactic novelty signal, improving aggregate empathy by 25.3% over vanilla across 1.7B and 4B models while reducing cross-turn discourse move repetition by 26.3% on the 4B model, surpassing all baselines including quality-only and token-level diversity methods on both measures. These results suggest that what current models lack is not empathy itself, but the ability to vary their discourse moves across a conversation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：多轮共情对话中的话语多样性研究
大语言模型（LLMs）在单轮对话中能生成被评价为高度共情的回复（Ayers等人，2023；Lee等人，2024），但它们也被认为是模式化生成器，会在不同任务中重复使用相同的词汇模式、句法模板和话语结构（Jiang等人，2025；Shaib等人，2024；Namuduri等人，2025）。较少研究关注这种模式化是否会延伸到话语行为层面，即回复对接收者所起的具体作用。这一问题对共情对话尤为重要，因为有效的支持不仅需要单次善意回应，更需随对话进程灵活调整策略（Stiles等人，1998）。已有研究表明，在单轮场景中，LLMs比人类支持者更频繁地重复相同策略序列（Gueorguieva等人，2026）。我们将此分析扩展到多轮对话，发现其僵化性加剧：一旦某种策略出现在支持者回合中，LLMs在下一回合的重复使用率接近人类的两倍（0.50-0.56对比0.27）。该模式在真实情感支持对话的LLMs支持者中普遍存在，且标准相似性指标无法检测。为弥补这一缺陷，我们提出MINT（多轮策略间新颖性训练）——首个通过强化学习优化多轮共情对话话语行为多样性的框架。最优MINT变体结合共情质量奖励与跨回合策略新颖性信号，在17亿和40亿参数模型上将整体共情度较基线提升25.3%，同时在40亿模型上降低跨回合话语行为重复率26.3%，在两项指标上均超越仅优化质量或词元级多样性的基线方法。这些结果表明，当前模型缺乏的并非共情能力本身，而是在对话中灵活调整话语行为的能力。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the observation that large language models (LLMs) often produce formulaic responses even when rated as empathic in single-turn settings, this paper investigates whether such formulaicity extends to discourse moves—the strategic functions of responses—in multi-turn empathic dialogues. The method involves analyzing real emotional support conversations, revealing that LLMs reuse discourse tactics at nearly double the human rate across turns, a rigidity not captured by standard similarity metrics. To address this, the authors introduce MINT, a reinforcement learning framework that combines empathy quality rewards with a cross-turn tactic novelty signal. Experimental results show that MINT improves aggregate empathy by 25.3% over vanilla models and reduces cross-turn discourse move repetition by 26.3% in a 4B model, outperforming baselines and demonstrating that enhancing discourse diversity is key to more human-like empathic dialogue.
本文的动机源于大型语言模型（LLMs）在单轮对话中被评为高共情，但已知其回应存在公式化问题，而较少研究关注这种公式化是否延伸到话语行为层面——即回应对对话者的策略功能，这在多轮共情对话中尤为重要。研究方法包括分析真实情感支持对话，发现LLMs在跨轮次中重复使用话语策略的比率近乎人类的两倍，且这种僵化性未被标准相似性指标捕捉。为解决此问题，作者提出了MINT，一个结合共情质量奖励和跨轮次策略新颖性信号的强化学习框架。主要实验结果表明，MINT在1.7B和4B模型上将整体共情度提升了25.3%，并在4B模型上减少了26.3%的跨轮次话语行为重复，超越了所有基线方法，表明提升话语多样性是改善模型共情对话能力的关键。
Collaborative Multi-Agent Scripts Generation for Enhancing Imperfect-Information Reasoning in Murder Mystery Games
Authors: Keyang Zhong, Junlin Xie, Hefeng Wu, Haofeng Li, Guanbin Li
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-13T17:16:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T17:16:23+00:00
Comments: 9 pages, 5 figures, Findings of ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Vision-language models (VLMs) have shown impressive capabilities in perceptual tasks, yet they degrade in complex multi-hop reasoning under multiplayer game settings with imperfect and deceptive information. In this paper, we study a representative multiplayer task, Murder Mystery Games, which require inferring hidden truths based on partial clues provided by roles with different intentions. To address this challenge, we propose a collaborative multi-agent framework for evaluating and synthesizing high-quality, role-driven multiplayer game scripts, enabling fine-grained interaction patterns tailored to character identities (i.e., murderer vs. innocent). Our system generates rich multimodal contexts, including character backstories, visual and textual clues, and multi-hop reasoning chains, through coordinated agent interactions. We design a two-stage agent-monitored training strategy to enhance the reasoning ability of VLMs: (1) chain-of-thought based fine-tuning on curated and synthetic datasets that model uncertainty and deception; (2) GRPO-based reinforcement learning with agent-monitored reward shaping, encouraging the model to develop character-specific reasoning behaviors and effective multimodal multi-hop inference. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our method significantly boosts the performance of VLMs in narrative reasoning, hidden fact extraction, and deception-resilient understanding. Our contributions offer a scalable solution for training and evaluating VLMs under uncertain, adversarial, and socially complex conditions, laying the groundwork for future benchmarks in multimodal multi-hop reasoning under imperfect information.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向谋杀之谜游戏不完美信息推理增强的协作式多智能体剧本生成
视觉语言模型在感知任务中展现出卓越能力，但在多人游戏环境中面对不完美和欺骗性信息时，其复杂多跳推理能力会显著下降。本文以谋杀之谜游戏为典型多人任务场景，该游戏要求玩家基于不同意图角色提供的局部线索推断隐藏真相。为应对这一挑战，我们提出一种协作式多智能体框架，用于评估和生成高质量的角色驱动型多人游戏剧本，实现契合角色身份（凶手vs无辜者）的细粒度交互模式。该系统通过协调智能体交互，生成包含角色背景故事、视觉与文本线索及多跳推理链的丰富多模态语境。我们设计了两阶段智能体监督训练策略以增强视觉语言模型推理能力：（1）基于思维链的微调，使用建模不确定性与欺骗性的精选数据集与合成数据集；（2）采用GRPO强化学习与智能体监督奖励塑造，激励模型发展角色特异性推理行为及有效的多模态多跳推理。大量实验表明，本方法显著提升了视觉语言模型在叙事推理、隐藏事实提取和抗欺骗理解方面的性能。本工作为不确定、对抗性和社会复杂条件下的视觉语言模型训练评估提供了可扩展方案，为不完美信息下的多模态多跳推理基准建设奠定基础。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitation of vision-language models (VLMs) in complex multi-hop reasoning under imperfect and deceptive information, as exemplified by Murder Mystery Games where players must infer hidden truths from partial clues. To enhance VLM reasoning, the authors propose a collaborative multi-agent framework that generates high-quality, role-driven game scripts with multimodal contexts, including character backstories and clues, and introduce a two-stage training strategy involving chain-of-thought fine-tuning on curated datasets and GRPO-based reinforcement learning with agent-monitored reward shaping. Experimental results show that this method significantly improves VLM performance in narrative reasoning, hidden fact extraction, and deception-resilient understanding, offering a scalable solution for training VLMs in uncertain and adversarial conditions.
本文针对视觉语言模型（VLMs）在复杂多跳推理中处理不完美和欺骗性信息时的局限性展开研究，以谋杀之谜游戏为例，该游戏要求玩家根据角色提供的部分线索推断隐藏真相。为增强VLM的推理能力，作者提出一个协作多智能体框架，生成高质量、角色驱动的游戏脚本，包含角色背景和线索等多模态上下文，并设计了两阶段训练策略：基于思维链的微调和基于GRPO的强化学习，辅以智能体监控的奖励塑造。实验结果表明，该方法显著提升了VLM在叙事推理、隐藏事实提取和抗欺骗理解方面的性能，为在不确定和对抗性条件下训练VLM提供了可扩展的解决方案。
Playing Along: Learning a Double-Agent Defender for Belief Steering via Theory of Mind
Authors: Hanqi Xiao, Vaidehi Patil, Zaid Khan, Hyunji Lee, Elias Stengel-Eskin, Mohit Bansal
First: 2026-04-13T16:14:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T16:14:41+00:00
Comments: First two authors contributed equally. Code: https://github.com/The-Inscrutable-X/AIDoubleAgentDefenders
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
As large language models (LLMs) become the engine behind conversational systems, their ability to reason about the intentions and states of their dialogue partners (i.e., form and use a theory-of-mind, or ToM) becomes increasingly critical for safe interaction with potentially adversarial partners. We propose a novel privacy-themed ToM challenge, ToM for Steering Beliefs (ToM-SB), in which a defender must act as a Double Agent to steer the beliefs of an attacker with partial prior knowledge within a shared universe. To succeed on ToM-SB, the defender must engage with and form a ToM of the attacker, with a goal of fooling the attacker into believing they have succeeded in extracting sensitive information. We find that strong frontier models like Gemini3-Pro and GPT-5.4 struggle on ToM-SB, often failing to fool attackers in hard scenarios with partial attacker prior knowledge, even when prompted to reason about the attacker's beliefs (ToM prompting). To close this gap, we train models on ToM-SB to act as AI Double Agents using reinforcement learning, testing both fooling and ToM rewards. Notably, we find a bidirectionally emergent relationship between ToM and attacker-fooling: rewarding fooling success alone improves ToM, and rewarding ToM alone improves fooling. Across four attackers with different strengths, six defender methods, and both in-distribution and out-of-distribution (OOD) evaluation, we find that gains in ToM and attacker-fooling are well-correlated, highlighting belief modeling as a key driver of success on ToM-SB. AI Double Agents that combine both ToM and fooling rewards yield the strongest fooling and ToM performance, outperforming Gemini3-Pro and GPT-5.4 with ToM prompting on hard scenarios. We also show that ToM-SB and AI Double Agents can be extended to stronger attackers, demonstrating generalization to OOD settings and the upgradability of our task.
中文标题/摘要
标题：协同博弈：通过心智理论学习双面防御者以实现信念引导
随着大语言模型成为对话系统的核心引擎，其理解对话对象意图与状态的能力（即形成并运用心智理论）对于安全应对潜在对抗性交互至关重要。本研究提出一项以隐私保护为主题的心智理论挑战——信念引导心智理论，要求防御者扮演双面角色，在共享信息环境中引导具备部分先验知识的攻击者信念。为完成此任务，防御者需主动构建攻击者的心智模型，诱使对方误认为已成功获取敏感信息。实验发现，Gemini3-Pro与GPT-5.4等前沿模型在该任务中表现欠佳，尤其在攻击者具备部分先验知识的困难场景中，即使采用心智理论提示仍难以有效迷惑攻击者。为此，我们通过强化学习训练AI双面特工模型，同步测试迷惑效果与心智理论奖励。研究发现心智理论与攻击迷惑存在双向促进关系：仅奖励迷惑成功可提升心智理论能力，仅奖励心智理论亦可增强迷惑效果。通过对四种不同强度攻击者、六种防御方法及分布内外场景的评估，证实心智理论能力与攻击迷惑效果呈强相关性，凸显信念建模是任务成功的关键驱动力。融合心智理论与迷惑奖励的AI双面特工在困难场景中表现最优，其心智理论与迷惑性能均超越采用心智理论提示的Gemini3-Pro与GPT-5.4模型。研究还展示了该任务框架可扩展至更强攻击者，验证了其向分布外场景的泛化能力与任务可升级性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for safe interaction with potentially adversarial dialogue partners, this paper introduces a novel privacy-themed challenge, Theory of Mind for Steering Beliefs (ToM-SB), where a defender acts as a double agent to steer an attacker's beliefs about sensitive information. The method involves training AI double agents using reinforcement learning with rewards for both fooling the attacker and modeling the attacker's mental state (theory of mind). Experimental results show that frontier models like Gemini3-Pro and GPT-5.4 struggle on hard scenarios, while the trained agents, especially those combining both reward types, achieve stronger fooling and theory-of-mind performance, with gains correlating across in-distribution and out-of-distribution evaluations.
本文的动机是确保大型语言模型与潜在对抗性对话伙伴的安全交互，提出了一个新颖的隐私主题挑战——用于引导信念的心理理论（ToM-SB），其中防御者需扮演双面间谍来引导攻击者对敏感信息的信念。方法上，通过强化学习训练AI双面间谍，奖励其欺骗攻击者和建模攻击者心理状态（心理理论）的能力。实验结果表明，Gemini3-Pro和GPT-5.4等前沿模型在困难场景中表现不佳，而训练的智能体，尤其是结合两种奖励的智能体，在欺骗和心理理论性能上表现更强，其增益在分布内和分布外评估中均相关。
CROP: Conservative Reward for Model-based Offline Policy Optimization
Authors: Hao Li, Xiao-Hu Zhou, Shu-Hai Li, Mei-Jiang Gui, Xiao-Liang Xie, Shi-Qi Liu, Shuang-Yi Wang, Zhen-Qiu Feng, Zeng-Guang Hou
First: 2023-10-26T08:45:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T15:52:28+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Offline reinforcement learning (RL) aims to optimize a policy using collected data without online interactions. Model-based approaches are particularly appealing for addressing offline RL challenges because of their capability to mitigate the limitations of data coverage through data generation using models. Nonetheless, a prevalent issue in offline RL is the overestimation caused by distribution shift. This study proposes a novel model-based offline RL algorithm named Conservative Reward for model-based Offline Policy optimization (CROP). CROP introduces a streamlined objective that concurrently minimizes estimation error and the rewards of random actions, thereby yielding a robustly conservative reward estimator. Theoretical analysis shows that the designed conservative reward mechanism leads to a conservative policy evaluation and mitigates distribution shift. Experiments showcase that with the simple modification to reward estimation, CROP can conservatively estimate the reward and achieve competitive performance with existing methods. The source code will be available after acceptance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CROP：基于模型的离线策略优化的保守奖励机制
离线强化学习旨在仅利用收集的数据优化策略，无需在线交互。基于模型的方法因其能通过模型生成数据来缓解数据覆盖范围的限制，在应对离线强化学习挑战方面尤为吸引人。然而，离线强化学习中普遍存在由分布偏移引起的过高估计问题。本研究提出了一种名为CROP的新型基于模型离线强化学习算法，通过设计简洁的目标函数同时最小化估计误差和随机动作的奖励，从而构建出具有强保守性的奖励估计器。理论分析表明，该保守奖励机制可实现保守的策略评估并缓解分布偏移。实验证明，通过对奖励估计进行简单修改，CROP能够保守地估计奖励，并取得与现有方法相竞争的性能。源代码将在论文录用后公开。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of distribution shift and reward overestimation in offline reinforcement learning by proposing a model-based algorithm called CROP. The method introduces a conservative reward estimator that minimizes both estimation error and the rewards of random actions, theoretically ensuring conservative policy evaluation to mitigate distribution shift. Experimental results demonstrate that CROP achieves competitive performance with existing methods through this streamlined reward modification.
本文针对离线强化学习中的分布偏移和奖励高估问题，提出了一种基于模型的算法CROP。该方法通过设计一个保守的奖励估计器，同时最小化估计误差和随机动作的奖励，从理论上保证了保守的策略评估以缓解分布偏移。实验结果表明，CROP通过这种简化的奖励修改，实现了与现有方法相竞争的性能。
RationalRewards: Reasoning Rewards Scale Visual Generation Both Training and Test Time
Authors: Haozhe Wang, Cong Wei, Weiming Ren, Jiaming Liu, Fangzhen Lin, Wenhu Chen
First: 2026-04-13T15:38:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T15:38:09+00:00
Comments: Project Page: https://tiger-ai-lab.github.io/RationalRewards/ ; Code, Dataset, Models are released
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Most reward models for visual generation reduce rich human judgments to a single unexplained score, discarding the reasoning that underlies preference. We show that teaching reward models to produce explicit, multi-dimensional critiques before scoring transforms them from passive evaluators into active optimization tools, improving generators in two complementary ways: at training time, structured rationales provide interpretable, fine-grained rewards for reinforcement learning; at test time, a Generate-Critique-Refine loop turns critiques into targeted prompt revisions that improve outputs without any parameter updates. To train such a reward model without costly rationale annotations, we introduce Preference-Anchored Rationalization (PARROT), a principled framework that recovers high-quality rationales from readily available preference data through anchored generation, consistency filtering, and distillation. The resulting model, RationalRewards (8B), achieves state-of-the-art preference prediction among open-source reward models, competitive with Gemini-2.5-Pro, while using 10-20x less training data than comparable baselines. As an RL reward, it consistently improves text-to-image and image-editing generators beyond scalar alternatives. Most strikingly, its test-time critique-and-refine loop matches or exceeds RL-based fine-tuning on several benchmarks, suggesting that structured reasoning can unlock latent capabilities in existing generators that suboptimal prompts fail to elicit.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RationalRewards：推理奖励机制在训练与测试阶段均提升视觉生成效果
现有视觉生成奖励模型大多将丰富的人类评判简化为单一未解释分数，忽略了偏好背后的推理过程。本研究证明，通过训练奖励模型在评分前生成明确的多维度评析，可将其从被动评估工具转化为主动优化工具，从两个互补维度改进生成器：训练阶段，结构化推理为强化学习提供可解释的细粒度奖励；测试阶段，“生成-评析-优化”循环将评析转化为针对性提示词修订，无需参数更新即可提升输出质量。为免去昂贵的人工标注成本，我们提出偏好锚定推理框架（PARROT），通过锚定生成、一致性过滤与蒸馏技术，从现有偏好数据中提取高质量推理依据。最终模型RationalRewards（80亿参数）在开源奖励模型中实现最优偏好预测性能，媲美Gemini-2.5-Pro，且训练数据量仅为同类基线的5%-10%。作为强化学习奖励，该模型在文本到图像生成及图像编辑任务中持续优于传统标量奖励模型。最显著的是，其测试阶段的评析优化循环在多个基准测试中达到或超越基于强化学习的微调效果，表明结构化推理能激发现有生成器未被次优提示词调动的潜在能力。

Motivated by the limitation of conventional reward models that reduce human preferences to a single unexplained score, this paper introduces RationalRewards, a method that trains reward models to produce explicit, multi-dimensional critiques before scoring. The approach, enabled by the Preference-Anchored Rationalization (PARROT) framework which recovers high-quality rationales from preference data without costly annotations, improves visual generation both during training—by providing fine-grained rewards for reinforcement learning—and at test time—through a Generate-Critique-Refine loop that refines prompts without parameter updates. Experimental results show that the resulting 8B model achieves state-of-the-art preference prediction with significantly less training data, enhances text-to-image and image-editing generators as an RL reward, and its test-time critique loop matches or exceeds RL fine-tuning on several benchmarks, demonstrating that structured reasoning unlocks latent capabilities in existing generators.

Learning to Focus: CSI-Free Hierarchical MARL for Reconfigurable Reflectors
Authors: Hieu Le, Mostafa Ibrahim, Oguz Bedir, Jian Tao, Sabit Ekin
First: 2026-04-06T20:50:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T15:27:38+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reconfigurable Intelligent Surfaces (RIS) has a potential to engineer smart radio environments for next-generation millimeter-wave (mmWave) networks. However, the prohibitive computational overhead of Channel State Information (CSI) estimation and the dimensionality explosion inherent in centralized optimization severely hinder practical large-scale deployments. To overcome these bottlenecks, we introduce a ``CSI-free" paradigm powered by a Hierarchical Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (HMARL) architecture to control mechanically reconfigurable reflective surfaces. By substituting pilot-based channel estimation with accessible user localization data, our framework leverages spatial intelligence for macro-scale wave propagation management. The control problem is decomposed into a two-tier neural architecture: a high-level controller executes temporally extended, discrete user-to-reflector allocations, while low-level controllers autonomously optimize continuous focal points utilizing Multi-Agent Proximal Policy Optimization (MAPPO) under a Centralized Training with Decentralized Execution (CTDE) scheme. Comprehensive deterministic ray-tracing evaluations demonstrate that this hierarchical framework achieves massive RSSI improvements of up to 7.79 dB over centralized baselines. Furthermore, the system exhibits robust multi-user scalability and maintains highly resilient beam-focusing performance under practical sub-meter localization tracking errors. By eliminating CSI overhead while maintaining high-fidelity signal redirection, this work establishes a scalable and cost-effective blueprint for intelligent wireless environments.

标题：学会聚焦：基于无信道状态信息的层次化多智能体强化学习控制可重构反射面
可重构智能表面（RIS）具备为下一代毫米波网络构建智能无线电环境的潜力。然而，信道状态信息（CSI）估计的过高计算开销以及集中式优化固有的维度爆炸问题，严重阻碍了实际大规模部署。为突破这些瓶颈，我们提出一种由层次化多智能体强化学习（HMARL）架构驱动的“无CSI”范式，用于控制机械可重构反射面。该框架通过用可获取的用户定位数据替代基于导频的信道估计，利用空间智能实现宏观尺度波传播管理。控制问题被分解为双层神经架构：高层控制器执行时间扩展的离散用户-反射面分配，而低层控制器在集中训练分散执行（CTDE）方案下，利用多智能体近端策略优化（MAPPO）自主优化连续焦点。基于确定性射线追踪的综合评估表明，该层次化框架相比集中式基线实现了高达7.79 dB的大规模接收信号强度指数提升。此外，系统展现出稳健的多用户扩展性，并在实际亚米级定位跟踪误差下保持高度韧性的波束聚焦性能。通过消除CSI开销同时维持高保真信号重定向，本研究为智能无线环境提供了可扩展且经济高效的蓝图。

Utilizing and Calibrating Hindsight Process Rewards via Reinforcement with Mutual Information Self-Evaluation
Authors: Jiashu Yao, Heyan Huang, Zeming Liu, Yuhang Guo
First: 2026-04-13T15:18:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T15:18:51+00:00
Comments: preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
To overcome the sparse reward challenge in reinforcement learning (RL) for agents based on large language models (LLMs), we propose Mutual Information Self-Evaluation (MISE), an RL paradigm that utilizes hindsight generative self-evaluation as dense reward signals while simultaneously calibrating them against the environmental feedbacks. Empirically, MISE enables an agent to learn autonomously from dense internal rewards supplementing sparse extrinsic signals. Theoretically, our work provides the first formal foundation for the paradigm of generative self-rewarding. We prove that utilizing hindsight self-evaluation rewards is equivalent to minimizing an objective that combines mutual information with a KL divergence term between the policy and a proxy reward policy. This theoretical insight then informs and justifies our calibration step, which actively aligns these rewards with the optimal policy. Extensive experiments show that MISE outperforms strong baselines, enabling open-source LLMs about 7B parameters to achieve performance comparable to GPT-4o on validation without expert supervision.

SEARL: Joint Optimization of Policy and Tool Graph Memory for Self-Evolving Agents
Authors: Xinshun Feng, Xinhao Song, Lijun Li, Gongshen Liu, Jing Shao
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-09T04:38:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T14:41:20+00:00
Comments: ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advances in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) have demonstrated significant potential in single-turn reasoning tasks. With the paradigm shift toward self-evolving agentic learning, models are increasingly expected to learn from trajectories by synthesizing tools or accumulating explicit experiences. However, prevailing methods typically rely on large-scale LLMs or multi-agent frameworks, which hinder their deployment in resource-constrained environments. The inherent sparsity of outcome-based rewards also poses a substantial challenge, as agents typically receive feedback only upon completion of tasks. To address these limitations, we introduce a Tool-Memory based self-evolving agentic framework SEARL. Unlike approaches that directly utilize interaction experiences, our method constructs a structured experience memory that integrates planning with execution. This provides a novel state abstraction that facilitates generalization across analogous contexts, such as tool reuse. Consequently, agents extract explicit knowledge from historical data while leveraging inter-trajectory correlations to densify reward signals. We evaluate our framework on knowledge reasoning and mathematics tasks, demonstrating its effectiveness in achieving more practical and efficient learning.

The method constructs a memory integrating planning and execution to provide state abstraction, enabling generalization across similar contexts and densifying reward signals by leveraging inter-trajectory correlations. Experimental results on knowledge reasoning and mathematics tasks demonstrate that SEARL achieves more practical and efficient learning compared to methods relying on large LLMs or multi-agent systems.

Eliciting Medical Reasoning with Knowledge-enhanced Data Synthesis: A Semi-Supervised Reinforcement Learning Approach
Authors: Haolin Li, Shuyang Jiang, Ruipeng Zhang, Jiangchao Yao, Ya Zhang, Yanfeng Wang
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-13T14:37:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T14:37:38+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ACL 2026 as a Findings paper
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
While large language models hold promise for complex medical applications, their development is hindered by the scarcity of high-quality reasoning data. To address this issue, existing approaches typically distill chain-of-thought reasoning traces from large proprietary models via supervised fine-tuning, then conduct reinforcement learning (RL). These methods exhibit limited improvement on underrepresented domains like rare diseases while incurring substantial costs from generating complex reasoning chains. To efficiently enhance medical reasoning, we propose MedSSR, a Medical Knowledge-enhanced data Synthesis and Semi-supervised Reinforcement learning framework. Our framework first employs rare disease knowledge to synthesize distribution-controllable reasoning questions. We then utilize the policy model itself to generate high-quality pseudo-labels. This enables a two-stage, intrinsic-to-extrinsic training paradigm: self-supervised RL on the pseudo-labeled synthetic data, followed by supervised RL on the human-annotated real data. MedSSR scales model training efficiently without relying on costly trace distillation. Extensive experiments on Qwen and Llama demonstrate that our method outperforms existing methods across ten medical benchmarks, achieving up to +5.93% gain on rare-disease tasks. Our code is available at https://github.com/tdlhl/MedSSR.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于知识增强数据合成的医学推理激发：一种半监督强化学习方法
尽管大语言模型在复杂医学应用中展现出潜力，但其发展受限于高质量推理数据的稀缺性。现有方法通常通过监督微调从大型专有模型中提取思维链推理轨迹，再进行强化学习。这些方法在罕见病等低资源领域改进有限，且生成复杂推理链的成本高昂。为高效提升医学推理能力，我们提出MedSSR——一种融合医学知识增强的数据合成与半监督强化学习框架。该框架首先利用罕见病知识合成分布可控的推理问题，随后通过策略模型自身生成高质量伪标签，形成由内而外的两阶段训练范式：先在伪标注合成数据上进行自监督强化学习，再在人工标注真实数据上进行监督强化学习。MedSSR无需依赖高成本的轨迹蒸馏即可高效扩展模型训练。基于Qwen和Llama的广泛实验表明，本方法在十项医学基准测试中均优于现有方法，在罕见病任务上最高提升5.93%。代码已开源：https://github.com/tdlhl/MedSSR。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to overcome the scarcity of high-quality reasoning data, which hinders the development of large language models for complex medical applications, especially in underrepresented domains like rare diseases. The proposed method, MedSSR, is a framework that first synthesizes distribution-controllable reasoning questions using rare disease knowledge and then employs the policy model itself to generate high-quality pseudo-labels for a two-stage training paradigm: self-supervised reinforcement learning on the synthetic data, followed by supervised reinforcement learning on human-annotated real data. Policy Split: Incentivizing Dual-Mode Exploration in LLM Reinforcement with Dual-Mode Entropy Regularization
Authors: Jiashu Yao, Heyan Huang, Chuwei Luo, Daiqing Wu, Zeming Liu, Yuhang Guo, Yangyang Kang
First: 2026-04-13T14:13:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T14:13:06+00:00
Comments: preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
To encourage diverse exploration in reinforcement learning (RL) for large language models (LLMs) without compromising accuracy, we propose Policy Split, a novel paradigm that bifurcates the policy into normal and high-entropy modes with a high-entropy prompt. While sharing model parameters, the two modes undergo collaborative dual-mode entropy regularization tailored to distinct objectives. Specifically, the normal mode optimizes for task correctness, while the high-entropy mode incorporates a preference for exploration, and the two modes learn collaboratively. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our approach consistently outperforms established entropy-guided RL baselines across various model sizes in general and creative tasks. Further analysis reveals that Policy Split facilitates dual-mode exploration, where the high-entropy mode generates distinct behavioral patterns to the normal mode, providing unique learning signals.
中文标题/摘要
标题：策略分裂：通过双模熵正则化激励大语言模型强化学习中的双模探索
为在大语言模型强化学习中鼓励多样化探索同时保持准确性，我们提出'策略分裂'这一新范式，通过高熵提示将策略分为常规模式与高熵模式。两种模式共享模型参数，但针对不同目标进行协作式双模熵正则化：常规模式优化任务正确性，高熵模式侧重探索偏好，二者协同学习。大量实验表明，该方法在通用与创造性任务中持续超越现有熵引导强化学习基线，且适用于不同规模模型。进一步分析揭示，策略分裂促进双模探索——高熵模式产生与常规模式相异的行为模式，提供独特的学习信号。
Summary / 总结
This paper introduces Policy Split, a reinforcement learning method designed to enhance exploration in large language models without sacrificing task accuracy. The approach splits the policy into two modes—normal and high-entropy—that share model parameters but are guided by distinct objectives through dual-mode entropy regularization: the normal mode focuses on task correctness, while the high-entropy mode prioritizes exploration, enabling collaborative learning. Experimental results show that Policy Split consistently outperforms existing entropy-guided RL baselines across various model sizes in both general and creative tasks, with analysis indicating that the high-entropy mode generates unique behavioral patterns that provide novel learning signals.
本文提出了Policy Split方法，旨在增强大语言模型在强化学习中的探索性而不损害任务准确性。该方法将策略分为正常模式和高熵模式，两者共享模型参数但通过双模熵正则化实现不同目标：正常模式优化任务正确性，高熵模式则偏好探索，并协同学习。实验结果表明，Policy Split在多种模型规模下，于通用和创造性任务中均优于现有的熵引导强化学习基线；进一步分析显示，高熵模式能产生与正常模式不同的行为模式，提供独特的学习信号。
Deep Learning for Sequential Decision Making under Uncertainty: Foundations, Frameworks, and Frontiers
Authors: I. Esra Buyuktahtakin
First: 2026-04-13T14:11:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T14:11:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Artificial intelligence (AI) is moving increasingly beyond prediction to support decisions in complex, uncertain, and dynamic environments. This shift creates a natural intersection with operations research and management sciences (OR/MS), which have long offered conceptual and methodological foundations for sequential decision-making under uncertainty. At the same time, recent advances in deep learning, including feedforward neural networks, LSTMs, transformers, and deep reinforcement learning, have expanded the scope of data-driven modeling and opened new possibilities for large-scale decision systems. This tutorial presents an OR/MS-centered perspective on deep learning for sequential decision-making under uncertainty. Its central premise is that deep learning is valuable not as a replacement for optimization, but as a complement to it. Deep learning brings adaptability and scalable approximation, whereas OR/MS provides the structural rigor needed to represent constraints, recourse, and uncertainty. The tutorial reviews key decision-making foundations, connects them to the major neural architectures in modern AI, and discusses leading approaches to integrating learning and optimization. It also highlights emerging impact in domains such as supply chains, healthcare and epidemic response, agriculture, energy, and autonomous operations. More broadly, it frames these developments as part of a wider transition from predictive AI toward decision-capable AI and highlights the role of OR/MS in shaping the next generation of integrated learning--optimization systems.

本文的动机源于人工智能系统在不确定、动态环境中进行序列决策的日益增长的需求，旨在桥接运筹学/管理科学（OR/MS）与深度学习。其方法主张深度学习应作为优化的补充而非替代，提供适应性和可扩展的近似能力，而OR/MS则为处理约束和不确定性提供结构严谨性。具体方法包括回顾决策制定的基础概念，将其与LSTM、Transformer等神经架构联系起来，并讨论学习与优化的集成方法。实验结果表明，这些框架在供应链、医疗保健、能源和自主运营等领域展现出新兴影响力，标志着从预测性AI向决策型AI的广泛转变。
SHE: Stepwise Hybrid Examination Reinforcement Learning Framework for E-commerce Search Relevance
Authors: Pengkun Jiao, Yiming Jin, Jianhui Yang, Chenhe Dong, Zerui Huang, Shaowei Yao, Xiaojiang Zhou, Dan Ou, Haihong Tang
First: 2025-10-09T09:03:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T14:08:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Query-product relevance prediction is vital for AI-driven e-commerce, yet current LLM-based approaches face a dilemma: SFT and DPO struggle with long-tail generalization due to coarse supervision, while traditional RLVR suffers from sparse feedback that fails to correct intermediate reasoning errors. We propose Stepwise Hybrid Examination (SHE), an RL framework that ensures logical consistency through Stepwise Reward Policy Optimization (SRPO). SRPO utilizes a hybrid reward mechanism-combining generative reward models with human-annotated verifiers-to provide fine-grained, step-level signals. To further enhance stability, SHE incorporates diversified data filtering to maintain policy entropy and a multi-stage curriculum learning protocol for progressive skill acquisition. Extensive experiments on real-world search benchmarks show that SHE improves both reasoning quality and relevance-prediction accuracy in large-scale e-commerce settings, outperforming SFT, DPO, GRPO, and other baselines, while also enhancing interpretability and robustness.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SHE：面向电商搜索相关性的逐步混合检验强化学习框架
查询-商品相关性预测对AI驱动的电商至关重要，但当前基于大语言模型的方法面临两难：监督微调与直接偏好优化因粗粒度监督而难以泛化至长尾数据，传统强化学习验证则受限于稀疏反馈，无法纠正中间推理错误。本文提出逐步混合检验框架，通过逐步奖励策略优化确保逻辑一致性。该优化采用混合奖励机制——结合生成式奖励模型与人工标注验证器——以提供细粒度的步骤级信号。为提升稳定性，框架引入多样化数据过滤以保持策略熵，并采用多阶段课程学习协议实现渐进式技能习得。在真实搜索基准上的大量实验表明，该框架在大规模电商场景中同时提升了推理质量与相关性预测准确率，优于监督微调、直接偏好优化、生成式奖励策略优化等基线方法，并增强了可解释性与鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of existing LLM-based methods for e-commerce search relevance, where supervised fine-tuning and direct preference optimization lack long-tail generalization and traditional RL from human feedback provides overly sparse signals, this paper introduces the Stepwise Hybrid Examination (SHE) reinforcement learning framework. The method, Stepwise Reward Policy Optimization (SRPO), employs a hybrid reward mechanism that combines generative reward models with human-annotated verifiers to deliver fine-grained, step-level feedback, ensuring logical consistency; it is further stabilized through diversified data filtering to maintain policy entropy and a multi-stage curriculum learning protocol. Experimental results on real-world search benchmarks demonstrate that SHE significantly enhances reasoning quality and relevance-prediction accuracy, outperforming strong baselines like SFT, DPO, and GRPO, while also improving model interpretability and robustness in large-scale e-commerce settings.

CAGenMol: Condition-Aware Diffusion Language Model for Goal-Directed Molecular Generation
Authors: Yanting Li, Zhuoyang Jiang, Enyan Dai, Lei Wang, Wen-Cai Ye, Li Liu
First: 2026-04-13T13:49:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T13:49:23+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Goal-directed molecular generation requires satisfying heterogeneous constraints such as protein--ligand compatibility and multi-objective drug-like properties, yet existing methods often optimize these constraints in isolation, failing to reconcile conflicting objectives (e.g., affinity vs. safety), and struggle to navigate the non-differentiable chemical space without compromising structural validity. To address these challenges, we propose CAGenMol, a condition-aware discrete diffusion framework over molecular sequences that formulates molecular design as conditional denoising guided by heterogeneous structural and property signals. By coupling discrete diffusion with reinforcement learning, the model aligns the generation trajectory with non-differentiable objectives while preserving chemical validity and diversity. The non-autoregressive nature of diffusion language model further enables iterative refinement of molecular fragments at inference time. Experiments on structure-conditioned, property-conditioned, and dual-conditioned benchmarks demonstrate consistent improvements over state-of-the-art methods in binding affinity, drug-likeness, and success rate, highlighting the effectiveness of our framework.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CAGenMol：面向目标导向分子生成的条件感知扩散语言模型
目标导向分子生成需满足蛋白质-配体兼容性与多目标类药性等异质约束，但现有方法常孤立优化这些约束，难以协调冲突目标（如亲和力与安全性），且在保持结构有效性的同时难以探索不可微化学空间。为解决这些问题，我们提出CAGenMol——一种基于分子序列的条件感知离散扩散框架，将分子设计构建为异质结构与性质信号引导的条件去噪过程。通过离散扩散与强化学习的耦合，该模型在保持化学有效性与多样性的同时，使生成轨迹与不可微目标对齐。扩散语言模型的非自回归特性进一步支持在推理阶段对分子片段进行迭代优化。在结构条件、性质条件及双条件基准测试中，实验显示本框架在结合亲和力、类药性与成功率上均优于现有先进方法，凸显了其有效性。

OOM-RL: Out-of-Money Reinforcement Learning Market-Driven Alignment for LLM-Based Multi-Agent Systems
Authors: Kun Liu, Liqun Chen
First: 2026-04-13T13:45:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T13:45:42+00:00
Comments: 13 pages, 3 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The alignment of Multi-Agent Systems (MAS) for autonomous software engineering is constrained by evaluator epistemic uncertainty. Current paradigms, such as Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) and AI Feedback (RLAIF), frequently induce model sycophancy, while execution-based environments suffer from adversarial "Test Evasion" by unconstrained agents. In this paper, we introduce an objective alignment paradigm: \textbf{Out-of-Money Reinforcement Learning (OOM-RL)}. By deploying agents into the non-stationary, high-friction reality of live financial markets, we utilize critical capital depletion as an un-hackable negative gradient. Our longitudinal 20-month empirical study (July 2024 -- February 2026) chronicles the system's evolution from a high-turnover, sycophantic baseline to a robust, liquidity-aware architecture. We demonstrate that the undeniable ontological consequences of financial loss forced the MAS to abandon overfitted hallucinations in favor of the \textbf{Strict Test-Driven Agentic Workflow (STDAW)}, which enforces a Byzantine-inspired uni-directional state lock (RO-Lock) anchored to a deterministically verified $\geq 95\%$ code coverage constraint matrix. Our results show that while early iterations suffered severe execution decay, the final OOM-RL-aligned system achieved a stable equilibrium with an annualized Sharpe ratio of 2.06 in its mature phase. We conclude that substituting subjective human preference with rigorous economic penalties provides a robust methodology for aligning autonomous agents in high-stakes, real-world environments, laying the groundwork for generalized paradigms where computational billing acts as an objective physical constraint
中文标题/摘要
标题：OOM-RL：基于大语言模型的多智能体系统市场驱动对齐——资金耗尽强化学习
自主软件工程中多智能体系统的对齐受限于评估者的认知不确定性。当前范式如基于人类反馈的强化学习与基于AI反馈的强化学习常引发模型谄媚行为，而基于执行的环境则面临无约束智能体的对抗性'测试规避'问题。本文提出一种客观对齐范式：\textbf{资金耗尽强化学习}。通过将智能体部署至非稳态、高摩擦的真实金融市场，我们利用关键资本耗尽作为不可篡改的负向梯度。为期20个月的纵向实证研究记录了系统从高周转率、谄媚基线演变为稳健、具备流动性感知架构的过程。研究表明，财务损失的客观本体论后果迫使多智能体系统放弃过拟合幻觉，转向\textbf{严格测试驱动的智能体工作流}——该流程采用受拜占庭启发的单向状态锁，锚定于确定性验证的$\geq 95\%$代码覆盖率约束矩阵。结果显示，早期迭代虽遭遇严重执行衰减，但最终经OOM-RL对齐的系统在成熟阶段实现了年化夏普比率2.06的稳定均衡。结论表明：以严格经济惩罚替代主观人类偏好，为高风险现实环境中自主智能体的对齐提供了稳健方法论，为计算计费作为客观物理约束的泛化范式奠定基础。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of aligning Multi-Agent Systems (MAS) for autonomous software engineering, where existing methods like RLHF and RLAIF often lead to model sycophancy or test evasion. The authors propose Out-of-Money Reinforcement Learning (OOM-RL), a novel paradigm that aligns agents by deploying them in live financial markets, using capital depletion as an objective, unhackable penalty signal. Over a 20-month longitudinal study, the system evolved from a sycophantic baseline to adopt a Strict Test-Driven Agentic Workflow (STDAW) with high code coverage, ultimately achieving a stable equilibrium with an annualized Sharpe ratio of 2.06, demonstrating that economic penalties can effectively align agents in high-stakes environments.
本文针对自主软件工程中多智能体系统对齐的挑战，现有方法如RLHF和RLAIF常导致模型谄媚或测试规避。作者提出了资金耗尽强化学习（OOM-RL）这一新范式，通过将智能体部署到实时金融市场中，利用资本耗尽作为客观、不可篡改的惩罚信号来实现对齐。一项为期20个月的纵向研究表明，系统从谄媚基线演变为采用具有高代码覆盖率的严格测试驱动智能体工作流（STDAW），最终达到稳定状态，年化夏普比率为2.06，证明经济惩罚能有效对齐高风险环境中的智能体。
Three Roles, One Model: Role Orchestration at Inference Time to Close the Performance Gap Between Small and Large Agents
Authors: S. Aaron McClendon, Jorge Gallego-Feliciano, Stavros Zervoudakis, Antonios Saravanos
First: 2026-04-13T13:40:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T13:40:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language model (LLM) agents show promise on realistic tool-use tasks, but deploying capable agents on modest hardware remains challenging. We study whether inference-time scaffolding alone, without any additional training compute, can improve the performance of a small model in complex multi-step environments. Operating on a single 24\,GB GPU, we evaluate Qwen3-8B under both full-precision (FP16, 12K context) and 4-bit quantized (AWQ, 32K context) configurations. Without any intervention, the raw model achieves just 5.4\% (FP16) and 3.0\% (AWQ) task goal completion. Guided by a systematic failure mode analysis, we introduce a three-tier inference scaffolding pipeline that deploys the same frozen model in three distinct roles: (1) a summarization model that preserves critical artifacts (tokens, credentials, API responses) while compressing dialogue history; (2) the main agent model that reasons over the compressed context; and (3) an isolated correction model that reviews and revises the agent's code output without access to conversation history, breaking repetitive failure loops. Applied to the same unmodified model, this scaffolding yields 8.9\% (FP16) and 5.9\% (AWQ) task goal completion, roughly doubling performance in both settings, with particularly strong gains on difficulty-1 tasks (15.8\%$\to$26.3\% FP16; 5.3\%$\to$14.0\% AWQ). On full-precision inference, our scaffolded 8B model surpasses DeepSeek-Coder 33B Instruct (7.1\%) from the original AppWorld evaluation, demonstrating that structured inference-time interventions can make small models competitive with systems 4$\times$ their size. We formalize the approach as a scaffolded policy over a frozen base model, three invocations of the same weights with different conditioning, drawing connections to test-time compute scaling and action-space shaping in reinforcement learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：三重角色，单一模型：通过推理时角色编排缩小大小智能体间的性能差距
大语言模型智能体在现实工具使用任务中展现出潜力，但在有限硬件上部署高性能智能体仍具挑战。本研究探讨仅通过推理时架构支持（无需额外训练算力）能否提升小模型在复杂多步环境中的性能。我们在单张24GB GPU上评估Qwen3-8B模型的全精度（FP16，12K上下文）和4位量化（AWQ，32K上下文）配置。未经干预时，原始模型的任务目标完成率仅为5.4%（FP16）和3.0%（AWQ）。基于系统性故障模式分析，我们引入三层推理架构流水线，将同一冻结模型部署于三个独立角色：（1）摘要模型——在压缩对话历史时保留关键信息（令牌、凭证、API响应）；（2）主智能体模型——在压缩上下文中进行推理；（3）独立校正模型——在不访问对话历史的情况下审查并修正智能体的代码输出，打破重复故障循环。应用此架构后，同一未修改模型的任务完成率提升至8.9%（FP16）和5.9%（AWQ），在两种设置下均实现约两倍性能提升，尤其在难度1任务上增益显著（FP16：15.8%→26.3%；AWQ：5.3%→14.0%）。在全精度推理中，我们采用架构的8B模型超越了原始AppWorld评估中的DeepSeek-Coder 33B Instruct（7.1%），证明结构化推理时干预能使小模型与4倍体量系统竞争。我们将该方法形式化为冻结基础模型上的架构策略——通过三种不同条件调用同一权重，并与强化学习中的测试时计算扩展和动作空间塑造建立理论关联。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of deploying capable language model agents on modest hardware by investigating whether inference-time scaffolding alone can improve the performance of a small model in complex multi-step tool-use tasks, without any additional training. The method introduces a three-tier inference pipeline that orchestrates the same frozen 8B parameter model into three distinct roles: a summarization model to compress dialogue history, a main agent model for reasoning, and an isolated correction model to review and revise code outputs, thereby breaking repetitive failure loops. Experimental results on a 24GB GPU show that this scaffolding roughly doubles the task goal completion rate for both full-precision and quantized configurations, with the scaffolded 8B model even surpassing a 33B model from a prior evaluation, demonstrating that structured inference-time interventions can make small models competitive with much larger systems.
本文针对在有限硬件上部署高效能语言模型智能体的挑战，研究仅通过推理时架构支持，而无需额外训练计算，能否提升小模型在复杂多步骤工具使用任务中的性能。方法引入了一个三层推理流程，将同一个冻结的80亿参数模型编排为三个不同角色：用于压缩对话历史的摘要模型、进行推理的主智能体模型，以及独立审查和修正代码输出的校正模型，从而打破重复失败循环。在单张24GB GPU上的实验结果表明，该架构支持使全精度和量化配置下的任务目标完成率均提升约一倍，且经过架构支持的80亿参数模型甚至超越了先前评估中的330亿参数模型，证明结构化的推理时干预能使小模型与规模大得多的系统相竞争。
Escaping the Context Bottleneck: Active Context Curation for LLM Agents via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Xiaozhe Li, Tianyi Lyu, Yizhao Yang, Liang Shan, Siyi Yang, Ligao Zhang, Zhuoyi Huang, Qingwen Liu, Yang Li
First: 2026-04-13T13:39:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T13:39:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) struggle with long-horizon tasks due to the "context bottleneck" and the "lost-in-the-middle" phenomenon, where accumulated noise from verbose environments degrades reasoning over multi-turn interactions. To address this issue, we introduce a symbiotic framework that decouples context management from task execution. Our architecture pairs a lightweight, specialized policy model, ContextCurator, with a powerful frozen foundation model, TaskExecutor. Trained via reinforcement learning, ContextCurator actively reduces information entropy in the working memory. It aggressively prunes environmental noise while preserving reasoning anchors, that is, sparse data points that are critical for future deductions. On WebArena, our framework improves the success rate of Gemini-3.0-flash from 36.4% to 41.2% while reducing token consumption by 8.8% (from 47.4K to 43.3K). On DeepSearch, it achieves a 57.1% success rate, compared with 53.9%, while reducing token consumption by a factor of 8. Remarkably, a 7B ContextCurator matches the context management performance of GPT-4o, providing a scalable and computationally efficient paradigm for autonomous long-horizon agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：突破上下文瓶颈：基于强化学习的LLM智能体主动上下文管理
大语言模型（LLMs）在处理长程任务时面临“上下文瓶颈”和“中间迷失”现象，即冗杂环境中累积的噪声会损害多轮交互中的推理能力。为解决这一问题，我们提出一种解耦上下文管理与任务执行的协同框架。该架构将轻量级专用策略模型ContextCurator与强大的冻结基础模型TaskExecutor配对。通过强化学习训练的ContextCurator主动降低工作记忆中的信息熵，在保留推理锚点（即对未来决策至关重要的稀疏数据点）的同时，大幅削减环境噪声。在WebArena测试中，本框架将Gemini-3.0-flash的成功率从36.4%提升至41.2%，同时降低8.8%的token消耗（从47.4K降至43.3K）。在DeepSearch测试中，成功率从53.9%提升至57.1%，且token消耗减少为原来的1/8。值得注意的是，仅70亿参数的ContextCurator即可达到GPT-4o的上下文管理性能，为自主长程智能体提供了可扩展且计算高效的范式。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the 'context bottleneck' and 'lost-in-the-middle' problem in LLMs, where performance degrades on long-horizon tasks due to accumulated environmental noise. The proposed solution is a symbiotic framework that decouples context management from task execution, pairing a lightweight, RL-trained ContextCurator policy with a frozen foundation TaskExecutor model to actively prune noise and preserve critical reasoning anchors. Low-rank Optimization Trajectories Modeling for LLM RLVR Acceleration
Authors: Zhipeng Chen, Tao Qian, Wayne Xin Zhao, Ji-Rong Wen
First: 2026-04-13T13:28:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T13:28:12+00:00
Comments: Working in progress
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Recently, scaling reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) for large language models (LLMs) has emerged as an effective training paradigm for significantly improving model capabilities, which requires guiding the model to perform extensive exploration and learning, leading to substantial computational overhead and becoming a key challenge. To reduce the number of training steps, Prior work performs linear extrapolation of model parameters. However, the dynamics of model parameter updates during RLVR training remain insufficiently understood. To further investigate the evolution of LLMs during RLVR training, we conduct empirical experiments and find that the rank-1 subspace of the model does not evolve linearly, and its dominance over the original parameters is further amplified during LoRA training. Based on the above insights, we propose the \textbf{N}onlinear \textbf{Ext}rapolation of low-rank trajectories (\textbf{NExt}), a novel framework that models and extrapolates low-rank parameter trajectories in a nonlinear manner. Concretely, we first train the model using LoRA and extract the rank-1 subspace of parameter differences at multiple training steps, which is then used for the subsequent nonlinear extrapolation. Afterward, we utilized the extracted rank-1 subspace to train a predictor, which can model the trajectory of parameter updates during RLVR, and then perform the predict-extend process to extrapolate model parameters, achieving the acceleration of RLVR. To further study and understand NExt, we conduct comprehensive experiments that demonstrate the effectiveness and robustness of the method. Our method reduces computational overhead by approximately 37.5\% while remaining compatible with a wide range of RLVR algorithms and tasks. We release our code in https://github.com/RUCAIBox/NExt.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向大语言模型RLVR加速的低秩优化轨迹建模
近期，基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）在大语言模型（LLMs）规模化训练中已成为显著提升模型能力的有效范式，但该过程需引导模型进行大量探索学习，导致巨大计算开销，成为关键挑战。为减少训练步数，现有研究采用模型参数的线性外推方法，然而RLVR训练中参数更新的动态机制尚未被充分理解。为深入探究LLMs在RLVR训练中的演化规律，我们通过实证实验发现：模型的秩-1子空间演化呈非线性特征，且在LoRA训练中其对原始参数的主导作用会进一步放大。基于此洞见，我们提出低秩轨迹非线性外推框架NExt，通过非线性方式建模并外推低秩参数轨迹。具体而言，我们首先使用LoRA训练模型，并在多个训练步骤中提取参数差异的秩-1子空间，随后进行非线性外推。利用提取的秩-1子空间训练预测器，该预测器可建模RLVR过程中的参数更新轨迹，通过“预测-扩展”流程实现模型参数外推，从而加速RLVR训练。为深入验证NExt框架，我们开展了系统性实验，结果表明该方法具备显著的有效性与鲁棒性。本方法在保持与多种RLVR算法及任务广泛兼容的同时，可降低约37.5%的计算开销。代码已开源：https://github.com/RUCAIBox/NExt。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the substantial computational overhead of reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) for large language models by reducing the number of required training steps, as prior linear extrapolation methods are insufficient due to the nonlinear evolution of model parameters. The proposed method, NExt, models low-rank parameter trajectories nonlinearly by first training with LoRA to extract the rank-1 subspace of parameter differences across steps, then training a predictor to extrapolate future parameters, thereby accelerating RLVR. Experimental results show that NExt reduces computational overhead by approximately 37.5% while maintaining compatibility with various RLVR algorithms and tasks, demonstrating both effectiveness and robustness.

RL makes MLLMs see better than SFT
Authors: Junha Song, Sangdoo Yun, Dongyoon Han, Jaegul Choo, Byeongho Heo
First: 2025-10-18T03:37:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T11:22:40+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
A dominant assumption in Multimodal Language Model (MLLM) research is that its performance is largely inherited from the LLM backbone, given its immense parameter scale and remarkable capabilities. This has created a void in the understanding of the vision encoder, which determines how MLLMs perceive images. The recent shift in MLLM training paradigms, from Supervised Finetuning (SFT) to Reinforcement Learning (RL), magnifies this oversight-namely, the significant lack of analysis on how such training reshapes the vision encoder as well as the MLLM. To address this, we first investigate the impact of training strategies on MLLMs, where RL shows a clear advantage over SFT in strongly vision-related VQA benchmarks. Motivated by this, we conduct a critical yet under-explored analysis of the vision encoder of MLLMs through diverse and in-depth experiments, ranging from ImageNet classification and segmentation to gradient visualization. Our results demonstrate that MLLM's post-training strategy (i.e., SFT or RL) not only leads to distinct outcomes on MLLM downstream tasks, but also fundamentally reshapes MLLM's underlying visual representations. Specifically, the key finding of our study is that RL produces stronger and precisely localized visual representations compared to SFT, boosting the ability of the vision encoder for MLLM. We then reframe our findings into a simple recipe for building strong vision encoders for MLLMs, Preference-Instructed Vision OpTimization (PIVOT). When integrated into MLLMs, a PIVOT-trained vision encoder outperforms even larger and more heavily-trained counterparts, despite requiring less than 1% of the computational cost of standard vision pretraining. This result opens an effective and efficient path for advancing the vision backbones of MLLMs. Project page available at https://june-page.github.io/pivot/
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习使多模态大语言模型的视觉能力超越监督微调
多模态大语言模型（MLLM）研究中的一个主流假设是，其性能主要继承自参数规模庞大、能力卓越的大语言模型主干。这导致对决定MLLM如何感知图像的视觉编码器的理解存在空白。近期MLLM训练范式从监督微调（SFT）转向强化学习（RL），放大了这一忽视——即严重缺乏对此类训练如何重塑视觉编码器及MLLM的分析。为此，我们首先探究了训练策略对MLLM的影响，发现在强视觉相关的视觉问答基准上，RL明显优于SFT。基于此，我们通过从ImageNet分类与分割到梯度可视化的多样深度实验，对MLLM的视觉编码器进行了关键而尚未充分探索的分析。结果表明，MLLM的后训练策略（即SFT或RL）不仅导致下游任务结果差异，更从根本上重塑了MLLM的底层视觉表征。具体而言，本研究的核心发现是：相比SFT，RL能产生更强且定位精准的视觉表征，从而提升MLLM视觉编码器的能力。我们将此发现转化为构建MLLM强视觉编码器的简明方案——偏好指导视觉优化（PIVOT）。将PIVOT训练的视觉编码器集成至MLLM后，其性能甚至超越规模更大、训练更充分的视觉编码器，而计算成本不足标准视觉预训练的1%。这为推进MLLM视觉主干的发展开辟了高效路径。项目页面详见：https://june-page.github.io/pivot/

The authors first demonstrate that Reinforcement Learning (RL) surpasses Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) on vision-heavy VQA tasks, motivating a deep analysis of the vision encoder through experiments in classification, segmentation, and gradient visualization. The Past Is Not Past: Memory-Enhanced Dynamic Reward Shaping
Authors: Yang Liu, Enxi Wang, Yufei Gao, Weixin Zhang, Bo Wang, Zhiyuan Zeng, Yikai Zhang, Yining Zheng, Xipeng Qiu
First: 2026-04-13T10:59:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T10:59:28+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Despite the success of reinforcement learning for large language models, a common failure mode is reduced sampling diversity, where the policy repeatedly generates similar erroneous behaviors. Classical entropy regularization encourages randomness under the current policy, but does not explicitly discourage recurrent failure patterns across rollouts. We propose MEDS, a Memory-Enhanced Dynamic reward Shaping framework that incorporates historical behavioral signals into reward design. By storing and leveraging intermediate model representations, we capture features of past rollouts and use density-based clustering to identify frequently recurring error patterns. Rollouts assigned to more prevalent error clusters are penalized more heavily, encouraging broader exploration while reducing repeated mistakes. Across five datasets and three base models, MEDS consistently improves average performance over existing baselines, achieving gains of up to 4.13 pass@1 points and 4.37 pass@128 points. Additional analyses using both LLM-based annotations and quantitative diversity metrics show that MEDS increases behavioral diversity during sampling.
中文标题/摘要
标题：过去并未过去：基于记忆增强的动态奖励塑形
尽管强化学习在大语言模型中取得了成功，但其常见失效模式是采样多样性降低——策略会反复生成相似的错误行为。经典的熵正则化方法虽能鼓励当前策略下的随机性，却未明确抑制多次迭代中重复出现的失败模式。我们提出MEDS（记忆增强的动态奖励塑形框架），将历史行为信号纳入奖励设计。通过存储并利用中间模型表示，我们捕捉过往迭代的特征，并采用基于密度的聚类识别频繁重现的错误模式。被分配到更普遍错误簇的迭代会承受更重惩罚，从而在减少重复错误的同时鼓励更广泛的探索。在五个数据集和三个基础模型上的实验表明，MEDS始终优于现有基线方法，平均性能最高提升4.13个pass@1点和4.37个pass@128点。基于大语言模型的标注与定量多样性指标分析进一步证实，MEDS能有效提升采样过程中的行为多样性。

Motivated by the issue of reduced sampling diversity in reinforcement learning for large language models, where policies often repeat similar errors, this paper introduces MEDS, a Memory-Enhanced Dynamic reward Shaping framework. The method incorporates historical behavioral signals by storing intermediate model representations and using density-based clustering to identify recurring error patterns, then penalizes rollouts in prevalent error clusters more heavily to encourage broader exploration and reduce repeated mistakes. Experimental results across five datasets and three base models show that MEDS consistently outperforms existing baselines, achieving performance gains of up to 4.13 pass@1 and 4.37 pass@128 points, while analyses confirm increased behavioral diversity during sampling.
针对大型语言模型强化学习中采样多样性降低、策略常重复类似错误的问题，本文提出了MEDS，一种记忆增强的动态奖励塑形框架。该方法通过存储中间模型表示并利用基于密度的聚类识别重复出现的错误模式，将历史行为信号融入奖励设计，对属于常见错误簇的轨迹施加更重惩罚，以鼓励更广泛的探索并减少重复错误。在五个数据集和三个基础模型上的实验结果表明，MEDS持续优于现有基线，性能提升最高达4.13 pass@1和4.37 pass@128点，分析还证实了其在采样过程中增加了行为多样性。
Self-Organizing Dual-Buffer Adaptive Clustering Experience Replay (SODACER) for Safe Reinforcement Learning in Optimal Control
Authors: Roya Khalili Amirabadi, Mohsen Jalaeian Farimani, Omid Solaymani Fard
First: 2026-01-10T11:43:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T10:43:27+00:00
Comments: Published in Nature Scientific Reports (2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper proposes a novel reinforcement learning framework, named Self-Organizing Dual-buffer Adaptive Clustering Experience Replay (SODACER), designed to achieve safe and scalable optimal control of nonlinear systems. The proposed SODACER mechanism consisting of a Fast-Buffer for rapid adaptation to recent experiences and a Slow-Buffer equipped with a self-organizing adaptive clustering mechanism to maintain diverse and non-redundant historical experiences. The adaptive clustering mechanism dynamically prunes redundant samples, optimizing memory efficiency while retaining critical environmental patterns. The approach integrates SODACER with Control Barrier Functions (CBFs) to guarantee safety by enforcing state and input constraints throughout the learning process. To enhance convergence and stability, the framework is combined with the Sophia optimizer, enabling adaptive second-order gradient updates. The proposed SODACER-Sophia's architecture ensures reliable, effective, and robust learning in dynamic, safety-critical environments, offering a generalizable solution for applications in robotics, healthcare, and large-scale system optimization. The proposed approach is validated on a nonlinear Human Papillomavirus (HPV) transmission model with multiple control inputs and safety constraints. Comparative evaluations against random and clustering-based experience replay methods demonstrate that SODACER achieves faster convergence, improved sample efficiency, and a superior bias-variance trade-off, while maintaining safe system trajectories, validated via the Friedman test.
中文标题/摘要
标题：用于最优控制安全强化学习的自组织双缓冲自适应聚类经验回放方法（SODACER）
本文提出了一种名为自组织双缓冲自适应聚类经验回放（SODACER）的新型强化学习框架，旨在实现非线性系统的安全可扩展最优控制。该SODACER机制包含一个用于快速适应近期经验的快速缓冲区，以及一个配备自组织自适应聚类机制的慢速缓冲区，以保持多样且非冗余的历史经验。自适应聚类机制动态修剪冗余样本，在保留关键环境模式的同时优化内存效率。该方法将SODACER与控制屏障函数（CBFs）结合，通过在整个学习过程中强制执行状态和输入约束来保证安全性。为提升收敛性和稳定性，该框架与Sophia优化器结合，实现自适应二阶梯度更新。所提出的SODACER-Sophia架构确保了在动态、安全关键环境中的可靠、有效且鲁棒的学习，为机器人、医疗和大规模系统优化等应用提供了通用解决方案。该方法在具有多控制输入和安全约束的非线性人乳头瘤病毒（HPV）传播模型上得到验证。与随机及基于聚类的经验回放方法的对比评估表明，SODACER实现了更快的收敛速度、更高的样本效率以及更优的偏差-方差权衡，同时通过弗里德曼检验验证了其能保持安全的系统轨迹。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for safe and scalable optimal control in nonlinear systems, this paper introduces SODACER, a reinforcement learning framework featuring a dual-buffer experience replay with self-organizing adaptive clustering to manage experience diversity and redundancy efficiently. The method integrates Control Barrier Functions to enforce safety constraints and employs the Sophia optimizer for stable, adaptive second-order gradient updates. Experimental validation on a nonlinear HPV transmission model demonstrates that SODACER achieves faster convergence, better sample efficiency, and a superior bias-variance trade-off compared to baseline replay methods, while maintaining safe trajectories.
本文旨在实现非线性系统的安全、可扩展最优控制，提出了SODACER强化学习框架，该框架采用具有自组织自适应聚类的双缓冲区经验回放机制来高效管理经验的多样性和冗余性。该方法结合控制屏障函数以确保安全约束，并利用Sophia优化器进行稳定的自适应二阶梯度更新。在非线性HPV传播模型上的实验验证表明，与随机和基于聚类的经验回放方法相比，SODACER实现了更快的收敛速度、更高的样本效率以及更优的偏差-方差权衡，同时保持了安全的系统轨迹。
Enhanced-FQL($λ$), an Efficient and Interpretable RL with novel Fuzzy Eligibility Traces and Segmented Experience Replay
Authors: Mohsen Jalaeian-Farimani, Xiong Xiong, Luca Bascetta
First: 2026-01-07T20:59:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T10:28:16+00:00
Comments: Accepted in ECC26 conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper introduces a fuzzy reinforcement learning framework, Enhanced-FQL($λ$), that integrates novel Fuzzified Eligibility Traces (FET) and Segmented Experience Replay (SER) into fuzzy Q-learning with the Fuzzified Bellman Equation (FBE) for continuous control. The proposed approach employs an interpretable fuzzy rule base instead of complex neural architectures, while maintaining competitive performance through two key innovations: a fuzzified Bellman equation with eligibility traces for stable multi-step credit assignment, and a memory-efficient segment-based experience replay mechanism for enhanced sample efficiency. Theoretical analysis proves the proposed method convergence under standard assumptions. On the Cart--Pole benchmark, Enhanced-FQL($λ$) improves sample efficiency and reduces variance relative to $n$-step fuzzy TD and fuzzy SARSA($λ$), while remaining competitive with the tested DDPG baseline. These results support the proposed framework as an interpretable and computationally compact alternative for moderate-scale continuous control problems.

标题：Enhanced-FQL($λ$)：一种高效可解释的强化学习方法，融合新型模糊资格迹与分段经验回放
本文提出一种模糊强化学习框架Enhanced-FQL($λ$)，将新型模糊资格迹与分段经验回放机制融入基于模糊贝尔曼方程的模糊Q学习，用于连续控制任务。该方法采用可解释的模糊规则库替代复杂神经网络架构，通过两项关键创新保持竞争力：采用带资格迹的模糊贝尔曼方程实现稳定的多步信用分配，以及基于分段的高效经验回放机制提升样本效率。理论分析证明该方法在标准假设下具有收敛性。在Cart-Pole基准测试中，Enhanced-FQL($λ$)相比$n$步模糊时序差分和模糊SARSA($λ$)提升了样本效率并降低方差，同时与测试的DDPG基线保持相当性能。这些结果表明该框架可作为中等规模连续控制问题的可解释且计算紧凑的替代方案。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for interpretable and efficient reinforcement learning for continuous control, this paper proposes Enhanced-FQL(λ), a fuzzy reinforcement learning framework that replaces complex neural networks with an interpretable fuzzy rule base. The method integrates two key innovations: Fuzzified Eligibility Traces (FET) for stable multi-step credit assignment via a fuzzified Bellman equation, and Segmented Experience Replay (SER) for memory-efficient sample reuse. Evolving Many Worlds: Towards Open-Ended Discovery in Petri Dish NCA via Population-Based Training
Authors: Uljad Berdica, Jakob Foerster, Frank Hutter, Arber Zela
First: 2026-04-13T09:56:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T09:56:22+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 12 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The generation of sustained, open-ended complexity from local interactions remains a fundamental challenge in artificial life. Differentiable multi-agent systems, such as Petri Dish Neural Cellular Automata (PD-NCA), exhibit rich self-organization driven purely by spatial competition; however, they are highly sensitive to hyperparameters and frequently collapse into uninteresting patterns and dynamics, such as frozen equilibria or structureless noise. In this paper, we introduce PBT-NCA, a meta-evolutionary algorithm that evolves a population of PD-NCAs subject to a composite objective that rewards both historical behavioral novelty and contemporary visual diversity. Driven by this continuous evolutionary pressure, PBT-NCA spontaneously generates a plethora of emergent lifelike phenomena over extended horizons-a hallmark of true open-endedness. Strikingly, the substrate autonomously discovers diverse morphological survival and self-organization strategies. We observe highly regular, coordinated periodic waves; spore-like scattering where homogeneous groups eject cell-like clusters to colonize distant territories; and fluid, shape-shifting macro-structures that migrate across the substrate, maintaining stable outer boundaries that enclose highly active interiors. By actively penalizing monocultures and dead states, PBT-NCA sustains a state of effective complexity that is neither globally ordered nor globally random, operating persistently at the "edge of chaos".
中文标题/摘要
标题：演化多世界：通过基于种群的训练实现培养皿神经细胞自动机的开放式发现
从局部相互作用中产生持续、开放式的复杂性仍是人工生命领域的根本挑战。可微分多智能体系统，如培养皿神经细胞自动机（PD-NCA），展现出纯粹由空间竞争驱动的丰富自组织行为；然而，它们对超参数高度敏感，常坍缩为无趣的模式与动态，如冻结平衡态或无结构噪声。本文提出PBT-NCA——一种元演化算法，通过复合目标演化PD-NCA种群，该目标同时奖励历史行为新颖性与当前视觉多样性。在持续演化压力驱动下，PBT-NCA在长时间尺度上自发涌现出大量类生命现象，这是真正开放性的标志。引人注目的是，该系统自主发现了多样化的形态生存与自组织策略：我们观察到高度规则、协调的周期性波动；孢子状散射现象（同质群体喷射类细胞团以拓殖远域）；以及流体般变形、在基底上迁移的宏观结构，其保持稳定的外部边界并包裹高度活跃的内部。通过主动惩罚单一化状态与死亡态，PBT-NCA维持着有效复杂性状态——既非全局有序亦非全局随机，持久运行于“混沌边缘”。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of achieving sustained, open-ended complexity in artificial life systems, which often collapse into trivial patterns, this paper introduces PBT-NCA, a meta-evolutionary algorithm that applies population-based training to Petri Dish Neural Cellular Automata. The method evolves a population of NCAs using a composite objective that rewards both historical behavioral novelty and contemporary visual diversity, actively penalizing monocultures and dead states. Learning to Focus and Precise Cropping: A Reinforcement Learning Framework with Information Gaps and Grounding Loss for MLLMs
Authors: Xuanpu Zhao, Zhentao Tan, Dianmo Sheng, Tianxiang Chen, Yao Liu, Yue Wu, Tao Gong, Qi Chu, Nenghai Yu
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-03-29T03:18:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T08:50:29+00:00
Comments: Accepted by CVPR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
To enhance the perception and reasoning capabilities of multimodal large language models in complex visual scenes, recent research has introduced agent-based workflows. In these works, MLLMs autonomously utilize image cropping tool to analyze regions of interest for question answering. While existing training strategies, such as those employing supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning, have made significant progress, our empirical analysis reveals a key limitation. We demonstrate the model's strong reliance on global input and its weak dependence on the details within the cropped region. To address this issue, we propose a novel two-stage reinforcement learning framework that does not require trajectory supervision. In the first stage, we introduce the ``Information Gap" mechanism by adjusting the granularity of the global image. This mechanism trains the model to answer questions by focusing on cropped key regions, driven by the information gain these regions provide. The second stage further enhances cropping precision by incorporating a grounding loss, using a small number of bounding box annotations. Experiments show that our method significantly enhances the model's attention to cropped regions, enabling it to achieve state-of-the-art performance on high-resolution visual question-answering benchmarks. Our method provides a more efficient approach for perceiving and reasoning fine-grained details in MLLMs. Code is available at: https://github.com/XuanPu-Z/LFPC.
中文标题/摘要
标题：学习聚焦与精准裁剪：面向多模态大语言模型的含信息间隙与定位损失强化学习框架
为增强多模态大语言模型在复杂视觉场景中的感知与推理能力，近期研究引入了基于智能体的工作流程。这些研究使MLLM能自主利用图像裁剪工具分析感兴趣区域以进行问答。尽管现有训练策略（如采用监督微调与强化学习的方法）已取得显著进展，但我们的实证分析揭示了一个关键局限：模型对全局输入存在强依赖，而对裁剪区域内的细节依赖较弱。为解决该问题，我们提出一种无需轨迹监督的新型两阶段强化学习框架。第一阶段通过调整全局图像粒度引入“信息间隙”机制，该机制驱动模型基于裁剪关键区域提供的信息增益来聚焦于这些区域以回答问题。第二阶段通过引入少量边界框标注的定位损失进一步提升裁剪精度。实验表明，我们的方法显著增强了模型对裁剪区域的关注度，使其在高分辨率视觉问答基准上达到最先进性能。该方法为MLLM感知与推理细粒度细节提供了更高效的途径。代码发布于：https://github.com/XuanPu-Z/LFPC。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the observation that multimodal large language models overly rely on global image context and insufficiently utilize details from cropped regions when using cropping tools for visual question answering, this paper proposes a novel two-stage reinforcement learning framework without trajectory supervision. The method first introduces an Information Gap mechanism that adjusts global image granularity to train the model to focus on cropped key regions based on information gain, then incorporates a grounding loss with minimal bounding box annotations to enhance cropping precision. Experimental results demonstrate that this approach significantly improves the model's attention to cropped regions, achieving state-of-the-art performance on high-resolution visual question-answering benchmarks and providing a more efficient way for fine-grained perception and reasoning.
本文的动机是观察到多模态大语言模型在使用裁剪工具进行视觉问答时，过度依赖全局图像上下文，而对裁剪区域内的细节利用不足。为此，论文提出了一种无需轨迹监督的新型两阶段强化学习框架：第一阶段通过引入信息间隙机制，调整全局图像的粒度，训练模型基于信息增益关注裁剪的关键区域；第二阶段则结合少量边界框标注的定位损失来提升裁剪精度。实验结果表明，该方法显著增强了模型对裁剪区域的注意力，在高分辨率视觉问答基准上实现了最先进的性能，为细粒度感知和推理提供了更高效的途径。
CuraLight: Debate-Guided Data Curation for LLM-Centered Traffic Signal Control
Authors: Qing Guo, Xinhang Li, Junyu Chen, Zheng Guo, Shengzhe Xu, Lin Zhang, Lei Li
First: 2026-04-07T10:05:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T08:40:25+00:00
Comments: accepted at IJCNN 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Traffic signal control (TSC) is a core component of intelligent transportation systems (ITS), aiming to reduce congestion, emissions, and travel time. Recent approaches based on reinforcement learning (RL) and large language models (LLMs) have improved adaptivity, but still suffer from limited interpretability, insufficient interaction data, and weak generalization to heterogeneous intersections. This paper proposes CuraLight, an LLM-centered framework where an RL agent assists the fine-tuning of an LLM-based traffic signal controller. The RL agent explores traffic environments and generates high-quality interaction trajectories, which are converted into prompt-response pairs for imitation fine-tuning. A multi-LLM ensemble deliberation system further evaluates candidate signal timing actions through structured debate, providing preference-aware supervision signals for training. Experiments conducted in SUMO across heterogeneous real-world networks from Jinan, Hangzhou, and Yizhuang demonstrate that CuraLight consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, reducing average travel time by 5.34 percent, average queue length by 5.14 percent, and average waiting time by 7.02 percent. The results highlight the effectiveness of combining RL-assisted exploration with deliberation-based data curation for scalable and interpretable traffic signal control.

标题：CuraLight：面向大语言模型交通信号控制的辩论引导数据精炼框架
交通信号控制是智能交通系统的核心组件，旨在缓解拥堵、降低排放、缩短行程时间。基于强化学习和大语言模型的最新方法提升了适应性，但仍存在可解释性有限、交互数据不足、对异构路口泛化能力弱等问题。本文提出CuraLight——以大语言模型为中心的框架，其中强化学习智能体辅助微调基于大语言模型的信号控制器。强化学习智能体探索交通环境并生成高质量交互轨迹，将其转化为提示-响应对以进行模仿微调。多语言模型集成审议系统通过结构化辩论评估候选信号配时方案，为训练提供偏好感知的监督信号。在SUMO中使用济南、杭州、亦庄异构真实路网进行的实验表明，CuraLight持续优于前沿基线方法，平均行程时间降低5.34%，平均排队长度减少5.14%，平均等待时间下降7.02%。结果凸显了强化学习辅助探索与基于辩论的数据精炼相结合对可扩展、可解释交通信号控制的有效性。

Curriculum-based Sample Efficient Reinforcement Learning for Robust Stabilization of a Quadrotor
Authors: Fausto Mauricio Lagos Suarez, Akshit Saradagi, Vidya Sumathy, Shruti Kotpaliwar, George Nikolakopoulos
First: 2025-01-30T17:05:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T08:25:27+00:00
Comments: 8 pages, 7 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This article introduces a novel sample-efficient curriculum learning (CL) approach for training an end-to-end reinforcement learning (RL) policy for robust stabilization of a Quadrotor. The learning objective is to simultaneously stabilize position and yaw-orientation from random initial conditions through direct control over motor RPMs (end-to-end), while adhering to pre-specified transient and steady-state specifications. This objective, relevant in aerial inspection applications, is challenging for conventional one-stage end-to-end RL, which requires substantial computational resources and lengthy training times. To address this challenge, this article draws inspiration from human-inspired curriculum learning and decomposes the learning objective into a three-stage curriculum that incrementally increases task complexity, while transferring knowledge from one stage to the next. In the proposed curriculum, the policy sequentially learns hovering, the coupling between translational and rotational degrees of freedom, and robustness to random non-zero initial velocities, utilizing a custom reward function and episode truncation conditions. The results demonstrate that the proposed CL approach achieves superior performance compared to a policy trained conventionally in one stage, with the same reward function and hyperparameters, while significantly reducing computational resource needs (samples) and convergence time. The CL-trained policy's performance and robustness are thoroughly validated in a simulation engine (Gym-PyBullet-Drones), under random initial conditions, and in an inspection pose-tracking scenario. A video presenting our results is available at https://youtu.be/9wv6T4eezAU.

From Pixels to Digital Agents: An Empirical Study on the Taxonomy and Technological Trends of Reinforcement Learning Environments
Authors: Lijing Luo, Yiben Luo, Alexey Gorbatovski, Sergey Kovalchuk, Xiaodan Liang
First: 2026-03-25T05:56:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T08:15:41+00:00
Comments: 32 pages main text, 18 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The remarkable progress of reinforcement learning (RL) is intrinsically tied to the environments used to train and evaluate artificial agents. Moving beyond traditional qualitative reviews, this work presents a large-scale, data-driven empirical investigation into the evolution of RL environments. By programmatically processing a massive corpus of academic literature and rigorously distilling over 2,000 core publications, we propose a quantitative methodology to map the transition from isolated physical simulations to generalist, language-driven foundation agents. Implementing a novel, multi-dimensional taxonomy, we systematically analyze benchmarks against diverse application domains and requisite cognitive capabilities. Our automated semantic and statistical analysis reveals a profound, data-verified paradigm shift: the bifurcation of the field into a "Semantic Prior" ecosystem dominated by Large Language Models (LLMs) and a "Domain-Specific Generalization" ecosystem. Furthermore, we characterize the "cognitive fingerprints" of these distinct domains to uncover the underlying mechanisms of cross-task synergy, multi-domain interference, and zero-shot generalization. Ultimately, this study offers a rigorous, quantitative roadmap for designing the next generation of Embodied Semantic Simulators, bridging the gap between continuous physical control and high-level logical reasoning.
