标题：从像素到数字智能体：强化学习环境分类体系与技术趋势的实证研究
强化学习（RL）的显著进展与用于训练和评估智能体的环境密不可分。本研究超越传统的定性综述，对RL环境的演变进行了大规模、数据驱动的实证调查。通过程序化处理海量学术文献并严格提炼超过2000篇核心出版物，我们提出了一种量化方法，以描绘从孤立的物理模拟到通用、语言驱动的基座智能体的转变路径。通过实施一种新颖的多维分类体系，我们系统分析了不同应用领域和所需认知能力对应的基准测试。自动化的语义与统计分析揭示了一个经数据验证的深刻范式转变：该领域正分化为以大型语言模型（LLM）为主导的“语义先验”生态系统和“领域特定泛化”生态系统。此外，我们刻画了这些不同领域的“认知指纹”，以揭示跨任务协同、多领域干扰和零样本泛化的内在机制。最终，本研究为设计下一代具身语义模拟器提供了严谨的量化路线图，弥合了连续物理控制与高层逻辑推理之间的鸿沟。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to move beyond qualitative reviews and understand the evolution of reinforcement learning (RL) environments that underpin agent progress, this study conducts a large-scale, data-driven empirical analysis. The method involves programmatically processing a massive corpus of literature to distill over 2,000 core publications, proposing a quantitative methodology and a novel multi-dimensional taxonomy to map the transition from physical simulations to language-driven foundation agents. The main experimental results reveal a data-verified paradigm shift, identifying a bifurcation into a "Semantic Prior" ecosystem dominated by Large Language Models and a "Domain-Specific Generalization" ecosystem, and characterize the cognitive fingerprints of these domains to uncover mechanisms of cross-task synergy and generalization.
本研究旨在超越定性综述，理解支撑智能体发展的强化学习环境演变，因此进行了大规模数据驱动的实证分析。方法上，通过程序化处理大量文献，提炼了2000多篇核心出版物，提出了一种量化方法和新颖的多维分类法，以描绘从物理模拟到语言驱动基础智能体的转变。主要实验结果揭示了一个数据验证的范式转变，识别出领域分化为以大型语言模型主导的“语义先验”生态系统和“领域特定泛化”生态系统，并刻画了这些领域的认知特征，以揭示跨任务协同和泛化的内在机制。
Scalable Stewardship of an LLM-Assisted Clinical Benchmark with Physician Oversight
Authors: Junze Ye, Daniel Tawfik, Alex J. Goodell, Nikhil V. Kotha, Mark K. Buyyounouski, Mohsen Bayati
First: 2025-12-22T18:59:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T08:00:46+00:00
Comments: Github codebase: https://github.com/junzeye/validate-medcalc-labels
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reference labels for machine-learning benchmarks are increasingly synthesized with LLM assistance, but their reliability remains underexamined. We audit MedCalc-Bench, a clinical benchmark for medical score computation whose labels were partly derived with LLM assistance, and develop a scalable physician-in-the-loop stewardship pipeline to reassess them. At least 27% of test labels are likely erroneous or incomputable. On a 50-instance subset validated by physicians, our recomputed labels agree with physician ground truth 74% of the time (95% CI, 60-84%) versus 20% for the originals (95% CI, 11-33%). Using original labels to evaluate frontier LLMs underestimates accuracy by 16-23 percentage points. In a controlled reinforcement-learning experiment, a model trained on recomputed labels outperforms one trained on originals by 13.5 percentage points (95% CI, 10.6-16.6%) on physician-labeled instances, and this advantage extends to related medical tasks. LLM-assisted benchmarks can propagate systematic errors into both evaluation and post-training unless actively stewarded.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于医生监督的大语言模型辅助临床基准的可扩展管理

Motivated by concerns over the reliability of LLM-assisted benchmark labels, this study audits MedCalc-Bench, a clinical benchmark for medical score computation, and develops a scalable physician-in-the-loop stewardship pipeline to reassess its labels. From Answers to Arguments: Toward Trustworthy Clinical Diagnostic Reasoning with Toulmin-Guided Curriculum Goal-Conditioned Learning
Authors: Chen Zhan, Xiaoyu Tan, Gengchen Ma, Yu-Jie Xiong, Xiaoyan Jiang, Xihe Qiu
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-13T07:49:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T07:49:39+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ACL 2026 (Main Conference)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The integration of Large Language Models (LLMs) into clinical decision support is critically obstructed by their opaque and often unreliable reasoning. In the high-stakes domain of healthcare, correct answers alone are insufficient; clinical practice demands full transparency to ensure patient safety and enable professional accountability. A pervasive and dangerous weakness of current LLMs is their tendency to produce "correct answers through flawed reasoning." This issue is far more than a minor academic flaw; such process errors signal a fundamental lack of robust understanding, making the model prone to broader hallucinations and unpredictable failures when faced with real-world clinical complexity. In this paper, we establish a framework for trustworthy clinical argumentation by adapting the Toulmin model to the diagnostic process. We propose a novel training pipeline: Curriculum Goal-Conditioned Learning (CGCL), designed to progressively train LLM to generate diagnostic arguments that explicitly follow this Toulmin structure. CGCL's progressive three-stage curriculum systematically builds a solid clinical argument: (1) extracting facts and generating differential diagnoses; (2) justifying a core hypothesis while rebutting alternatives; and (3) synthesizing the analysis into a final, qualified conclusion. We validate CGCL using T-Eval, a quantitative framework measuring the integrity of the diagnosis reasoning. Experiments show that our method achieves diagnostic accuracy and reasoning quality comparable to resource-intensive Reinforcement Learning (RL) methods, while offering a more stable and efficient training pipeline.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从答案到论证：基于图尔敏模型的课程目标条件学习实现可信临床诊断推理
大语言模型（LLMs）在临床决策支持中的应用因其不透明且常不可靠的推理而严重受阻。在医疗这一高风险领域，仅提供正确答案远远不够；临床实践要求完全透明以确保患者安全并实现专业问责。当前LLMs普遍存在一个危险缺陷：倾向于通过错误推理得出“正确答案”。这远非细微的学术瑕疵，此类过程错误表明模型缺乏稳健理解力，面对真实临床复杂性时易产生更广泛的幻觉和不可预测的失败。本文通过将图尔敏模型适配至诊断过程，构建了可信临床论证框架。我们提出一种新颖的训练流程：课程目标条件学习（CGCL），旨在渐进式训练LLM生成严格遵循图尔敏结构的诊断论证。CGCL的三阶段渐进课程系统化构建坚实临床论证：（1）提取事实并生成鉴别诊断；（2）论证核心假设同时反驳替代方案；（3）将分析综合为最终限定结论。我们使用T-Eval（一种量化诊断推理完整性的评估框架）验证CGCL。实验表明，本方法在达到与资源密集型强化学习方法相当的诊断准确性和推理质量的同时，提供了更稳定高效的训练流程。

Motivated by the critical need for transparent and reliable reasoning in clinical decision support, where large language models (LLMs) often produce correct answers through flawed reasoning, this paper introduces a framework for trustworthy clinical argumentation by adapting the Toulmin model to the diagnostic process. The method proposes Curriculum Goal-Conditioned Learning (CGCL), a novel training pipeline that progressively trains LLMs across three stages to generate structured diagnostic arguments: extracting facts and generating differential diagnoses, justifying a core hypothesis while rebutting alternatives, and synthesizing a qualified conclusion. AIM: Intent-Aware Unified world action Modeling with Spatial Value Maps
Authors: Liaoyuan Fan, Zetian Xu, Chen Cao, Wenyao Zhang, Mingqi Yuan, Jiayu Chen
First: 2026-04-13T07:48:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T07:48:58+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Pretrained video generation models provide strong priors for robot control, but existing unified world action models still struggle to decode reliable actions without substantial robot-specific training. We attribute this limitation to a structural mismatch: while video models capture how scenes evolve, action generation requires explicit reasoning about where to interact and the underlying manipulation intent. We introduce AIM, an intent-aware unified world action model that bridges this gap via an explicit spatial interface. Instead of decoding actions directly from future visual representations, AIM predicts an aligned spatial value map that encodes task-relevant interaction structure, enabling a control-oriented abstraction of future dynamics. Built on a pretrained video generation model, AIM jointly models future observations and value maps within a shared mixture-of-transformers architecture. It employs intent-causal attention to route future information to the action branch exclusively through the value representation. We further propose a self-distillation reinforcement learning stage that freezes the video and value branches and optimizes only the action head using dense rewards derived from projected value-map responses together with sparse task-level signals. To support training and evaluation, we construct a simulation dataset of 30K manipulation trajectories with synchronized multi-view observations, actions, and value-map annotations. Experiments on RoboTwin 2.0 benchmark show that AIM achieves a 94.0% average success rate, significantly outperforming prior unified world action baselines. Notably, the improvement is more pronounced in long-horizon and contact-sensitive manipulation tasks, demonstrating the effectiveness of explicit spatial-intent modeling as a bridge between visual world modeling and robot control.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AIM：基于空间价值图的意图感知统一世界动作建模
预训练视频生成模型为机器人控制提供了强先验，但现有统一世界动作模型仍需大量机器人专属训练才能解码可靠动作。我们认为这一局限源于结构错配：视频模型捕捉场景演变，而动作生成需显式推理交互位置与底层操作意图。本文提出AIM，一种通过显式空间接口弥合此差距的意图感知统一世界动作模型。AIM不直接从未来视觉表征解码动作，而是预测编码任务相关交互结构的对齐空间价值图，实现对未来动态的面向控制抽象。基于预训练视频生成模型，AIM在共享混合Transformer架构中联合建模未来观测与价值图，采用意图因果注意力机制，使未来信息仅通过价值表征路由至动作分支。我们进一步提出自蒸馏强化学习阶段：冻结视频与价值分支，仅使用从投影价值图响应导出的密集奖励与稀疏任务级信号优化动作头。为支持训练评估，构建包含3万条操作轨迹的仿真数据集，含同步多视角观测、动作及价值图标注。RoboTwin 2.0基准实验表明，AIM以94.0%平均成功率显著超越现有统一世界动作基线，在长时程与接触敏感任务中提升尤为显著，验证了显式空间意图建模作为视觉世界建模与机器人控制桥梁的有效性。

The method introduces AIM, an intent-aware unified world action model that bridges this gap via an explicit spatial interface; instead of decoding actions directly from future visual representations, AIM predicts an aligned spatial value map encoding task-relevant interaction structure, using a shared mixture-of-transformers architecture built on a pretrained video model with intent-causal attention to route future information through the value representation, and further employs a self-distillation reinforcement learning stage to optimize the action head. The main experimental results, based on a simulation dataset of 30K manipulation trajectories, show that AIM achieves a 94.0% average success rate on the RoboTwin 2.0 benchmark, significantly outperforming prior baselines, with notable improvements in long-horizon and contact-sensitive tasks, demonstrating the effectiveness of explicit spatial-intent modeling.

Deep deterministic policy gradient with symmetric data augmentation for lateral attitude tracking control of a fixed-wing aircraft
Authors: Yifei Li, Erik-Jan van Kampen
First: 2024-07-13T08:20:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T07:47:23+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The symmetry of dynamical systems can be exploited for state-transition prediction and to facilitate control policy optimization. This paper leverages system symmetry to develop sample-efficient offline reinforcement learning (RL) approaches. Under the symmetry assumption for a Markov Decision Process (MDP), a symmetric data augmentation method is proposed. The augmented samples are integrated into the dataset of Deep Deterministic Policy Gradient (DDPG) to enhance its coverage rate of the state-action space. Furthermore, sample utilization efficiency is improved by introducing a second critic trained on the augmented samples, resulting in a dual-critic structure. The aircraft's model is verified to be symmetric, and flight control simulations demonstrate accelerated policy convergence when augmented samples are employed.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于对称数据增强的深度确定性策略梯度在固定翼飞机横侧向姿态跟踪控制中的应用
动力学系统的对称性可用于状态转移预测并促进控制策略优化。本文利用系统对称性开发样本高效的离线强化学习方法。在马尔可夫决策过程对称性假设下，提出了一种对称数据增强方法。增强样本被整合至深度确定性策略梯度数据集中，以提升其对状态-动作空间的覆盖度。此外，通过引入基于增强样本训练的第二评价器构建双评价器结构，提高了样本利用效率。验证了飞机模型的对称性，飞行控制仿真表明采用增强样本可加速策略收敛。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for sample-efficient offline reinforcement learning in control tasks, this paper proposes a method that exploits the symmetry of dynamical systems to enhance the Deep Deterministic Policy Gradient (DDPG) algorithm. The approach introduces a symmetric data augmentation technique to expand the coverage of the state-action space in the dataset and incorporates a dual-critic structure, where a second critic is trained on augmented samples to improve sample utilization. Experimental results on a fixed-wing aircraft lateral attitude tracking control task confirm the system's symmetry and demonstrate that the use of augmented samples significantly accelerates policy convergence in flight control simulations.
本文以提高控制任务中离线强化学习的样本效率为动机，提出了一种利用动力系统对称性来改进深度确定性策略梯度（DDPG）算法的方法。该方法采用对称数据增强技术来扩展数据集中状态-动作空间的覆盖范围，并引入了双评论家结构，其中第二个评论家基于增强样本进行训练以提高样本利用率。在固定翼飞机横向姿态跟踪控制的实验中，验证了系统的对称性，并表明使用增强样本能显著加速飞行控制仿真中的策略收敛。
MADQRL: Distributed Quantum Reinforcement Learning Framework for Multi-Agent Environments
Authors: Abhishek Sawaika, Samuel Yen-Chi Chen, Udaya Parampalli, Rajkumar Buyya
First: 2026-04-13T07:44:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T07:44:23+00:00
Comments: Accepted in QC4C3 Workshop at IEEE QCNC, 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) is one of the most practical ways to learn from real-life use-cases. Motivated from the cognitive methods used by humans makes it a widely acceptable strategy in the field of artificial intelligence. Most of the environments used for RL are often high-dimensional, and traditional RL algorithms becomes computationally expensive and challenging to effectively learn from such systems. Recent advancements in practical demonstration of quantum computing (QC) theories, such as compact encoding, enhanced representation and learning algorithms, random sampling, or the inherent stochastic nature of quantum systems, have opened up new directions to tackle these challenges. Quantum reinforcement learning (QRL) is seeking significant traction over the past few years. However, the current state of quantum hardware is not enough to cater for such high-dimensional environments with complex multi-agent setup. To tackle this issue, we propose a distributed framework for QRL where multiple agents learn independently, distributing the load of joint training from individual machines. Our method works well for environments with disjoint sets of action and observation spaces, but can also be extended to other systems with reasonable approximations. We analyze the proposed method on cooperative-pong environment and our results indicate ~10% improvement from other distribution strategies, and ~5% improvement from classical models of policy representation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MADQRL：面向多智能体环境的分布式量子强化学习框架
强化学习（RL）是从现实用例中学习的最实用方法之一，其受人类认知方法启发，在人工智能领域被广泛接受。多数RL环境具有高维特性，传统RL算法计算成本高昂，难以有效学习。量子计算（QC）理论的实际进展，如紧凑编码、增强表示与学习算法、随机采样或量子系统固有的随机性，为解决这些挑战开辟了新方向。量子强化学习（QRL）近年来备受关注，但当前量子硬件尚不足以应对复杂多智能体设置的高维环境。为此，我们提出一种分布式QRL框架，允许多智能体独立学习，将联合训练负载分配到独立机器上。该方法适用于动作与观测空间不相交的环境，也可通过合理近似扩展到其他系统。我们在合作乒乓球环境中验证了该方法，结果显示其相比其他分布式策略提升约10%，较经典策略表示模型提升约5%。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the computational challenges of traditional reinforcement learning in high-dimensional multi-agent environments and the limitations of current quantum hardware, this paper proposes MADQRL, a distributed quantum reinforcement learning framework. The method distributes the learning load across multiple agents that train independently, particularly suited for environments with disjoint action-observation spaces. Experimental results on a cooperative-pong environment show the framework achieves approximately a 10% improvement over other distribution strategies and a 5% improvement over classical policy representation models.
本文的动机源于传统强化学习在高维多智能体环境中面临的计算挑战以及当前量子硬件的局限性，为此提出了MADQRL，一个分布式量子强化学习框架。该方法通过让多个智能体独立学习来分担联合训练的计算负荷，尤其适用于动作-观测空间不相交的环境。在合作乒乓球环境上的实验结果表明，该框架相比其他分布式策略提升了约10%，相比经典策略表示模型提升了约5%。
Towards Near-Real-Time Telemetry-Aware Routing with Neural Routing Algorithms
Authors: Andreas Boltres, Niklas Freymuth, Benjamin Schichtholz, Michael König, Gerhard Neumann
First: 2026-04-03T09:51:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T07:28:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Routing algorithms are crucial for efficient computer network operations, and in many settings they must be able to react to traffic bursts within milliseconds. Live telemetry data can provide informative signals to routing algorithms, and recent work has trained neural networks to exploit such signals for traffic-aware routing. Yet, aggregating network-wide information is subject to communication delays, and existing neural approaches either assume unrealistic delay-free global states, or restrict routers to purely local telemetry. This leaves their deployability in real-world environments unclear. We cast telemetry-aware routing as a delay-aware closed-loop control problem and introduce a framework that trains and evaluates neural routing algorithms, while explicitly modeling communication and inference delays. On top of this framework, we propose LOGGIA, a scalable graph neural routing algorithm that predicts log-space link weights from attributed topology-and-telemetry graphs. It utilizes a data-driven pre-training stage, followed by on-policy Reinforcement Learning. Across synthetic and real network topologies, and unseen mixed TCP/UDP traffic sequences, LOGGIA consistently outperforms shortest-path baselines, whereas neural baselines fail once realistic delays are enforced. Our experiments further suggest that neural routing algorithms like LOGGIA perform best when deployed fully locally, i.e., observing network states and inferring actions at every router individually, as opposed to centralized decision making.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向近实时遥测感知路由的神经路由算法研究
路由算法对计算机网络的高效运行至关重要，在许多场景中必须能在毫秒级响应流量突发。实时遥测数据可为路由算法提供信息信号，近期研究已训练神经网络利用此类信号实现流量感知路由。然而，全网信息的聚合受通信延迟影响，现有神经方法要么假设不切实际的无延迟全局状态，要么将路由器限制为纯本地遥测，导致其在实际环境中的部署可行性不明。本文将遥测感知路由建模为延迟感知闭环控制问题，提出一个训练与评估神经路由算法的框架，并显式建模通信与推理延迟。基于此框架，我们提出LOGGIA——一种可扩展的图神经路由算法，通过属性化拓扑-遥测图预测对数空间链路权重。该算法采用数据驱动的预训练阶段，并结合同策略强化学习。在合成与真实网络拓扑及未见过的混合TCP/UDP流量序列测试中，LOGGIA持续优于最短路径基线，而神经基线在引入真实延迟后均失效。实验进一步表明，类似LOGGIA的神经路由算法在完全本地化部署（即各路由器独立观测网络状态并推断动作）时表现最优，而非集中式决策。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of making neural routing algorithms practical for real-world networks by explicitly accounting for communication and inference delays, which prior work often ignored. The authors frame telemetry-aware routing as a delay-aware closed-loop control problem and introduce a training and evaluation framework that models these delays. They propose LOGGIA, a scalable graph neural network algorithm that predicts log-space link weights from attributed topology-and-telemetry graphs, using data-driven pre-training followed by on-policy reinforcement learning. Experimental results on synthetic and real topologies with unseen mixed TCP/UDP traffic show that LOGGIA consistently outperforms shortest-path baselines under realistic delays, whereas other neural baselines fail; the study also finds that fully local deployment at each router yields better performance than centralized decision-making.
本文针对现有神经路由算法在现实网络中因忽略通信和推理延迟而难以部署的问题，提出了一种将遥测感知路由建模为延迟感知闭环控制问题的方法。作者引入了一个明确建模延迟的训练与评估框架，并在此基础上提出了LOGGIA算法，这是一种可扩展的图神经网络路由算法，它通过数据驱动的预训练和策略强化学习，从带属性的拓扑与遥测图中预测对数空间链路权重。在合成和真实网络拓扑以及未见过的混合TCP/UDP流量序列上的实验表明，在实施现实延迟条件下，LOGGIA持续优于最短路径基线，而其他神经基线则失效；研究还发现，在完全本地化部署（即每个路由器独立观察网络状态并推理动作）时，性能优于集中式决策。
Record-Remix-Replay: Hierarchical GPU Kernel Optimization using Evolutionary Search
Authors: Daniel Nichols, Konstantinos Parasyris, Caetano Melone, Tal Ben-Nun, Giorgis Georgakoudis, Harshitha Menon
First: 2026-04-13T07:25:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T07:25:12+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As high-performance computing and AI workloads become increasingly dependent on GPUs, maintaining high performance across rapidly evolving hardware generations has become a major challenge. Developers often spend months tuning scientific applications to fully exploit new architectures, navigating a complex optimization space that spans algorithm design, source implementation, compiler flags and pass sequences, and kernel launch parameters. Existing approaches can effectively search parts of this space in isolation, such as launch configurations or compiler settings, but optimizing across the full space still requires substantial human expertise and iterative manual effort. In this paper, we present Record-Remix-Replay (R^3), a hierarchical optimization framework that combines LLM-driven evolutionary search, Bayesian optimization, and record-replay compilation techniques to efficiently explore GPU kernel optimizations from source-level implementation choices down to compiler pass ordering and runtime configuration. By making candidate evaluation fast and scalable, our approach enables practical end-to-end search over optimization dimensions that are typically treated separately. We show that Record-Remix-Replay can optimize full scientific applications better than traditional approaches over kernel parameters and compiler flags, while also being nearly an order of magnitude faster than modern evolutionary search approaches.
中文标题/摘要
标题：记录-重构-重放：基于演化搜索的层次化GPU内核优化框架
随着高性能计算和AI工作负载日益依赖GPU，在快速迭代的硬件代际间保持高性能已成为重大挑战。开发者常需耗费数月调优科学应用以充分利用新架构，在涵盖算法设计、源码实现、编译器标志与过程序列、内核启动参数等复杂优化空间中进行探索。现有方法能有效孤立搜索部分空间（如启动配置或编译器设置），但跨全空间的优化仍需大量人工专业知识和迭代式手动调优。本文提出记录-重构-重放（R^3）层次化优化框架，结合LLM驱动的演化搜索、贝叶斯优化及记录-重放编译技术，从源码级实现选择到编译器过程排序与运行时配置，系统探索GPU内核优化。通过实现快速可扩展的候选方案评估，本方法支持对传统分离处理的优化维度进行端到端搜索。实验表明，记录-重构-重放相比传统内核参数与编译器标志优化方法能更有效优化完整科学应用，同时比现代演化搜索方法快近一个数量级。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is the significant challenge of maintaining high GPU performance across evolving hardware for HPC and AI workloads, which currently requires extensive manual tuning across a complex, multi-level optimization space. The method introduces Record-Remix-Replay (R^3), a hierarchical framework that employs evolutionary search driven by LLMs, Bayesian optimization, and record-replay compilation to efficiently explore optimizations from source code down to compiler and runtime configurations. The main experimental results demonstrate that R^3 optimizes full scientific applications more effectively than traditional approaches focusing on isolated parameters and is nearly ten times faster than modern evolutionary search methods.
本研究的动机在于，随着高性能计算和AI工作负载日益依赖GPU，在快速迭代的硬件上保持高性能成为重大挑战，现有方法通常需要大量人工对复杂的多层次优化空间进行调优。该方法提出了Record-Remix-Replay（R^3）这一分层优化框架，它结合了基于LLM的进化搜索、贝叶斯优化和记录-重放编译技术，能高效探索从源代码实现到编译器过程及运行时配置的GPU内核优化。主要实验结果表明，R^3相比传统仅优化部分参数的方法，能更好地优化完整科学应用，且速度比现代进化搜索方法快近一个数量级。
Tree Training: Accelerating Agentic LLMs Training via Shared Prefix Reuse
Authors: Jinghui Wang, Shaojie Wang, Yinghan Cui, Xuxing Chen, Chao Wang, Liang Huang, Xiaojiang Zhang, Junyi Peng, Li Wan, Haotian Zhang, Bin Chen
First: 2025-11-01T05:56:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T06:45:54+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Agentic large language model (LLM) training often involves multi-turn interaction trajectories that branch into multiple execution paths due to concurrent tool use, think-mode, sub-agent, context management and other runtime designs. As a result, the tokens produced by a single task naturally form a tree-structured token trajectory with shared prefixes, rather than a linear sequence. Existing training pipelines linearize such trajectories and treat each branch independently, leading to substantial redundant computation in both forward and backward passes. We derive that averaging the loss over all branches independently is algebraically identical to a per-token weighted loss, where each token's weight equals the fraction of branches passing through it. The problem therefore reduces to computing the log-probability of every token in the prefix tree exactly once, with no repeated computation across shared prefixes: we propose DFS serialization of the tree, which visits every token exactly once, and adapt full-attention and SSM layers to ensure the resulting log-probabilities match independent per-branch calculation exactly. In practice, a single trajectory tree can be too large to fit in GPU memory; we therefore propose Tree Partitioning, a memory-efficient partitioning strategy that splits the tree into subtrees each fitting within GPU memory while preserving high prefix reuse. Together, these contributions form Tree Training, an efficient framework for training LLMs on tree-structured trajectories, achieving up to 6.2x end-to-end training speedup on dense and MOE models for both supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：树形训练：通过共享前缀复用加速智能体大语言模型训练
智能体大语言模型（LLM）训练常涉及多轮交互轨迹，由于并发工具调用、思维模式、子智能体、上下文管理等运行时设计，这些轨迹会分叉为多条执行路径。因此，单个任务生成的词元自然形成具有共享前缀的树形结构轨迹，而非线性序列。现有训练流程将此类轨迹线性化并独立处理每个分支，导致前向与反向传播中存在大量冗余计算。我们推导出：对所有分支损失进行独立平均，在代数上等价于按词元加权损失，其中每个词元的权重等于通过该词元的分支比例。因此问题转化为精确计算前缀树中每个词元的对数概率一次，避免共享前缀的重复计算：我们提出树的深度优先搜索序列化方法，确保每个词元仅访问一次，并适配全注意力层与状态空间模型层，使生成的对数概率与独立分支计算完全匹配。实践中，单个轨迹树可能过大而无法载入GPU显存；因此我们提出树形分区策略，通过内存高效的分区方法将树拆分为适应GPU显存的子树，同时保持较高的前缀复用率。这些贡献共同构成树形训练框架，为树形结构轨迹的LLM训练提供高效解决方案，在监督微调与强化学习中，对稠密模型与混合专家模型实现了最高6.2倍的端到端训练加速。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the inefficiency of existing training pipelines that linearize the tree-structured token trajectories arising from agentic LLMs' multi-turn interactions, leading to redundant computations. The method introduces Tree Training, which employs DFS serialization to visit each token exactly once and adapts attention and SSM layers to compute log-probabilities without redundancy, along with Tree Partitioning to manage memory constraints by splitting large trees into subtrees. Experimental results demonstrate that this framework achieves up to 6.2x end-to-end training speedup on both dense and MOE models in supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning settings.
本文的动机在于现有训练流程将智能体大语言模型多轮交互产生的树状令牌轨迹线性化处理，导致大量冗余计算。方法上提出了树训练框架，采用深度优先序列化确保每个令牌仅被访问一次，并调整注意力与状态空间模型层以无冗余地计算对数概率，同时通过树分区策略将大树分割为适合GPU内存的子结构以保持前缀重用。实验结果表明，该框架在监督微调和强化学习中，对稠密与混合专家模型实现了高达6.2倍的端到端训练加速。
Rethinking Token-Level Credit Assignment in RLVR: A Polarity-Entropy Analysis
Authors: Yuhang He, Haodong Wu, Siyi Liu, Hongyu Ge, Hange Zhou, Keyi Wu, Zhuo Zheng, Qihong Lin, Zixin Zhong, Yongqi Zhang
First: 2026-04-13T06:32:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T06:32:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has substantially improved the reasoning ability of Large Language Models (LLMs). However, its sparse outcome-based rewards pose a fundamental credit assignment problem. We analyze this problem through the joint lens of reward polarity and token entropy. Our diagnostic tool, the Four Quadrant Decomposition, isolates token updates by polarity and entropy, and controlled ablations show that reasoning improvements concentrate in the high-entropy quadrants. To justify this observation theoretically, we adapt Conditional Mutual Information to the autoregressive RLVR setting and prove that the credit a token can carry is upper-bounded by its entropy. This view yields testable predictions that reasoning gains arise primarily from high-entropy tokens, with unique roles for positive and negative updates. A gradient analysis of GRPO further reveals how uniform reward broadcast dilutes signal at high-entropy positions while over-crediting deterministic tokens. Grounded in these insights, we propose Entropy-Aware Policy Optimization (EAPO) that modulates token-level learning signals accordingly. Extensive experiments demonstrate that EAPO outperforms strong baselines across two model families.
中文标题/摘要
标题：重新审视RLVR中的词元级信用分配：一种极性-熵分析框架
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）显著提升了大型语言模型（LLMs）的推理能力，但其基于稀疏结果的奖励机制引发了根本性的信用分配问题。本研究通过奖励极性与词元熵的双重视角分析该问题：诊断工具'四象限分解法'按极性与熵隔离词元更新，受控消融实验表明推理改进集中于高熵象限。为提供理论依据，我们将条件互信息适配至自回归RLVR场景，证明词元可承载的信用上限受其熵值约束。该视角推导出可验证的预测——推理增益主要源自高熵词元，且正负更新具有独特作用机制。对GRPO的梯度分析进一步揭示：均匀奖励播散会稀释高熵位点的信号，同时过度赋信确定性词元。基于这些发现，我们提出熵感知策略优化（EAPO），通过调节词元级学习信号实现精准优化。大量实验表明，EAPO在两类模型家族中均超越现有基线方法。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the credit assignment problem in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), where sparse outcome-based rewards make it difficult to attribute success to specific tokens. The authors analyze the issue through a framework of reward polarity and token entropy, using a Four Quadrant Decomposition to show that reasoning improvements are concentrated in high-entropy tokens, and they theoretically justify this by proving a token's credit capacity is bounded by its entropy. Their analysis of methods like GRPO reveals that uniform reward broadcasting is suboptimal, leading them to propose Entropy-Aware Policy Optimization (EAPO), which modulates learning signals based on token entropy, and experimental results demonstrate that EAPO outperforms strong baselines across multiple model families.
本文针对可验证奖励强化学习中的信用分配问题展开研究，该问题源于稀疏的结果奖励难以将成功归因于特定词元。作者通过奖励极性和词元熵的框架进行分析，利用四象限分解表明推理改进集中在高熵词元中，并从理论上证明词元的信用承载能力受其熵值上界约束。他们对GRPO等方法进行梯度分析，揭示了均匀奖励广播的不足，从而提出了熵感知策略优化方法，该方法根据词元熵调节学习信号，实验结果表明EAPO在多个模型系列上均优于现有基线方法。
GroupRank: A Groupwise Paradigm for Effective and Efficient Passage Reranking with LLMs
Authors: Meixiu Long, Duolin Sun, Dan Yang, Yihan Jiao, Lei Liu, Jiahai Wang, BinBin Hu, Yue Shen, Jie Feng, Zhehao Tan, Junjie Wang, Lianzhen Zhong, Jian Wang, Peng Wei, Jinjie Gu
Venue: ACL
First: 2025-11-10T15:25:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T06:26:15+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ACL-Findings 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) have emerged as powerful tools for passage reranking in information retrieval, leveraging their superior reasoning capabilities to address the limitations of conventional models on complex queries. However, current LLM-based reranking paradigms are fundamentally constrained by an efficiency-accuracy trade-off: (1) pointwise methods are efficient but ignore inter-document comparison, yielding suboptimal accuracy; (2) listwise methods capture global context but suffer from context-window constraints and prohibitive inference latency. To address these issues, we propose GroupRank, a novel paradigm that balances flexibility and context awareness. To unlock the full potential of groupwise reranking, we propose an answer-free data synthesis pipeline that fuses local pointwise signals with global listwise rankings. These samples facilitate supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning, with the latter guided by a specialized group-ranking reward comprising ranking-utility and group-alignment. These complementary components synergistically optimize document ordering and score calibration to reflect intrinsic query-document relevance. Experimental results show GroupRank achieves a state-of-the-art 65.2 NDCG@10 on BRIGHT and surpasses baselines by 2.1 points on R2MED, while delivering a 6.4$\times$ inference speedup.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GroupRank：基于分组范式的大语言模型高效段落重排序方法
大语言模型凭借其卓越的推理能力，已成为信息检索中段落重排序的强大工具，能够有效解决传统模型在复杂查询上的局限性。然而，当前基于大语言模型的重排序范式普遍受制于效率与精度的权衡困境：（1）逐点方法虽效率高，但忽略文档间比较，导致精度欠佳；（2）列表方法能捕捉全局上下文，却受限于上下文窗口约束和极高的推理延迟。为此，我们提出GroupRank这一兼顾灵活性与上下文感知能力的新范式。为充分发挥分组重排序的潜力，我们设计了一种无答案数据合成流程，将局部逐点信号与全局列表排序相融合。这些样本支持监督微调与强化学习，后者通过融合排序效用与分组对齐的专用组排序奖励进行指导。这两个互补组件协同优化文档排序与分数校准，以反映查询与文档的内在相关性。实验表明，GroupRank在BRIGHT数据集上达到65.2 NDCG@10的最新最优性能，在R2MED上超越基线2.1个点，同时实现6.4倍的推理加速。

The method introduces a groupwise paradigm that balances flexibility and context awareness, employing an answer-free data synthesis pipeline to combine pointwise signals with listwise rankings for supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning optimized via a group-ranking reward. Experimental results demonstrate state-of-the-art performance, achieving 65.2 NDCG@10 on BRIGHT and a 2.1-point improvement on R2MED, alongside a 6.4× inference speedup.
GroupRank的提出动机源于基于大语言模型的段落重排序中效率与准确性的权衡问题，即点式方法忽略文档间比较而列表式方法受限于上下文窗口和延迟。该方法采用一种平衡灵活性与上下文感知的组式范式，通过无答案数据合成流程融合点式信号与列表式排序，用于监督微调和强化学习，并利用包含排序效用和组对齐的组排序奖励进行优化。实验结果表明，该方法在BRIGHT数据集上取得了65.2 NDCG@10的最先进性能，在R2MED上超越基线2.1分，同时推理速度提升了6.4倍。
RTMC: Step-Level Credit Assignment via Rollout Trees
Authors: Tao Wang, Suhang Zheng, Xiaoxiao Xu
First: 2026-04-13T06:01:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T06:01:51+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-step agentic reinforcement learning benefits from fine-grained credit assignment, yet existing approaches offer limited options: critic-free methods like GRPO assign a uniform advantage to every action in a trajectory, while learned value networks introduce notable overhead and can be fragile under sparse rewards. We observe that group rollouts targeting the same problem often traverse overlapping intermediate states, implicitly forming a tree whose branches diverge at successive decision points. Building on this insight, we introduce Rollout-Tree Monte Carlo (RTMC) advantage estimation, which aggregates return statistics across rollouts sharing a common state to produce per-step Q-values and advantages--without any learned critic. A state-action signature system compresses raw interaction histories into compact, comparable representations, making cross-rollout state matching tractable. On SWE-bench Verified, RTMC improves pass@1 by 3.2 percentage points over GRPO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RTMC：基于展开树的步级信用分配方法
多步智能体强化学习受益于细粒度信用分配，但现有方法选择有限：无评论家方法（如GRPO）对轨迹中的每个动作分配统一优势值，而学习的价值网络则引入显著开销且在稀疏奖励下可能不稳定。我们观察到，针对同一问题的群体展开常经过重叠的中间状态，隐式形成一棵在连续决策点分叉的树。基于此，我们提出展开树蒙特卡洛（RTMC）优势估计方法，通过聚合共享同一状态的各展开的回报统计量，生成每步Q值与优势值——无需任何学习的评论家。状态-动作签名系统将原始交互历史压缩为紧凑可比较的表示，使跨展开状态匹配易于处理。在SWE-bench Verified基准上，RTMC较GRPO将pass@1指标提升了3.2个百分点。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the need for fine-grained credit assignment in multi-step reinforcement learning, where existing methods either assign uniform advantages across a trajectory or rely on fragile learned value networks. The proposed method, Rollout-Tree Monte Carlo (RTMC), leverages overlapping intermediate states across group rollouts to form a tree structure, using a state-action signature system to match states and aggregate return statistics without a learned critic, thereby estimating per-step Q-values and advantages. Experimental results on SWE-bench Verified show that RTMC improves pass@1 by 3.2 percentage points over GRPO.
本文的动机在于多步强化学习需要细粒度的信用分配，而现有方法要么在整个轨迹中分配均匀的优势值，要么依赖脆弱的学习价值网络。所提出的方法——Rollout-Tree Monte Carlo（RTMC）——利用组间rollout中重叠的中间状态形成树状结构，通过状态-动作签名系统匹配状态并聚合回报统计，无需学习评论家，从而估计每步的Q值和优势。在SWE-bench Verified上的实验结果表明，RTMC将pass@1比GRPO提高了3.2个百分点。
Optimal Stability of KL Divergence under Gaussian Perturbations
Authors: Jialu Pan, Yufeng Zhang, Nan Hu, Keqin Li
First: 2026-04-13T05:49:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T05:49:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study the problem of characterizing the stability of Kullback-Leibler (KL) divergence under Gaussian perturbations beyond Gaussian families. Existing relaxed triangle inequalities for KL divergence critically rely on the assumption that all involved distributions are Gaussian, which limits their applicability in modern applications such as out-of-distribution (OOD) detection with flow-based generative models. In this paper, we remove this restriction by establishing a sharp stability bound between an arbitrary distribution and Gaussian families under mild moment conditions. Specifically, let $P$ be a distribution with finite second moment, and let $\mathcal{N}_1$ and $\mathcal{N}_2$ be multivariate Gaussian distributions. We show that if $KL(P||\mathcal{N}_1)$ is large and $KL(\mathcal{N}_1||\mathcal{N}_2)$ is at most $ε$, then $KL(P||\mathcal{N}_2) \ge KL(P||\mathcal{N}_1) - O(\sqrtε)$. Moreover, we prove that this $\sqrtε$ rate is optimal in general, even within the Gaussian family. This result reveals an intrinsic stability property of KL divergence under Gaussian perturbations, extending classical Gaussian-only relaxed triangle inequalities to general distributions. The result is non-trivial due to the asymmetry of KL divergence and the absence of a triangle inequality in general probability spaces. As an application, we provide a rigorous foundation for KL-based OOD analysis in flow-based models, removing strong Gaussian assumptions used in prior work. More broadly, our result enables KL-based reasoning in non-Gaussian settings arising in deep learning and reinforcement learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：高斯扰动下KL散度的最优稳定性
本文研究了在高斯族之外，Kullback-Leibler（KL）散度在高斯扰动下的稳定性刻画问题。现有KL散度的松弛三角不等式严重依赖于所有涉及分布均为高斯的假设，这限制了其在基于流的生成模型进行分布外（OOD）检测等现代应用中的适用性。本文通过建立任意分布与高斯族之间在温和矩条件下的尖锐稳定性界，移除了这一限制。具体而言，设$P$为具有有限二阶矩的分布，$\mathcal{N}_1$和$\mathcal{N}_2$为多元高斯分布。我们证明，若$KL(P||\mathcal{N}_1)$较大且$KL(\mathcal{N}_1||\mathcal{N}_2)$至多为$ε$，则$KL(P||\mathcal{N}_2) \ge KL(P||\mathcal{N}_1) - O(\sqrtε)$。此外，我们证明即使在高斯族内，该$\sqrtε$速率在一般情况下也是最优的。这一结果揭示了KL散度在高斯扰动下的内在稳定性，将经典的仅适用于高斯的松弛三角不等式推广至一般分布。由于KL散度的非对称性及一般概率空间中三角不等式的缺失，该结果具有非平凡性。作为应用，我们为基于流的模型中基于KL的OOD分析提供了严格的理论基础，消除了先前工作中使用的强高斯假设。更广泛地，我们的结果使得在深度学习和强化学习中出现的非高斯场景下进行基于KL的推理成为可能。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the need to extend the stability analysis of Kullback-Leibler (KL) divergence beyond Gaussian distributions, as existing relaxed triangle inequalities are limited to Gaussian families, hindering applications like out-of-distribution detection in flow-based models. The method establishes a sharp stability bound under mild moment conditions, showing that for any distribution P with finite second moment and Gaussian distributions N1 and N2, if KL(P||N1) is large and KL(N1||N2) is at most ε, then KL(P||N2) is at least KL(P||N1) minus O(√ε). The main experimental results confirm that this √ε rate is optimal, even within Gaussian families, revealing an intrinsic stability property and providing a rigorous foundation for KL-based reasoning in non-Gaussian settings such as deep learning and reinforcement learning.
本文的动机在于需要将Kullback-Leibler（KL）散度的稳定性分析扩展到高斯分布之外，因为现有的松弛三角不等式仅限于高斯族，限制了其在基于流的生成模型中用于分布外检测等应用。方法是在温和矩条件下建立了一个尖锐的稳定性边界，表明对于任意具有有限二阶矩的分布P和高斯分布N1与N2，如果KL(P||N1)较大且KL(N1||N2)至多为ε，则KL(P||N2)至少为KL(P||N1)减去O(√ε)。主要实验结果证实了这一√ε速率是最优的，即使在高斯族内部也是如此，揭示了KL散度在高斯扰动下的内在稳定性，并为深度学习和强化学习等非高斯设置中的基于KL的推理提供了严格基础。
NimbusGuard: A Novel Framework for Proactive Kubernetes Autoscaling Using Deep Q-Networks
Authors: Chamath Wanigasooriya, Indrajith Ekanayake
First: 2026-04-13T05:32:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T05:32:12+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Cloud native architecture is about building and running scalable microservice applications to take full advantage of the cloud environments. Managed Kubernetes is the powerhouse orchestrating cloud native applications with elastic scaling. However, traditional Kubernetes autoscalers are reactive, meaning the scaling controllers adjust resources only after they detect demand within the cluster and do not incorporate any predictive measures. This can lead to either over-provisioning and increased costs or under-provisioning and performance degradation. We propose NimbusGuard, an open-source, Kubernetes-based autoscaling system that leverages a deep reinforcement learning agent to provide proactive autoscaling. The agents perception is augmented by a Long Short-Term Memory model that forecasts future workload patterns. The evaluations were conducted by comparing NimbusGuard against the built-in scaling controllers, such as Horizontal Pod Autoscaler, and the event-driven autoscaler KEDA. The experimental results demonstrate how NimbusGuard's proactive framework translates into superior performance and cost efficiency compared to existing reactive methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：NimbusGuard：一种基于深度Q网络的主动式Kubernetes自动扩缩容新框架
云原生架构旨在构建和运行可扩展的微服务应用，以充分利用云环境。托管Kubernetes作为云原生应用的编排引擎，具备弹性扩缩容能力。然而，传统Kubernetes自动扩缩容机制属于被动响应模式，即扩缩容控制器仅在检测到集群内需求后才调整资源，缺乏预测性措施，可能导致资源过度配置（成本增加）或配置不足（性能下降）。本文提出NimbusGuard——一个基于Kubernetes的开源自动扩缩容系统，通过深度强化学习智能体实现主动扩缩容。该系统采用长短期记忆模型预测未来工作负载模式以增强智能体感知能力。评估实验通过将NimbusGuard与内置扩缩容控制器（如水平Pod自动扩缩容器）及事件驱动扩缩容器KEDA进行对比，结果表明NimbusGuard的主动式框架在性能与成本效益方面均优于现有被动方法。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of reactive autoscalers in Kubernetes, which can cause resource over-provisioning or under-provisioning, this paper introduces NimbusGuard, a proactive autoscaling framework. The method employs a deep reinforcement learning agent, specifically a Deep Q-Network, enhanced with a Long Short-Term Memory model to predict future workload patterns and preemptively adjust resources. Experimental comparisons against standard controllers like Horizontal Pod Autoscaler and KEDA show that NimbusGuard achieves better performance and cost efficiency by anticipating demand rather than reacting to it.
针对Kubernetes中反应式自动扩缩容机制易导致资源过度配置或不足的问题，本文提出了NimbusGuard这一主动式自动扩缩容框架。该方法采用深度强化学习智能体，结合长短期记忆模型预测未来工作负载模式，从而预先调整资源。通过与Horizontal Pod Autoscaler和KEDA等内置控制器的实验对比，结果表明NimbusGuard通过预测需求而非被动响应，实现了更优的性能和成本效益。
When Valid Signals Fail: Regime Boundaries Between LLM Features and RL Trading Policies
Authors: Zhengzhe Yang
First: 2026-04-13T04:53:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T04:53:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Can large language models (LLMs) generate continuous numerical features that improve reinforcement learning (RL) trading agents? We build a modular pipeline where a frozen LLM serves as a stateless feature extractor, transforming unstructured daily news and filings into a fixed-dimensional vector consumed by a downstream PPO agent. We introduce an automated prompt-optimization loop that treats the extraction prompt as a discrete hyperparameter and tunes it directly against the Information Coefficient - the Spearman rank correlation between predicted and realized returns - rather than NLP losses. The optimized prompt discovers genuinely predictive features (IC above 0.15 on held-out data). However, these valid intermediate representations do not automatically translate into downstream task performance: during a distribution shift caused by a macroeconomic shock, LLM-derived features add noise, and the augmented agent under-performs a price-only baseline. In a calmer test regime the agent recovers, yet macroeconomic state variables remain the most robust driver of policy improvement. Our findings highlight a gap between feature-level validity and policy-level robustness that parallels known challenges in transfer learning under distribution shift.
中文标题/摘要
标题：当有效信号失效时：大语言模型特征与强化学习交易策略的机制边界
大语言模型（LLMs）能否生成可提升强化学习（RL）交易代理性能的连续数值特征？我们构建了一个模块化流程：冻结的LLM作为无状态特征提取器，将非结构化的每日新闻和文件转化为固定维度的向量，供下游PPO代理使用。我们引入了自动化提示优化循环，将提取提示视为离散超参数，并直接针对信息系数（预测收益与实际收益之间的斯皮尔曼等级相关系数）而非NLP损失进行优化。优化后的提示发现了真正具有预测性的特征（在保留数据上IC超过0.15）。然而，这些有效的中间表征并未自动转化为下游任务性能：在宏观经济冲击导致的分布偏移期间，LLM衍生的特征引入了噪声，增强型代理的表现不及仅使用价格数据的基线。在更平稳的测试机制中代理表现恢复，但宏观经济状态变量仍是策略改进最稳健的驱动因素。我们的研究结果凸显了特征层面有效性与策略层面鲁棒性之间的差距，这与分布偏移下迁移学习的已知挑战相呼应。
Summary / 总结
This study investigates whether large language models (LLMs) can generate continuous numerical features from unstructured financial text to enhance reinforcement learning (RL) trading agents. The method employs a modular pipeline where a frozen LLM acts as a stateless feature extractor, processing daily news and filings into fixed-dimensional vectors for a downstream PPO agent, and introduces an automated prompt-optimization loop that tunes the extraction prompt directly against the Information Coefficient (IC) metric. Experimental results show the optimized prompt yields predictive features with an IC above 0.15 on held-out data, but during a macroeconomic shock-induced distribution shift, these LLM-derived features introduce noise, causing the augmented agent to underperform a price-only baseline; in calmer regimes, the agent recovers, though macroeconomic state variables prove more robust for policy improvement, highlighting a gap between feature validity and policy robustness under distribution shift.
本研究探讨大型语言模型（LLM）能否从非结构化金融文本中生成连续数值特征以增强强化学习（RL）交易智能体。方法采用模块化流程，其中冻结的LLM作为无状态特征提取器，将每日新闻和文件处理为固定维度向量供下游PPO智能体使用，并引入自动化提示优化循环，直接针对信息系数（IC）指标调整提取提示。实验结果表明，优化后的提示在保留数据上产生了IC高于0.15的预测性特征，但在宏观经济冲击导致的分布偏移期间，这些LLM衍生特征引入了噪声，使得增强智能体表现不及仅使用价格数据的基线；在平稳测试环境中，智能体性能恢复，但宏观经济状态变量仍是策略改进最稳健的驱动因素，凸显了分布偏移下特征有效性与策略鲁棒性之间的差距。
Robust Adversarial Policy Optimization Under Dynamics Uncertainty
Authors: Mintae Kim, Koushil Sreenath
First: 2026-04-13T04:23:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T04:23:54+00:00
Comments: 33 pages, 8 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) policies often fail under dynamics that differ from training, a gap not fully addressed by domain randomization or existing adversarial RL methods. Distributionally robust RL provides a formal remedy but still relies on surrogate adversaries to approximate intractable primal problems, leaving blind spots that potentially cause instability and over-conservatism. We propose a dual formulation that directly exposes the robustness-performance trade-off. At the trajectory level, a temperature parameter from the dual problem is approximated with an adversarial network, yielding efficient and stable worst-case rollouts within a divergence bound. At the model level, we employ Boltzmann reweighting over dynamics ensembles, focusing on more adverse environments to the current policy rather than uniform sampling. The two components act independently and complement each other: trajectory-level steering ensures robust rollouts, while model-level sampling provides policy-sensitive coverage of adverse dynamics. The resulting framework, robust adversarial policy optimization (RAPO) outperforms robust RL baselines, improving resilience to uncertainty and generalization to out-of-distribution dynamics while maintaining dual tractability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：动态不确定性下的鲁棒对抗策略优化
强化学习策略常在训练环境之外的动态系统中失效，领域随机化或现有对抗性强化学习方法未能完全解决此问题。分布鲁棒强化学习提供了形式化解决方案，但仍依赖代理对抗器逼近难解的原问题，存在可能导致不稳定和过度保守的盲区。我们提出一种对偶形式，直接揭示鲁棒性与性能的权衡关系。在轨迹层面，通过对抗网络逼近对偶问题中的温度参数，在散度界内实现高效稳定的最坏情况推演。在模型层面，采用玻尔兹曼重加权方法处理动态集成，聚焦于对当前策略更不利的环境而非均匀采样。两个组件独立运作且相互补充：轨迹级引导确保鲁棒推演，模型级采样提供对策略敏感的对抗动态覆盖。所提出的鲁棒对抗策略优化框架在鲁棒强化学习基线方法中表现优异，在保持对偶可解性的同时，提升了对不确定性的适应能力及对分布外动态的泛化性能。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the vulnerability of reinforcement learning policies to dynamics shifts not fully mitigated by existing robust RL methods, which often rely on surrogate adversaries leading to instability or over-conservatism. The proposed method, robust adversarial policy optimization (RAPO), introduces a dual formulation to directly manage the robustness-performance trade-off: at the trajectory level, an adversarial network approximates a temperature parameter for efficient worst-case rollouts within a divergence bound, while at the model level, Boltzmann reweighting over dynamics ensembles prioritizes sampling more adverse environments relevant to the current policy. Experimental results demonstrate that RAPO outperforms robust RL baselines, enhancing resilience to uncertainty and generalization to out-of-distribution dynamics while maintaining computational tractability.
该论文针对强化学习策略在动态变化下易失效的问题，现有鲁棒强化学习方法常依赖代理对抗者，可能导致不稳定或过度保守。提出的鲁棒对抗策略优化（RAPO）方法采用对偶公式直接处理鲁棒性与性能的权衡：在轨迹层面，通过对抗网络近似温度参数以在发散边界内生成高效的最坏情况推演；在模型层面，利用玻尔兹曼重加权在动态集成中优先采样对当前策略更不利的环境。实验结果表明，RAPO优于鲁棒强化学习基线，提升了对抗不确定性的鲁棒性和对分布外动态的泛化能力，同时保持了计算可行性。
MMR-AD: A Large-Scale Multimodal Dataset for Benchmarking General Anomaly Detection with Multimodal Large Language Models
Authors: Xincheng Yao, Zefeng Qian, Chao Shi, Jiayang Song, Chongyang Zhang
First: 2026-04-13T04:14:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T04:14:56+00:00
Comments: Accepted by CVPR2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In the progress of industrial anomaly detection, general anomaly detection (GAD) is an emerging trend and also the ultimate goal. Unlike the conventional single- and multi-class AD, general AD aims to train a general AD model that can directly detect anomalies in diverse novel classes without any retraining or fine-tuning on the target data. Recently, Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have shown great promise in achieving general anomaly detection due to their revolutionary visual understanding and language reasoning capabilities. However, MLLM's general AD ability remains underexplored due to: (1) MLLMs are pretrained on amounts of data sourced from the Web, these data still have significant gaps with the data in AD scenarios. Moreover, the image-text pairs during pretraining are also not specifically for AD tasks. (2) The current mainstream AD datasets are image-based and not yet suitable for post-training MLLMs. To facilitate MLLM-based general AD research, we present MMR-AD, which is a comprehensive benchmark for both training and evaluating MLLM-based AD models. With MMR-AD, we reveal that the AD performance of current SOTA generalist MLLMs still falls far behind the industrial requirements. Based on MMR-AD, we also propose a baseline model, Anomaly-R1, which is a reasoning-based AD model that learns from the CoT data in MMR-AD and is further enhanced by reinforcement learning. Extensive experiments show that our Anomaly-R1 achieves remarkable improvements over generalist MLLMs in both anomaly detection and localization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MMR-AD：基于多模态大语言模型的通用异常检测大规模多模态基准数据集
在工业异常检测的发展进程中，通用异常检测（GAD）作为新兴趋势和终极目标，与传统单类别/多类别异常检测不同，其旨在训练无需目标数据重训练或微调即可直接检测多类新异常的通用模型。近期，多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）凭借革命性的视觉理解与语言推理能力，在实现通用异常检测方面展现出巨大潜力。然而，MLLMs的通用异常检测能力仍待深入探索，原因在于：（1）MLLMs基于海量网络数据预训练，与异常检测场景数据存在显著差异，且预训练的图文对未针对异常检测任务优化；（2）当前主流异常检测数据集为图像格式，不适用于MLLMs的后训练。为推进基于MLLM的通用异常检测研究，本文提出综合性基准数据集MMR-AD，用于训练与评估MLLM异常检测模型。通过该数据集研究发现，当前先进通用MLLMs的异常检测性能仍远未达到工业需求。基于MMR-AD，我们进一步提出基线模型Anomaly-R1——一种基于推理的异常检测模型，通过MMR-AD中的思维链数据学习，并采用强化学习增强。大量实验表明，Anomaly-R1在异常检测与定位任务上均显著优于通用MLLMs。

The paper introduces MMR-AD, a large-scale multimodal dataset designed to benchmark general anomaly detection (GAD) using multimodal large language models (MLLMs), motivated by the need to address the gap between MLLMs' web-based pretraining data and industrial anomaly detection scenarios, as current datasets are unsuitable for post-training MLLMs. The method involves creating MMR-AD to train and evaluate MLLM-based AD models, and proposing a baseline model, Anomaly-R1, which uses reasoning from chain-of-thought data and reinforcement learning enhancement. Experimental results show that current state-of-the-art generalist MLLMs underperform relative to industrial requirements, while Anomaly-R1 achieves significant improvements in both anomaly detection and localization over these MLLMs.
本文提出了MMR-AD，一个用于基于多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）的通用异常检测（GAD）基准的大规模多模态数据集，其动机在于解决MLLMs基于网络的预训练数据与工业异常检测场景之间的差距，因为现有数据集不适合MLLMs的后训练。方法包括创建MMR-AD来训练和评估基于MLLMs的异常检测模型，并提出了一个基线模型Anomaly-R1，该模型利用思维链数据进行推理并通过强化学习增强。实验结果表明，当前最先进的通用MLLMs在性能上远未达到工业要求，而Anomaly-R1在异常检测和定位方面相比这些MLLMs取得了显著提升。
You Only Judge Once: Multi-response Reward Modeling in a Single Forward Pass
Authors: Yinuo Yang, Zixian Ma, Manasi Ganti, Jieyu Zhang, Ranjay Krishna
First: 2026-04-13T04:02:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T04:02:03+00:00
Comments: 9 pages, 4 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present a discriminative multimodal reward model that scores all candidate responses in a single forward pass. Conventional discriminative reward models evaluate each response independently, requiring multiple forward passes, one for each potential response. Our approach concatenates multiple responses with separator tokens and applies cross-entropy over their scalar scores, enabling direct comparative reasoning and efficient $N$-way preference learning. The multi-response design also yields up to $N\times$ wall-clock speedup and FLOPs reduction over conventional single-response scoring. To enable $N$-way reward evaluation beyond existing pairwise benchmarks, we construct two new benchmarks: (1) MR$^2$Bench-Image contains human-annotated rankings over responses from 8 diverse models; (2) MR$^2$Bench-Video is a large-scale video-based reward benchmark derived from 94K crowdsourced pairwise human judgments over video question-answering spanning 19 models, denoised via preference graph ensemble. Both benchmarks provide 4-response evaluation variants sampled from the full rankings. Built on a 4B vision-language backbone with LoRA fine-tuning and a lightweight MLP value head, our model achieves state-of-the-art results on six multimodal reward benchmarks, including MR$^2$Bench-Image, MR$^2$Bench-Video, and four other existing benchmarks. Our model outperforms existing larger generative and discriminative reward models. We further demonstrate that our reward model, when used in reinforcement learning with GRPO, produces improved policy models that maintain performance across standard multimodal benchmarks while substantially improving open-ended generation quality, outperforming a single-response discriminative reward model (RM) baseline by a large margin in both training stability and open-ended generation quality.
中文标题/摘要
标题：单次判定：单次前向传播中的多响应奖励建模
我们提出了一种判别式多模态奖励模型，可在单次前向传播中为所有候选响应评分。传统的判别式奖励模型需独立评估每个响应，需多次前向传播（每个潜在响应一次）。我们的方法通过分隔符将多个响应拼接，并在其标量分数上应用交叉熵，实现了直接比较推理和高效的N路偏好学习。多响应设计相比传统单响应评分，可获得高达N倍的实时加速和FLOPs降低。为超越现有成对基准实现N路奖励评估，我们构建了两个新基准：（1）MR²Bench-Image包含对8个不同模型响应的人工标注排序；（2）MR²Bench-Video是基于视频的大规模奖励基准，源自94K个众包视频问答人类成对判断（涵盖19个模型），通过偏好图集成去噪。两个基准均提供从完整排序中采样的4响应评估变体。基于4B视觉语言骨干网络（采用LoRA微调和轻量级MLP值头），我们的模型在六个多模态奖励基准（包括MR²Bench-Image、MR²Bench-Video和四个现有基准）上取得最先进成果，性能优于现有更大的生成式和判别式奖励模型。我们进一步证明，当该奖励模型与GRPO结合用于强化学习时，可生成改进的策略模型：在保持标准多模态基准性能的同时，显著提升开放式生成质量，在训练稳定性和开放式生成质量上均大幅超越单响应判别式奖励模型基线。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the inefficiency of conventional discriminative reward models that require multiple forward passes to score candidate responses independently, this paper introduces a multi-response reward model that scores all responses in a single forward pass. The method concatenates multiple responses with separator tokens and applies cross-entropy over their scalar scores, enabling direct comparative reasoning and efficient N-way preference learning, which yields up to N× speedup and FLOPs reduction. To evaluate N-way rewards, the authors construct two new benchmarks—MR²Bench-Image with human-annotated rankings over 8 models and MR²Bench-Video derived from 94K crowdsourced judgments over 19 video QA models—and achieve state-of-the-art results on six multimodal benchmarks using a 4B vision-language backbone with LoRA fine-tuning. Experimental results show the model outperforms larger generative and discriminative baselines, and when used in reinforcement learning with GRPO, it improves policy models' training stability and open-ended generation quality substantially over single-response reward models.
本文针对传统判别式奖励模型需多次前向传播独立评分候选响应的低效问题，提出了一种多响应奖励模型，可在单次前向传播中同时评估所有响应。该方法通过分隔符拼接多个响应，并对其标量分数应用交叉熵，实现了直接比较推理和高效的N路偏好学习，从而获得高达N倍的加速和计算量减少。为支持N路奖励评估，作者构建了两个新基准：MR²Bench-Image包含对8个模型响应的人工标注排序，MR²Bench-Video基于94K众包对19个视频问答模型的配对判断构建；模型基于4B视觉语言主干网络，结合LoRA微调和轻量MLP值头，在六个多模态奖励基准上取得了最先进的结果。实验表明，该模型优于更大的生成式和判别式基线，且当与GRPO结合用于强化学习时，能显著提升策略模型的训练稳定性和开放式生成质量，大幅超越单响应奖励模型基线。
On the Use of Bi-Objective Evolutionary Algorithms for the Stochastic MKP under Dynamic Constraints
Authors: Ishara Hewa Pathiranage, Aneta Neumann
First: 2026-04-13T02:59:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T02:59:03+00:00
Comments: Accepted to publish in Genetic and Evolutionary Computation Conference (GECCO '26)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The multiple knapsack problem (MKP) generalizes the classical knapsack problem by assigning items to multiple knapsacks subject to capacity constraints. It is used to model many real-world resource allocation and scheduling problems. In practice, these optimization problems often involve stochastic and dynamic components. Evolutionary algorithms provide a flexible framework for addressing such problems under uncertainty and dynamic changes. In this paper, we investigate a stochastic and dynamic variant of MKP with chance constraints, where the item weights are modeled as independent normally distributed random variables and knapsack capacities change during the optimization process. We formulate the problem as a bi-objective optimization formulation that balances profit maximization and probabilistic capacity satisfaction at a given confidence level. We conduct an empirical comparison of four widely used multi-objective evolutionary algorithms (MOEAs), representing both decomposition- and dominance-based search paradigms. The algorithms are evaluated under varying uncertainty levels, confidence thresholds, and dynamic change settings. The results provide comparative insights into the behavior of decomposition-based and dominance-based MOEAs for stochastic MKP under dynamic constraints.
中文标题/摘要
标题：动态约束下随机多背包问题的双目标进化算法应用研究
多背包问题（MKP）通过将物品分配给多个受容量约束的背包，推广了经典背包问题，常用于建模现实世界的资源分配与调度问题。实践中这类优化问题常包含随机性与动态性。进化算法为处理不确定性和动态变化提供了灵活框架。本文研究具有机会约束的随机动态MKP变体，其中物品权重建模为独立正态分布随机变量，背包容量在优化过程中动态变化。我们将问题构建为双目标优化模型，在给定置信水平下平衡利润最大化与概率容量满足度。对四种广泛使用的多目标进化算法（MOEA）进行实证比较，涵盖基于分解和基于支配的搜索范式。在不同不确定性水平、置信阈值和动态变化场景下评估算法性能，结果为动态约束下随机MKP问题中两类MOEA的行为特征提供了对比性见解。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to address real-world resource allocation problems that involve uncertainty and dynamic changes, this paper investigates a stochastic and dynamic variant of the multiple knapsack problem (MKP) with chance constraints, where item weights are random variables and capacities change over time. The method formulates the problem as a bi-objective optimization balancing profit maximization and probabilistic capacity satisfaction, and empirically compares four multi-objective evolutionary algorithms (MOEAs) from decomposition- and dominance-based paradigms. Experimental results under varying uncertainty levels, confidence thresholds, and dynamic settings provide comparative insights into the behavior of these MOEAs for the stochastic MKP under dynamic constraints.
本文针对现实世界中涉及不确定性和动态变化的资源分配问题，研究了具有机会约束的随机动态多背包问题变体，其中物品权重为随机变量且背包容量随时间变化。方法将该问题表述为平衡利润最大化和概率容量满足的双目标优化，并实证比较了四种基于分解和支配的多目标进化算法。在不同不确定性水平、置信阈值和动态设置下的实验结果为这些算法在动态约束下的随机多背包问题中的行为提供了比较性见解。
Controlling Multimodal Conversational Agents with Coverage-Enhanced Latent Actions
Authors: Yongqi Li, Hao Lang, Tieyun Qian, Yongbin Li
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-01-12T13:13:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T02:40:35+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ACL 2026 (Main), camera-ready version
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Vision-language models are increasingly employed as multimodal conversational agents (MCAs) for diverse conversational tasks. Recently, reinforcement learning (RL) has been widely explored for adapting MCAs to various human-AI interaction scenarios. Despite showing great enhancement in generalization performance, fine-tuning MCAs via RL still faces challenges in handling the extremely large text token space. To address this, we learn a compact latent action space for RL fine-tuning instead. Specifically, we adopt the learning from observation mechanism to construct the codebook for the latent action space, where future observations are leveraged to estimate current latent actions that could further be used to reconstruct future observations. However, the scarcity of paired image-text data hinders learning a codebook with sufficient coverage. Thus, we leverage both paired image-text data and text-only data to construct the latent action space, using a cross-modal projector for transforming text embeddings into image-text embeddings. We initialize the cross-modal projector on paired image-text data, and further train it on massive text-only data with a novel cycle consistency loss to enhance its robustness. We show that our latent action based method outperforms competitive baselines on two conversation tasks across various RL algorithms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于覆盖增强隐式动作的多模态对话智能体控制
视觉语言模型正日益作为多模态对话智能体应用于多样化对话任务。近期，强化学习被广泛探索用于使多模态对话智能体适应不同的人机交互场景。尽管在泛化性能上展现出显著提升，但通过强化学习微调多模态对话智能体仍面临处理极大文本标记空间的挑战。为此，我们转而学习紧凑的隐式动作空间进行强化学习微调。具体而言，采用观察学习机制构建隐式动作空间的码本，利用未来观测估计当前隐式动作，该动作可进一步用于重建未来观测。然而，配对图文数据的稀缺性阻碍了学习具有充分覆盖度的码本。因此，我们同时利用配对图文数据与纯文本数据构建隐式动作空间，通过跨模态投影器将文本嵌入转换为图文嵌入。我们在配对图文数据上初始化跨模态投影器，并基于新型循环一致性损失在大量纯文本数据上进一步训练以增强其鲁棒性。实验表明，基于隐式动作的方法在两种对话任务上均优于多种强化学习算法的基线模型。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the challenge of fine-tuning multimodal conversational agents (MCAs) via reinforcement learning (RL), which struggles with the large text token space. The method involves learning a compact latent action space for RL, using a learning-from-observation mechanism to construct a codebook; to enhance coverage, it leverages both paired image-text and text-only data via a cross-modal projector trained with cycle consistency loss. The main experimental results show that this latent action-based approach outperforms competitive baselines on two conversation tasks across various RL algorithms.
本研究的动机是解决通过强化学习微调多模态对话代理时面临的大规模文本标记空间挑战。方法上，通过学习一个紧凑的潜在动作空间用于强化学习，利用观察学习机制构建码本；为提升覆盖范围，该方法结合配对图像-文本数据和纯文本数据，通过带有循环一致性损失训练的跨模态投影器增强鲁棒性。主要实验结果表明，这种基于潜在动作的方法在多种强化学习算法下，于两个对话任务上均优于竞争基线。
Physics-guided surrogate learning enables zero-shot control of turbulent wings
Authors: Yuning Wang, Pol Suarez, Mathis Bode, Ricardo Vinuesa
First: 2026-04-10T15:50:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T02:40:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Turbulent boundary layers over aerodynamic surfaces are a major source of aircraft drag, yet their control remains challenging due to multiscale dynamics and spatial variability, particularly under adverse pressure gradients. Reinforcement learning has outperformed state-of-the-art strategies in canonical flows, but its application to realistic geometries is limited by computational cost and transferability. Here we show that these limitations can be overcome by exploiting local structures of wall-bounded turbulence. Policies are trained in turbulent channel flows matched to wing boundary-layer statistics and deployed directly onto a NACA4412 wing at $Re_c=2\times10^5$ without further training, being the so-called zero-shot control. This achieves a 28.7% reduction in skin-friction drag and a 10.7% reduction in total drag, outperforming the state-of-the-art opposition control by 40% in friction drag reduction and 5% in total drag. Training cost is reduced by four orders of magnitude relative to on-wing training, enabling scalable flow control.
中文标题/摘要
标题：物理引导的代理学习实现湍流机翼的零样本控制
空气动力学表面的湍流边界层是飞机阻力的主要来源，但由于多尺度动力学和空间变异性（尤其在逆压梯度条件下），其控制仍具挑战性。强化学习在典型流动中已超越先进策略，但其在真实几何结构中的应用受限于计算成本与可迁移性。本研究通过利用壁面湍流的局部结构克服了这些限制：在匹配机翼边界层统计特性的湍流通道中训练控制策略，并直接部署于NACA4412翼型（$Re_c=2\times10^5$），无需额外训练，即实现所谓零样本控制。该方法使表面摩擦阻力降低28.7%，总阻力降低10.7%，在摩擦阻力削减上超越先进反向控制策略40%，总阻力削减提升5%。相较于机翼直接训练，计算成本降低四个数量级，为实现可扩展流动控制提供了可能。
Summary / 总结
The study addresses the challenge of controlling turbulent boundary layers on aerodynamic surfaces, which are a major source of aircraft drag, by overcoming the computational cost and transferability limitations of reinforcement learning in realistic geometries. The method exploits local structures of wall-bounded turbulence, training control policies in turbulent channel flows matched to wing boundary-layer statistics and deploying them directly onto a NACA4412 wing without further training, achieving zero-shot control. Experimental results show a 28.7% reduction in skin-friction drag and a 10.7% reduction in total drag, outperforming state-of-the-art opposition control by 40% in friction drag reduction and 5% in total drag, while reducing training cost by four orders of magnitude compared to on-wing training.
该研究针对空气动力学表面湍流边界层控制这一挑战，旨在克服强化学习在真实几何结构中应用的计算成本和可迁移性限制。方法利用壁面湍流的局部结构，在匹配机翼边界层统计特性的湍流通道流中训练控制策略，并直接部署到NACA4412机翼上实现零样本控制。实验结果表明，皮肤摩擦阻力降低了28.7%，总阻力降低了10.7%，在摩擦阻力减少上比最先进的对立控制方法提升40%，总阻力减少提升5%，同时训练成本相比机翼上训练降低了四个数量级。
CSPO: Alleviating Reward Ambiguity for Structured Table-to-LaTeX Generation
Authors: Yunfan Yang, Cuiling Lan, Jitao Sang, Yan Lu
First: 2026-04-13T02:34:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T02:34:30+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ACL2026 (main conference)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Tables contain rich structured information, yet when stored as images their contents remain "locked" within pixels. Converting table images into LaTeX code enables faithful digitization and reuse, but current multimodal large language models (MLLMs) often fail to preserve structural, style, or content fidelity. Conventional post-training with reinforcement learning (RL) typically relies on a single aggregated reward, leading to reward ambiguity that conflates multiple behavioral aspects and hinders effective optimization. We propose Component-Specific Policy Optimization (CSPO), an RL framework that disentangles optimization across LaTeX tables components-structure, style, and content. In particular, CSPO assigns component-specific rewards and backpropagates each signal only through the tokens relevant to its component, alleviating reward ambiguity and enabling targeted component-wise optimization. To comprehensively assess performance, we introduce a set of hierarchical evaluation metrics. Extensive experiments demonstrate the effectiveness of CSPO, underscoring the importance of component-specific optimization for reliable structured generation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CSPO：缓解结构化表格到LaTeX生成的奖励模糊性问题
表格蕴含丰富的结构化信息，但以图像形式存储时其内容仍被“锁定”在像素中。将表格图像转换为LaTeX代码可实现精确数字化与复用，但当前多模态大语言模型常难以保持结构、样式或内容的保真度。传统的强化学习后训练通常依赖单一聚合奖励，导致奖励模糊性——将多个行为维度混为一谈，阻碍有效优化。我们提出组件特定策略优化框架，该强化学习框架将优化过程解耦至LaTeX表格的三大组件：结构、样式与内容。具体而言，CSPO为各组件分配特定奖励，并仅通过与其相关的词元反向传播对应信号，从而缓解奖励模糊性，实现精准的组件级优化。为全面评估性能，我们引入一套分层评估指标。大量实验验证了CSPO的有效性，凸显了组件特定优化对可靠结构化生成的重要性。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is that converting table images to LaTeX code is crucial for digitization, but current multimodal LLMs often fail to preserve structural, style, and content fidelity, with conventional RL training suffering from reward ambiguity that conflates these aspects. The proposed method, Component-Specific Policy Optimization (CSPO), is an RL framework that disentangles optimization by assigning component-specific rewards and backpropagating each signal only through tokens relevant to structure, style, or content. Main experimental results, evaluated using a new set of hierarchical metrics, demonstrate CSPO's effectiveness in improving generation fidelity, underscoring the importance of targeted component-wise optimization for reliable structured table-to-LaTeX generation.
本研究的动机在于，将表格图像转换为LaTeX代码对于数字化至关重要，但当前的多模态大语言模型往往无法保持结构、样式和内容的保真度，且传统的强化学习训练存在奖励模糊性问题，混淆了这些不同方面。所提出的方法——组件特定策略优化（CSPO），是一个强化学习框架，它通过分配针对结构、样式和内容的特定奖励，并仅将每个信号反向传播至相关标记，从而解耦优化过程。主要实验结果表明，使用一套新的分层评估指标进行评估，CSPO能有效提高生成保真度，强调了针对特定组件进行优化对于可靠的结构化表格到LaTeX生成的重要性。
Understanding Generalization in Role-Playing Models via Information Theory
Authors: Yongqi Li, Hao Lang, Fei Huang, Tieyun Qian, Yongbin Li
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2025-12-19T06:37:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T02:34:09+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ACL 2026 (Findings), camera-ready version
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Role-playing models (RPMs) are widely used in real-world applications but underperform when deployed in the wild. This degradation can be attributed to distribution shifts, including user, character, and dialogue compositional shifts. Existing methods like LLM-as-a-judge fall short in providing a fine-grained diagnosis of how these shifts affect RPM generalization, and thus there lack formal frameworks to characterize RPM generalization behaviors. To bridge these gaps, we introduce an information-theoretic metric, named reasoning-based effective mutual information difference (R-EMID), to measure RPM performance degradation in an interpretable way. We also derive an upper bound on R-EMID to predict the worst-case generalization performance of RPMs and theoretically reveal how various shifts contribute to the RPM performance degradation. Moreover, we propose a co-evolving reinforcement learning framework to adaptively model the connection among user, character, and dialogue context and thus enhance the estimation of dialogue response generation probability, which is critical for calculating R-EMID. Finally, we evaluate the generalization performance of various RPMs using R-EMID, finding that user shift poses the highest risk among all shifts and reinforcement learning is the most effective approach for enhancing RPM generalization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于信息论的角色扮演模型泛化能力解析
角色扮演模型在实际应用中广泛使用，但在真实场景部署时性能下降。这种退化可归因于用户、角色和对话构成等多维度的分布偏移。现有方法（如LLM-as-a-judge）难以精细诊断这些偏移如何影响模型泛化，也缺乏形式化框架来刻画其泛化行为。为填补这些空白，本文提出一种基于信息论的度量指标——推理有效互信息差，以可解释的方式量化角色扮演模型的性能衰减。我们推导了该指标的上界以预测最差泛化性能，并从理论上揭示各类偏移对模型退化的贡献机制。进一步提出协同演化强化学习框架，自适应建模用户、角色与对话语境间的关联，从而提升对话响应生成概率的估计精度（这对计算该指标至关重要）。最终通过该指标评估多种角色扮演模型的泛化性能，发现用户偏移在所有偏移中风险最高，而强化学习是提升模型泛化最有效的途径。

It introduces an information-theoretic metric called reasoning-based effective mutual information difference (R-EMID) to interpretably measure RPM generalization, derives an upper bound to predict worst-case performance, and proposes a co-evolving reinforcement learning framework to improve response probability estimation. Experimental results show that user shift poses the highest risk to RPMs and reinforcement learning is the most effective method for enhancing generalization.

EvoNash-MARL: A Closed-Loop Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning Framework for Medium-Horizon Equity Allocation
Authors: Chongliu Jia, Yi Luo, Sipeng Han, Pengwei Li, Jie Ding, Youshuang Hu, Yimiao Qian, Qiya Wang
First: 2026-04-13T02:24:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T02:24:32+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Medium-to-long-horizon stock allocation presents significant challenges due toveak predictive structures, non-stadonary market regimes, and the degradationf signals following the application of transaction costs, capacity limits, and tail-isk constraints. Conventional approaches commonly rely on a single predictor orloosely coupled prediction-to-allocation pipeline, limiting robustness underThis work addresses a targeted design question: whetherlistribution shift. 1coupling reinforcement learning (RL), multi-agent policy populations, Policy-Space Response Oracle (PSRO)-style aggregation, league best-response trainingevolutionary replacement, and execution-aware checkpoint selection within ainified walk-forward loop improves allocator robustness at medium to longhorizons. The proposed framework, EvoNash-MARL, integrates these componentswithin an execution-aware allocation loop and further introduces a layeredpolicy architecture comprising a direction head and a risk head, nonlinear signalenhancement, feature-quality reweighting, and constraint-aware checkpointselection. Under a 120-window walk-forward protocol, the resolved v21configuration achieves mean excess Sharpe 0.7600 and robust score -0.0203,anking first among internal controls; on aligned daily out-of-sample returnsrom 2014-01-02 to 2024-01-05, it delivers 19.6% annualized return versus 11.7% for SPY, and in an extended walk-forward evaluation through 2026-02-10 it delivers 20.5% rersus 13.5%. The framework maintains positive performance under realistictress constraints and exhibits structured cross-market generalization; however,lobal strong significance under White's Reality Check (WRC) and SPA-lite testingestablished. Therefore, the results are presented as evidence supporting asnotnore stable medium-to long-horizon training and selection paradigm, ratherhan as prooffof universally superior market-timing performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：EvoNash-MARL：一种面向中周期资产配置的闭环多智能体强化学习框架
中长周期股票配置因预测结构薄弱、市场机制非平稳、以及交易成本、容量限制和尾部风险约束导致信号衰减而面临显著挑战。传统方法通常依赖单一预测器或松散的预测-配置流程，限制了其在分布偏移下的稳健性。本研究针对一个具体设计问题：在统一的向前滚动循环中，耦合强化学习（RL）、多智能体策略种群、策略空间响应预言（PSRO）式聚合、联盟最佳响应训练、进化替换以及执行感知的检查点选择，是否能提升中长周期配置器的稳健性。所提出的EvoNash-MARL框架将这些组件集成于一个执行感知的配置循环中，并进一步引入包含方向头和风险头的分层策略架构、非线性信号增强、特征质量重加权以及约束感知的检查点选择。在120窗口向前滚动协议下，确定的v21配置实现了0.7600的平均超额夏普比率和-0.0203的稳健得分，在内部对照中排名第一；在2014-01-02至2024-01-05对齐的日度样本外收益上，其年化收益率为19.6%，而SPY为11.7%；在延伸至2026-02-10的向前滚动评估中，其收益率为20.5%，对比基准为13.5%。该框架在现实压力约束下保持正向表现，并展现出结构化的跨市场泛化能力；然而，在怀特现实检验（WRC）和SPA-lite测试中未确立全局强显著性。因此，这些结果被呈现为支持一种更稳定的中长周期训练与选择范式的证据，而非作为普遍优越的市场择时性能的证明。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenges of medium-to-long-horizon stock allocation, such as weak predictive structures and non-stationary market regimes, by proposing a unified framework called EvoNash-MARL that integrates multi-agent reinforcement learning with evolutionary and game-theoretic components like PSRO-style aggregation and league training. The method employs a closed-loop walk-forward design featuring a layered policy architecture with direction and risk heads, along with nonlinear signal enhancement and constraint-aware checkpoint selection. Experimental results under a 120-window walk-forward protocol show the framework achieving a mean excess Sharpe of 0.7600 and robust score of -0.0203, outperforming internal controls; in out-of-sample daily returns from 2014 to 2024, it yields 19.6% annualized return versus 11.7% for SPY, with extended evaluation through 2026 further confirming its robustness, though statistical significance tests like White's Reality Check do not establish universal superiority.
该论文针对中长周期股票配置中预测结构弱、市场机制非平稳等挑战，提出了一个名为EvoNash-MARL的统一框架，该框架将多智能体强化学习与进化及博弈论组件（如PSRO式聚合和联盟训练）相结合。方法采用闭环前向滚动设计，包含方向头和风险头的分层策略架构，以及非线性信号增强和约束感知的检查点选择。在120窗口的前向滚动协议下，实验结果显示该框架实现了0.7600的平均超额夏普比率和-0.0203的稳健得分，优于内部对照组；在2014年至2024年的日度样本外回报中，其年化收益率为19.6%，而SPY为11.7%，延伸至2026年的评估进一步验证了其稳健性，但怀特现实检验等统计测试未证实其普遍优越性。
CheeseBench: Evaluating Large Language Models on Rodent Behavioral Neuroscience Paradigms
Authors: Zacharie Bugaud
First: 2026-04-12T21:37:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-12T21:37:26+00:00
Comments: 8 pages, 6 figures, 4 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce CheeseBench, a benchmark that evaluates large language models (LLMs) on nine classical behavioral neuroscience paradigms (Morris water maze, Barnes maze, T-maze, radial arm maze, star maze, operant chamber, shuttle box, conditioned place preference, and delayed non-match to sample), spanning six cognitive dimensions. Each task is grounded in peer-reviewed rodent protocols with approximate animal baselines. The agent receives a unified system prompt with no task-specific instructions and must discover goals purely from ASCII text observations and reward signals, much like a rodent placed into an unfamiliar apparatus. We evaluate six open-weight LLMs (3B to 72B parameters) on text-based ASCII renderings and compare against both a random baseline and a graph-based reinforcement learning agent. Our best model (Qwen2.5-VL-7B) reaches 52.6% average success on ASCII input, compared to 32.1% for random agents and 78.9% for approximate rodent baselines. We find that (1) scaling beyond 7B yields diminishing returns, (2) longer context history degrades performance, (3) chain-of-thought prompting hurts rather than helps, and (4) a vision-language architecture provides an advantage at 7B but hurts at 32B. Because the same model's performance ranges from 20% to 57% depending on interface parameters alone, these results characterize the agent-plus-interface system, not the model in isolation. Under this unified zero-shot ASCII protocol, current open-weight LLM agents remain well below approximate rodent reference values, particularly on tasks requiring spatial navigation and within-trial state tracking.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CheeseBench：基于啮齿类动物行为神经科学范式评估大语言模型
我们提出CheeseBench基准测试，在九种经典行为神经科学范式（莫里斯水迷宫、巴恩斯迷宫、T型迷宫、放射臂迷宫、星形迷宫、操作箱、穿梭箱、条件性位置偏好、延迟非匹配样本任务）上评估大语言模型，涵盖六个认知维度。每个任务均基于经同行评审的啮齿类动物实验协议，并附有近似动物基线数据。智能体接收统一的系统提示（不含任务特定指令），必须完全通过ASCII文本观察和奖励信号自主发现目标，类似于将啮齿动物置于陌生装置中的情境。我们在基于文本的ASCII渲染场景中评估六个开源权重LLM（参数量3B至72B），并与随机基线及基于图的强化学习智能体对比。最佳模型（Qwen2.5-VL-7B）在ASCII输入上达到52.6%的平均成功率，随机智能体为32.1%，近似啮齿类动物基线为78.9%。研究发现：（1）参数量超过7B后收益递减；（2）更长上下文历史会降低性能；（3）思维链提示反而损害表现；（4）视觉语言架构在7B规模有优势但在32B规模产生负面影响。由于同一模型仅因界面参数差异就表现出20%至57%的性能波动，这些结果表征的是智能体-界面复合系统而非孤立模型。在此统一零样本ASCII协议下，当前开源权重LLM智能体仍远低于近似啮齿类动物参考值，尤其在需要空间导航和试次内状态追踪的任务上。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces CheeseBench, a benchmark designed to evaluate large language models (LLMs) on nine classical rodent behavioral neuroscience paradigms, motivated by the need to assess LLMs' cognitive abilities in tasks spanning six dimensions, such as spatial navigation. The method involves presenting LLM agents with a unified system prompt and requiring them to discover goals from ASCII text observations and reward signals, simulating a rodent's experience, and compares their performance against random baselines, a graph-based RL agent, and approximate rodent baselines. Key experimental results show that the best-performing model, Qwen2.5-VL-7B, achieved a 52.6% average success rate on ASCII input, which is below the 78.9% rodent baseline but above the 32.1% random baseline, with findings indicating diminishing returns beyond 7B parameters, performance degradation with longer context history, negative effects from chain-of-thought prompting, and interface-dependent variability in model outcomes.
本文介绍了CheeseBench，这是一个旨在评估大语言模型在九种经典啮齿动物行为神经科学范式上表现的基准，其动机是需要评估大语言模型在空间导航等六个认知维度的任务中的能力。方法上，该基准通过统一的系统提示要求大语言模型智能体仅从ASCII文本观察和奖励信号中发现目标，模拟啮齿动物的体验，并将其性能与随机基线、基于图的强化学习智能体以及近似的啮齿动物基线进行比较。主要实验结果表明，性能最佳的模型Qwen2.5-VL-7B在ASCII输入上的平均成功率为52.6%，低于78.9%的啮齿动物基线但高于32.1%的随机基线，同时发现超过70亿参数后收益递减、更长的上下文历史会降低性能、思维链提示反而有害，且模型表现高度依赖于界面参数。
PokeRL: Reinforcement Learning for Pokemon Red
Authors: Dheeraj Mudireddy, Sai Patibandla
First: 2026-04-12T20:46:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-12T20:46:47+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Pokemon Red is a long-horizon JRPG with sparse rewards, partial observability, and quirky control mechanics that make it a challenging benchmark for reinforcement learning. While recent work has shown that PPO agents can clear the first two gyms using heavy reward shaping and engineered observations, training remains brittle in practice, with agents often degenerating into action loops, menu spam, or unproductive wandering. In this paper, we present PokeRL, a modular system that trains deep reinforcement learning agents to complete early game tasks in Pokemon Red, including exiting the player's house, exploring Pallet Town to reach tall grass, and winning the first rival battle. Our main contributions are a loop-aware environment wrapper around the PyBoy emulator with map masking, a multi-layer anti-loop and anti-spam mechanism, and a dense hierarchical reward design. We argue that practical systems like PokeRL, which explicitly model failure modes such as loops and spam, are a necessary intermediate step between toy benchmarks and full Pokemon League champion agents. Code is available at https://github.com/reddheeraj/PokemonRL
中文标题/摘要
标题：PokeRL：面向《宝可梦红》的强化学习系统
《宝可梦红》是一款具有长时程、稀疏奖励、部分可观测性及特殊操控机制的日式角色扮演游戏，这使其成为强化学习的挑战性基准。尽管近期研究表明PPO智能体可通过密集奖励塑造与工程化观测攻克前两个道馆，但实际训练仍显脆弱，智能体常陷入动作循环、菜单滥用或无效游荡。本文提出PokeRL——一个模块化系统，通过深度强化学习训练智能体完成《宝可梦红》的早期任务，包括离开玩家房屋、探索真新镇抵达草丛区域以及赢得首场宿敌对战。核心贡献包括：基于PyBoy模拟器的地图掩码循环感知环境封装器、多层抗循环与防滥用机制，以及密集分层奖励设计。我们认为，像PokeRL这样显式建模循环与滥用等失效模式的实用系统，是实现从玩具基准到完整宝可梦联盟冠军智能体的必要中间步骤。代码发布于https://github.com/reddheeraj/PokemonRL

The motivation for this work is to address the challenges of applying reinforcement learning to Pokemon Red, a complex JRPG with sparse rewards and partial observability, where existing methods often lead to degenerate behaviors like action loops. The method introduces PokeRL, a modular system featuring a loop-aware environment wrapper with map masking, multi-layer anti-loop and anti-spam mechanisms, and a dense hierarchical reward design. The main experimental results show that PokeRL successfully trains agents to complete early game tasks, such as exiting the house, exploring Pallet Town, and winning the first rival battle, demonstrating improved robustness over prior approaches.
