Advancing Polish Language Modeling through Tokenizer Optimization in the Bielik v3 7B and 11B Series
Authors: Krzysztof Ociepa, Łukasz Flis, Remigiusz Kinas, Krzysztof Wróbel, Adrian Gwoździej
First: 2026-04-12T20:19:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-12T20:19:27+00:00
Comments: arXiv admin note: text overlap with arXiv:2601.11579
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The development of the Bielik v3 PL series, encompassing both the 7B and 11B parameter variants, represents a significant milestone in the field of language-specific large language model (LLM) optimization. While general-purpose models often demonstrate impressive multilingual capabilities, they frequently suffer from a fundamental architectural inefficiency: the use of universal tokenizers. These tokenizers, typically designed to cover a broad spectrum of languages, often fail to capture the morphological nuances of specific languages like Polish, leading to higher fertility ratios, increased inference costs, and restricted effective context windows. This report details the transition from the universal Mistral-based tokenization to a dedicated Polish-optimized vocabulary for the Bielik v3 models, exploring the FOCUS-based embedding initialization, the multi-stage pretraining curriculum, and the subsequent post-training alignment involving Supervised Fine-Tuning, Direct Preference Optimization, and Reinforcement Learning through Group Relative Policy Optimization with verifiable rewards.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过分词器优化推进Bielik v3 7B与11B系列波兰语建模
Bielik v3 PL系列（含7B与110亿参数变体）的开发标志着语言专用大语言模型优化领域的重要里程碑。通用模型虽展现出色的多语言能力，却常存在根本性架构缺陷：采用通用分词器。这类为广泛语言设计的分词器往往无法捕捉波兰语等特定语言的形态学特征，导致生育率升高、推理成本增加及有效上下文窗口受限。本报告详述了Bielik v3模型从基于Mistral的通用分词转向专用波兰语优化词表的过程，探讨了基于FOCUS的嵌入初始化、多阶段预训练课程设计，以及后续包含监督微调、直接偏好优化、通过可验证奖励的群组相对策略优化进行强化学习的训练后对齐方案。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the inefficiency of universal tokenizers for language-specific modeling, which often fail to capture morphological nuances and lead to higher costs and restricted context in languages like Polish, this work introduces the Bielik v3 series (7B and 11B parameters) by transitioning from a Mistral-based tokenizer to a dedicated Polish-optimized vocabulary. The method employs FOCUS-based embedding initialization, a multi-stage pretraining curriculum, and post-training alignment via Supervised Fine-Tuning, Direct Preference Optimization, and Reinforcement Learning with verifiable rewards. The main experimental results demonstrate that this tokenizer optimization significantly advances Polish language modeling, improving efficiency and performance over general-purpose models.
本研究旨在解决通用分词器在特定语言建模中的低效问题，这些分词器通常无法捕捉波兰语等语言的形态学细微差别，导致成本增加和有效上下文窗口受限。为此，Bielik v3系列（70亿和110亿参数）从基于Mistral的分词器转向专用的波兰语优化词汇表，方法包括采用FOCUS嵌入初始化、多阶段预训练课程以及通过监督微调、直接偏好优化和基于可验证奖励的强化学习进行后训练对齐。主要实验结果表明，这种分词器优化显著推进了波兰语语言建模，在效率和性能上超越了通用模型。
TInR: Exploring Tool-Internalized Reasoning in Large Language Models
Authors: Qiancheng Xu, Yongqi Li, Fan Liu, Hongru Wang, Min Yang, Wenjie Li
First: 2026-04-12T19:38:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-12T19:38:19+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Tool-Integrated Reasoning (TIR) has emerged as a promising direction by extending Large Language Models' (LLMs) capabilities with external tools during reasoning. Existing TIR methods typically rely on external tool documentation during reasoning. However, this leads to tool mastery difficulty, tool size constraints, and inference inefficiency. To mitigate these issues, we explore Tool-Internalized Reasoning (TInR), aiming at facilitating reasoning with tool knowledge internalized into LLMs. Achieving this goal presents notable requirements, including tool internalization and tool-reasoning coordination. To address them, we propose TInR-U, a tool-internalized reasoning framework for unified reasoning and tool usage. TInR-U is trained through a three-phase pipeline: 1) tool internalization with a bidirectional knowledge alignment strategy; 2) supervised fine-tuning warm-up using high-quality reasoning annotations, and 3) reinforcement learning with TInR-specific rewards. We comprehensively evaluate our method across in-domain and out-of-domain settings. Experiment results show that TInR-U achieves superior performance in both settings, highlighting its effectiveness and efficiency.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TInR：探索大型语言模型中的工具内化推理
工具集成推理（TIR）通过为大型语言模型（LLM）在推理过程中引入外部工具，已成为一个前景广阔的研究方向。现有TIR方法通常在推理时依赖外部工具文档，但这导致工具掌握困难、工具规模受限及推理效率低下。为缓解这些问题，我们探索工具内化推理（TInR），旨在将工具知识内化至LLM中以辅助推理。实现此目标需满足工具内化与工具-推理协同两大核心需求。为此，我们提出TInR-U——一个统一推理与工具使用的工具内化推理框架。TInR-U通过三阶段流程训练：1）采用双向知识对齐策略实现工具内化；2）利用高质量推理标注进行监督微调预热；3）结合TInR定制奖励的强化学习。我们在领域内与跨领域场景中全面评估该方法，实验结果表明TInR-U在两种场景下均取得优越性能，彰显了其高效性与有效性。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by limitations in existing Tool-Integrated Reasoning (TIR) methods for Large Language Models, such as reliance on external tool documentation causing mastery difficulty, size constraints, and inefficiency. To address this, the authors propose TInR (Tool-Internalized Reasoning) and introduce TInR-U, a framework that internalizes tool knowledge into LLMs through a three-phase training pipeline involving bidirectional knowledge alignment, supervised fine-tuning, and reinforcement learning with specialized rewards. Experimental results demonstrate that TInR-U achieves superior performance in both in-domain and out-of-domain settings, confirming its effectiveness and efficiency in tool-internalized reasoning.
本文的动机源于现有大型语言模型的工具集成推理方法存在依赖外部工具文档、导致工具掌握困难、规模受限和推理效率低等局限性。为此，作者探索工具内化推理，并提出TInR-U框架，通过包含双向知识对齐、监督微调预热和基于特定奖励的强化学习的三阶段训练流程，将工具知识内化到模型中。实验结果表明，TInR-U在领域内和领域外设置下均取得了优越性能，凸显了其在工具内化推理中的有效性和高效性。
Influencing Humans to Conform to Preference Models for RLHF
Authors: Stephane Hatgis-Kessell, W. Bradley Knox, Serena Booth, Peter Stone
First: 2025-01-11T03:12:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-12T19:37:32+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Designing a reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) algorithm to approximate a human's unobservable reward function requires assuming, implicitly or explicitly, a model of human preferences. A preference model that poorly describes how humans generate preferences risks learning a poor approximation of the human's reward function. In this paper, we conduct three human studies to asses whether one can influence the expression of real human preferences to more closely conform to a desired preference model. Importantly, our approach does not seek to alter the human's unobserved reward function. Rather, we change how humans use this reward function to generate preferences, such that they better match whatever preference model is assumed by a particular RLHF algorithm. We introduce three interventions: showing humans the quantities that underlie a preference model, which is normally unobservable information derived from the reward function; training people to follow a specific preference model; and modifying the preference elicitation question. All intervention types show significant effects, providing practical tools to improve preference data quality and the resultant alignment of the learned reward functions. Overall we establish a novel research direction in model alignment: designing interfaces and training interventions to increase human conformance with the modeling assumptions of the algorithm that will learn from their input.
中文标题/摘要
标题：引导人类行为以符合强化学习人类反馈中的偏好模型
设计基于人类反馈的强化学习算法以逼近人类不可观测的奖励函数时，需要显式或隐式地假设人类偏好模型。若偏好模型无法准确描述人类生成偏好的机制，则可能导致对奖励函数的近似效果不佳。本文通过三项人类行为研究，评估是否能够影响真实人类偏好的表达，使其更贴近目标偏好模型。关键之处在于，我们的方法并非试图改变人类内在的奖励函数，而是调整人类如何运用该函数生成偏好，使其更契合特定RLHF算法所假设的偏好模型。我们提出三种干预措施：向人类展示通常源自奖励函数的不可观测偏好模型参数、训练人们遵循特定偏好模型、以及修改偏好收集问题。所有干预类型均显示出显著效果，为提升偏好数据质量及最终习得奖励函数的对齐性提供了实用工具。本研究开创了模型对齐的新研究方向：通过设计交互界面与训练干预机制，增强人类行为与算法建模假设的契合度，使算法能更有效地从人类输入中学习。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates whether human preference expression can be influenced to better conform to the specific preference models assumed by Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) algorithms, thereby improving the quality of learned reward functions without altering the human's underlying reward. The method introduces three practical interventions: revealing normally hidden model quantities to users, training people to follow a specific preference model, and modifying the format of the preference elicitation question itself. Experimental results from three human studies demonstrate that all intervention types significantly affect how preferences are expressed, offering practical tools to enhance data quality and the ultimate alignment of learned reward functions with human intent.
本文研究是否可以通过干预来影响人类偏好的表达，使其更符合强化学习人类反馈（RLHF）算法所假设的特定偏好模型，从而在不改变人类内在奖励函数的前提下，提升所学奖励函数的质量。方法上引入了三种实际干预措施：向用户揭示通常隐藏的模型量化信息、训练人们遵循特定的偏好模型、以及修改偏好收集问题的形式。三项人类研究的实验结果表明，所有干预类型均能显著影响偏好的表达方式，这为提高数据质量以及最终所学奖励函数与人类意图的对齐提供了实用工具。
Learning Preference-Based Objectives from Clinical Narratives for Sequential Treatment Decision-Making
Authors: Daniel J. Tan, Kay Choong See, Mengling Feng
First: 2026-04-12T19:18:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-12T19:18:02+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Designing reward functions remains a central challenge in reinforcement learning (RL) for healthcare, where outcomes are sparse, delayed, and difficult to specify. While structured data capture physiological states, they often fail to reflect the overall quality of a patient's clinical trajectory, including recovery dynamics, treatment burden, and stability. Clinical narratives, in contrast, summarize longitudinal reasoning and implicitly encode evaluations of treatment effectiveness. We propose Clinical Narrative-informed Preference Rewards (CN-PR), a framework for learning reward functions directly from discharge summaries by treating them as scalable supervision for trajectory-level preferences. Using a large language model, we derive trajectory quality scores (TQS) and construct pairwise preferences over patient trajectories, enabling reward learning via a structured preference-based objective. To account for variability in narrative informativeness, we incorporate a confidence signal that weights supervision based on its relevance to the decision-making task. The learned reward aligns strongly with trajectory quality (Spearman rho = 0.63) and enables policies that are consistently associated with improved recovery-related outcomes, including increased organ support-free days and faster shock resolution, while maintaining comparable performance on mortality. These effects persist under external validation. Our results demonstrate that narrative-derived supervision provides a scalable and expressive alternative to handcrafted or outcome-based reward design for dynamic treatment regimes.

标题：基于临床叙事学习偏好目标以支持序贯治疗决策
在医疗健康领域的强化学习中，设计奖励函数仍是一个核心挑战，因为医疗结果往往稀疏、延迟且难以明确界定。结构化数据虽能捕捉生理状态，却常无法全面反映患者临床轨迹的整体质量，包括康复动态、治疗负担及稳定性。相比之下，临床叙事总结了纵向推理过程，并隐含了对治疗效果的评估。我们提出临床叙事驱动的偏好奖励框架，通过将出院小结视为可扩展的轨迹级偏好监督信号，直接从叙事中学习奖励函数。利用大语言模型，我们推导轨迹质量评分并构建患者轨迹的成对偏好，从而通过结构化偏好目标实现奖励学习。为应对叙事信息量的差异性，我们引入置信度信号，根据叙事与决策任务的相关性对监督进行加权。所学奖励与轨迹质量高度相关，且能生成持续改善康复相关结局的策略，包括增加器官支持无干预天数、加速休克缓解，同时保持与死亡率相当的疗效。这些效果在外部分析中保持稳定。结果表明，叙事衍生的监督为动态治疗方案提供了一种可扩展且表达力强的替代方案，优于手工设计或基于结局的奖励机制。

Putting the Value Back in RL: Better Test-Time Scaling by Unifying LLM Reasoners With Verifiers
Authors: Kusha Sareen, Morgane M Moss, Alessandro Sordoni, Rishabh Agarwal, Arian Hosseini
First: 2025-05-07T22:41:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-12T16:48:19+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Prevalent reinforcement learning~(RL) methods for fine-tuning LLM reasoners, such as GRPO or Leave-one-out PPO, abandon the learned value function in favor of empirically estimated returns. This hinders test-time compute scaling that relies on using the value-function for verification. Yet if parallel test-time compute is already part of the deployment plan, training should be designed to support it. In this work, we propose RL$^V$ that augments any ``value-free'' RL method by jointly training the LLM as both a reasoner and a generative verifier using RL-generated data, adding verification capabilities without significant overhead. Empirically, RL$^V$ boosts MATH accuracy by over 20\% with parallel sampling and enables $8-32\times$ efficient test-time compute scaling compared to the base RL method. RL$^V$ also exhibits strong generalization capabilities for both easy-to-hard and out-of-domain tasks. Furthermore, RL$^V$ achieves $1.2-1.6\times$ higher performance when jointly scaling parallel and sequential test-time compute with a long reasoning R1 model. More broadly, RL$^V$ instantiates the principle of co-training for test-time scaling: jointly optimizing for task performance and a capability useful at inference, using data that RL training already produces.

标题：为强化学习重拾价值：通过统一大语言模型推理器与验证器实现更优测试时扩展
当前用于微调大语言模型推理器的强化学习方法（如GRPO或留一法PPO）普遍放弃已学习的价值函数，转而依赖经验估计的回报。这阻碍了依赖价值函数进行验证的测试时计算扩展。然而，若并行测试时计算本就是部署计划的一部分，训练过程应为此提供支持。本研究提出RL$^V$方法，通过使用强化学习生成的数据联合训练大语言模型同时作为推理器和生成式验证器，为任意“无价值函数”的强化学习方法增强验证能力，且不产生显著开销。实验表明：RL$^V$在并行采样下将MATH数据集准确率提升超20%，相比基础强化学习方法实现$8-32\times$的测试时计算效率扩展；在易至难任务及跨领域任务中均展现强大泛化能力；当与长推理R1模型联合扩展并行与顺序测试时计算时，性能提升达$1.2-1.6\times$。更广泛而言，RL$^V$实例化了测试时扩展的协同训练原则：利用强化学习训练已产生的数据，联合优化任务性能与推理阶段有用的能力。

Why Code, Why Now: An Information-Theoretic Perspective on the Limits of Machine Learning
Authors: Zhimin Zhao
First: 2026-02-15T00:14:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-12T16:25:39+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper offers a new perspective on the limits of machine learning: the ceiling on progress is set not by model size or algorithm choice but by the information structure of the task itself. Code generation has progressed more reliably than reinforcement learning, largely because code provides dense, local, verifiable feedback at every token, whereas most reinforcement learning problems do not. This difference in feedback quality is not binary but graded. We propose a five-level hierarchy of learnability based on information structure and argue that diagnosing a task's position in this hierarchy is more predictive of scaling outcomes than any property of the model. The hierarchy rests on a formal distinction among three properties of computational problems (expressibility, computability, and learnability). We establish their pairwise relationships, including where implications hold and where they fail, and present a unified template that makes the structural differences explicit. The analysis suggests why supervised learning on code scales predictably while reinforcement learning does not, and why the common assumption that scaling alone will solve remaining ML challenges warrants scrutiny.
中文标题/摘要
标题：为何是代码，为何是现在：从信息论视角看机器学习的局限
本文提出审视机器学习局限的新视角：进步的上限并非由模型规模或算法选择决定，而是由任务本身的信息结构所设定。代码生成比强化学习进展更稳定，主要因为代码在每个标记处提供密集、局部且可验证的反馈，而多数强化学习问题则不然。这种反馈质量的差异并非二元对立，而是存在梯度。我们基于信息结构提出五级可学习性层次体系，并论证通过诊断任务在该体系中的位置，比依赖模型任何特性更能预测规模化效果。该体系建立在计算问题三大特性（可表达性、可计算性、可学习性）的形式化区分之上，阐明三者间的成对关系（包括蕴含成立与失效的情形），并提出使结构差异显式化的统一模板。分析揭示了代码监督学习可预测扩展而强化学习不能的原因，并对‘仅靠扩展就能解决机器学习剩余挑战’的普遍假设提出质疑。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the observation that code generation scales more reliably than reinforcement learning, this paper argues that the fundamental limit of machine learning is determined by the information structure of a task rather than model size or algorithms. The method introduces a five-level hierarchy of learnability based on formal distinctions among expressibility, computability, and learnability, providing a unified template to analyze structural differences in feedback quality. Experimental results highlight that tasks with dense, local, verifiable feedback—like code generation—enable predictable scaling, whereas reinforcement learning often lacks such properties, challenging the assumption that scaling alone will solve remaining machine learning problems.
本文观察到代码生成比强化学习更具可扩展性，由此提出机器学习的基本限制取决于任务的信息结构，而非模型规模或算法。方法上，基于可表达性、可计算性和可学习性之间的形式区分，引入了一个五级可学习性层次结构，并提供了一个统一模板来明确反馈质量的结构差异。实验结果表明，具有密集、局部、可验证反馈的任务（如代码生成）可实现可预测的扩展，而强化学习通常缺乏此类特性，这挑战了仅靠扩展就能解决剩余机器学习问题的常见假设。
Bringing Value Models Back: Generative Critics for Value Modeling in LLM Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Zikang Shan, Han Zhong, Liwei Wang, Li Zhao
First: 2026-04-12T15:54:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-12T15:54:11+00:00
Comments: 16 pages including appendix, 4 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Credit assignment is a central challenge in reinforcement learning (RL). Classical actor-critic methods address this challenge through fine-grained advantage estimation based on a learned value function. However, learned value models are often avoided in modern large language model (LLM) RL because conventional discriminative critics are difficult to train reliably. We revisit value modeling and argue that this difficulty is partly due to limited expressiveness. In particular, representation complexity theory suggests that value functions can be hard to approximate under the one-shot prediction paradigm used by existing value models, and our scaling experiments show that such critics do not improve reliably with scale. Motivated by this observation, we propose Generative Actor-Critic (GenAC), which replaces one-shot scalar value prediction with a generative critic that performs chain-of-thought reasoning before producing a value estimate. We further introduce In-Context Conditioning, which helps the critic remain calibrated to the current actor throughout training. GenAC improves value approximation, ranking reliability, and out-of-distribution generalization, and these gains translate into stronger downstream RL performance than both value-based and value-free baselines. Overall, our results suggest that stronger value modeling is a promising direction for improving credit assignment in LLM reinforcement learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：价值模型回归：大语言模型强化学习中价值建模的生成式评论家
信用分配是强化学习（RL）的核心挑战。经典的演员-评论家方法通过基于学习价值函数的细粒度优势估计来解决这一挑战。然而，在现代大语言模型（LLM）强化学习中，学习到的价值模型常被回避，因为传统的判别式评论家难以可靠训练。我们重新审视价值建模，认为这一困难部分源于表达能力有限。具体而言，表示复杂性理论表明，在现有价值模型使用的单次预测范式下，价值函数可能难以近似，且我们的扩展实验显示此类评论家无法随规模提升而可靠改进。基于此观察，我们提出生成式演员-评论家（GenAC），用生成式评论家替代单次标量价值预测，该评论家在生成价值估计前执行思维链推理。我们进一步引入上下文条件化技术，帮助评论家在训练过程中保持与当前演员的校准。GenAC提升了价值近似、排序可靠性和分布外泛化能力，这些优势转化为优于基于价值和无价值基线的下游强化学习性能。总体而言，我们的结果表明，强化价值建模是改进LLM强化学习中信用分配的有前景方向。

Consolidation or Adaptation? PRISM: Disentangling SFT and RL Data via Gradient Concentration
Authors: Yang Zhao, Yangou Ouyang, Xiao Ding, Hepeng Wang, Bibo Cai, Kai Xiong, Jinglong Gao, Zhouhao Sun, Li Du, Bing Qin, Ting Liu
First: 2026-01-12T05:43:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-12T15:49:11+00:00
Comments: ACL2026 Main Conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While Hybrid Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) followed by Reinforcement Learning (RL) has become the standard paradigm for training LLM agents, effective mechanisms for data allocation between these stages remain largely underexplored. Current data arbitration strategies often rely on surface-level heuristics that fail to diagnose intrinsic learning needs. Since SFT targets pattern consolidation through imitation while RL drives structural adaptation via exploration, misaligning data with these functional roles causes severe optimization interference. We propose PRISM, a dynamics-aware framework grounded in Schema Theory that arbitrates data based on its degree of cognitive conflict with the model's existing knowledge. By analyzing the spatial geometric structure of gradients, PRISM identifies data triggering high spatial concentration as high-conflict signals that require RL for structural restructuring. In contrast, data yielding diffuse updates is routed to SFT for efficient consolidation. Extensive experiments on WebShop and ALFWorld demonstrate that PRISM achieves a Pareto improvement, outperforming state-of-the-art hybrid methods while reducing computational costs by up to 3.22$\times$. Our findings suggest that disentangling data based on internal optimization regimes is crucial for scalable and robust agent alignment.
中文标题/摘要
标题：巩固还是适应？PRISM：通过梯度集中度解耦监督微调与强化学习数据
虽然监督微调（SFT）与强化学习（RL）结合的混合范式已成为训练大语言模型智能体的标准方法，但两阶段间有效的数据分配机制仍缺乏深入探索。当前数据仲裁策略多依赖表层启发式方法，难以诊断内在学习需求。由于SFT通过模仿实现模式巩固，而RL通过探索驱动结构适应，数据与功能角色的错配会导致严重的优化干扰。我们提出PRISM——一个基于图式理论、具备动态感知能力的框架，通过数据与模型现有知识的认知冲突程度进行仲裁。通过分析梯度的空间几何结构，PRISM将引发高空间集中度的数据识别为高冲突信号，需通过RL进行结构重组；而产生分散更新的数据则分配给SFT进行高效巩固。在WebShop和ALFWorld上的大量实验表明，PRISM实现了帕累托改进，在降低最高3.22倍计算成本的同时，性能优于当前最先进的混合方法。我们的研究证明，基于内部优化机制解耦数据对实现可扩展且鲁棒的智能体对齐至关重要。

Motivated by the lack of effective data allocation mechanisms between Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) and Reinforcement Learning (RL) in standard LLM agent training, this paper introduces PRISM, a framework that uses Schema Theory and gradient spatial geometry to diagnose data based on its cognitive conflict with existing model knowledge. The method routes data causing high spatial gradient concentration, indicating a need for structural adaptation, to RL, while data yielding diffuse gradient updates is allocated to SFT for pattern consolidation. Main experimental results on WebShop and ALFWorld show that PRISM achieves a Pareto improvement over state-of-the-art hybrid methods and reduces computational costs by up to 3.22 times, demonstrating that disentangling data by internal optimization regimes is key for scalable agent alignment.
本文的动机在于，标准的大语言模型智能体训练中，监督微调（SFT）和强化学习（RL）两阶段之间缺乏有效的数据分配机制。为此，作者提出了PRISM框架，该方法基于图式理论，通过分析梯度的空间几何结构来诊断数据与模型现有知识的认知冲突程度：引发高度空间集中的梯度（高冲突）数据被分配给RL进行结构适应，而产生分散梯度更新的数据则路由给SFT进行模式巩固。在WebShop和ALFWorld上的主要实验结果表明，PRISM实现了帕累托改进，性能优于最先进的混合方法，并将计算成本降低了高达3.22倍，这表明根据内部优化机制分离数据对于可扩展的智能体对齐至关重要。
SCOPE: Signal-Calibrated On-Policy Distillation Enhancement with Dual-Path Adaptive Weighting
Authors: Binbin Zheng, Xing Ma, Yiheng Liang, Jingqing Ruan, Xiaoliang Fu, Kepeng Lin, Benchang Zhu, Ke Zeng, Xunliang Cai
First: 2026-04-12T15:26:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-12T15:26:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
On-policy reinforcement learning has become the dominant paradigm for reasoning alignment in large language models, yet its sparse, outcome-level rewards make token-level credit assignment notoriously difficult. On-Policy Distillation (OPD) alleviates this by introducing dense, token-level KL supervision from a teacher model, but typically applies this supervision uniformly across all rollouts, ignoring fundamental differences in signal quality. We propose Signal-Calibrated On-Policy Distillation Enhancement (SCOPE), a dual-path adaptive training framework that routes on-policy rollouts by correctness into two complementary supervision paths. For incorrect trajectories, SCOPE performs teacher-perplexity-weighted KL distillation to prioritize instances where the teacher demonstrates genuine corrective capability, while down-weighting unreliable guidance. For correct trajectories, it applies student-perplexity-weighted MLE to concentrate reinforcement on low-confidence samples at the capability boundary rather than over-reinforcing already mastered ones. Both paths employ a group-level normalization to adaptively calibrate weight distributions, accounting for the intrinsic difficulty variance across prompts. Extensive experiments on six reasoning benchmarks show that SCOPE achieves an average relative improvement of 11.42% in Avg@32 and 7.30% in Pass@32 over competitive baselines, demonstrating its consistent effectiveness.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SCOPE：基于信号校准的双路径自适应加权策略蒸馏增强方法
策略强化学习已成为大语言模型推理对齐的主流范式，但其稀疏的结果级奖励使得词级信用分配极为困难。策略蒸馏通过引入教师模型的密集词级KL监督缓解了这一问题，但通常对所有推演轨迹施加均匀监督，忽略了信号质量的根本差异。本文提出信号校准的策略蒸馏增强方法，该双路径自适应训练框架根据推演轨迹的正确性将其路由至两条互补的监督路径：对于错误轨迹，采用教师困惑度加权的KL蒸馏，优先处理教师模型展现真实纠错能力的样本，同时降低不可靠指导的权重；对于正确轨迹，采用学生困惑度加权的最大似然估计，将强化重点集中于能力边界的低置信度样本，避免对已掌握样本的过度强化。两条路径均采用组级归一化自适应校准权重分布，以应对不同提示间的内在难度差异。在六个推理基准上的大量实验表明，SCOPE在Avg@32和Pass@32指标上分别实现了11.42%和7.30%的平均相对提升，验证了其持续有效性。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for SCOPE stems from the difficulty of token-level credit assignment in on-policy reinforcement learning for large language models, where sparse rewards are problematic, and standard On-Policy Distillation applies uniform supervision despite varying signal quality. The method introduces a dual-path adaptive framework that separates rollouts by correctness: for incorrect trajectories, it uses teacher-perplexity-weighted KL distillation to focus on reliable teacher corrections, and for correct ones, it applies student-perplexity-weighted maximum likelihood estimation to reinforce low-confidence samples at the capability boundary, with group-level normalization to adjust for prompt difficulty. Experimental results across six reasoning benchmarks show average relative improvements of 11.42% in Avg@32 and 7.30% in Pass@32 over baselines, confirming its consistent effectiveness.
SCOPE的提出动机在于，大语言模型的对齐训练中，基于策略的强化学习存在稀疏奖励问题，使得令牌级信用分配困难，而标准的策略上蒸馏方法忽略了信号质量的差异而施加均匀监督。该方法采用双路径自适应训练框架，根据正确性将策略轨迹分流：对于错误轨迹，使用基于教师困惑度加权的KL蒸馏以聚焦教师模型可靠的纠正能力；对于正确轨迹，则应用基于学生困惑度加权的最大似然估计，强化能力边界上的低置信度样本，并通过组级归一化适应不同提示的固有难度差异。在六个推理基准上的广泛实验表明，相比基线方法，SCOPE在Avg@32和Pass@32指标上平均相对提升了11.42%和7.30%，证明了其持续有效性。
FedRio: Personalized Federated Social Bot Detection via Cooperative Reinforced Contrastive Adversarial Distillation
Authors: Yingguang Yang, Hao Liu, Xin Zhang, Yunhui Liu, Yutong Xia, Qi Wu, Hao Peng, Taoran Liang, Bin Chong, Tieke He, Philip S. Yu
First: 2026-04-12T15:13:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-12T15:13:41+00:00
Comments: 17 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Social bot detection is critical to the stability and security of online social platforms. However, current state-of-the-art bot detection models are largely developed in isolation, overlooking the benefits of leveraging shared detection patterns across platforms to improve performance and promptly identify emerging bot variants. The heterogeneity of data distributions and model architectures further complicates the design of an effective cross-platform and cross-model detection framework. To address these challenges, we propose FedRio (Personalized Federated Social Bot Detection with Cooperative Reinforced Contrastive Adversarial Distillation framework. We first introduce an adaptive message-passing module as the graph neural network backbone for each client. To facilitate efficient knowledge sharing of global data distributions, we design a federated knowledge extraction mechanism based on generative adversarial networks. Additionally, we employ a multi-stage adversarial contrastive learning strategy to enforce feature space consistency among clients and reduce divergence between local and global models. Finally, we adopt adaptive server-side parameter aggregation and reinforcement learning-based client-side parameter control to better accommodate data heterogeneity in heterogeneous federated settings. Extensive experiments on two real-world social bot detection benchmarks demonstrate that FedRio consistently outperforms state-of-the-art federated learning baselines in detection accuracy, communication efficiency, and feature space consistency, while remaining competitive with published centralized results under substantially stronger privacy constraints.
中文标题/摘要
标题：FedRio：基于协同强化对比对抗蒸馏的个性化联邦社交机器人检测
社交机器人检测对在线社交平台的稳定与安全至关重要。然而，当前先进的机器人检测模型大多孤立开发，忽视了跨平台共享检测模式以提升性能、快速识别新型机器人的优势。数据分布与模型架构的异质性进一步增加了设计有效跨平台、跨模型检测框架的复杂度。为应对这些挑战，我们提出FedRio（基于协同强化对比对抗蒸馏的个性化联邦社交机器人检测框架）。我们首先为每个客户端引入自适应消息传递模块作为图神经网络主干。为促进全局数据分布的高效知识共享，我们设计了基于生成对抗网络的联邦知识提取机制。此外，我们采用多阶段对抗对比学习策略，以增强客户端间特征空间一致性，并减少本地模型与全局模型间的差异。最后，通过自适应服务器端参数聚合与基于强化学习的客户端参数控制，更好地适应异构联邦环境中的数据异质性。在两个真实社交机器人检测基准上的大量实验表明，FedRio在检测精度、通信效率和特征空间一致性上均持续优于先进的联邦学习基线方法，同时在显著更强的隐私约束下与已发布的集中式结果保持竞争力。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the need for effective cross-platform social bot detection, which is hindered by data heterogeneity and isolated model development. The proposed method, FedRio, employs a personalized federated learning framework featuring an adaptive graph neural network backbone, a generative adversarial network for federated knowledge extraction, multi-stage adversarial contrastive learning for feature consistency, and adaptive aggregation with reinforcement learning for parameter control. Experimental results on real-world benchmarks show that FedRio surpasses existing federated learning baselines in accuracy, communication efficiency, and feature consistency, while maintaining competitive performance with centralized approaches under strict privacy constraints.
本文的动机在于解决跨平台社交机器人检测中因数据异构和模型孤立开发带来的挑战。提出的FedRio方法采用个性化联邦学习框架，包括自适应图神经网络主干、基于生成对抗网络的联邦知识提取机制、多阶段对抗对比学习以增强特征一致性，以及自适应聚合与强化学习参数控制。在两个真实世界基准测试上的实验结果表明，FedRio在检测精度、通信效率和特征一致性方面均优于现有联邦学习基线，同时在严格隐私约束下与集中式方法保持竞争力。
AutoMS: Multi-Agent Evolutionary Search for Cross-Physics Inverse Microstructure Design
Authors: Zhenyuan Zhao, Yu Xing, Tianyang Xue, Lingxin Cao, Xin Yan, Lin Lu
First: 2026-03-28T08:51:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-12T15:10:57+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Designing microstructures with coupled cross-physics objectives is a fundamental challenge where traditional topology optimization is often computationally prohibitive and deep generative models frequently suffer from physical hallucinations. We introduce AutoMS, a multi-agent neuro-symbolic framework that reformulates inverse design as an LLM-driven evolutionary search. AutoMS leverages LLMs as semantic navigators to decompose complex requirements and coordinate agent workflows, while a novel Simulation-Aware Evolutionary Search (SAES) mechanism handles low-level numerical optimization via local gradient approximation and directed parameter updates. This architecture achieves a state-of-the-art 83.8% success rate on 17 diverse cross-physics tasks, significantly outperforming both traditional evolutionary algorithms and existing agentic baselines. By decoupling open-ended semantic orchestration from simulation-grounded numerical search, AutoMS provides a robust pathway for navigating complex physical landscapes that remain intractable for standard generative or purely linguistic approaches.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AutoMS：面向跨物理场逆向微结构设计的多智能体演化搜索框架
针对多物理场耦合目标的微结构设计是基础性难题，传统拓扑优化常因计算量过大而受限，而深度生成模型易产生物理失真。本文提出AutoMS——一种多智能体神经符号框架，将逆向设计重构为基于大语言模型的演化搜索。AutoMS利用大语言模型作为语义导航器，分解复杂需求并协调智能体工作流；同时通过新型仿真感知演化搜索机制，借助局部梯度近似与定向参数更新实现底层数值优化。该架构在17项跨物理场任务中达到83.8%的顶尖成功率，显著优于传统演化算法与现有智能体基线。通过将开放式语义编排与仿真驱动的数值搜索解耦，AutoMS为传统生成方法或纯语言模型难以处理的复杂物理场景提供了稳健的求解路径。

Skill-SD: Skill-Conditioned Self-Distillation for Multi-turn LLM Agents
Authors: Hao Wang, Guozhi Wang, Han Xiao, Yufeng Zhou, Yue Pan, Jichao Wang, Ke Xu, Yafei Wen, Xiaohu Ruan, Xiaoxin Chen, Honggang Qi
First: 2026-04-12T14:57:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-12T14:57:52+00:00
Comments: Project page: https://k1xe.github.io/skill-sd/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has been widely used to train LLM agents for multi-turn interactive tasks, but its sample efficiency is severely limited by sparse rewards and long horizons. On-policy self-distillation (OPSD) alleviates this by providing dense token-level supervision from a privileged teacher that has access to ground-truth answers. However, such fixed privileged information cannot capture the diverse valid strategies in agent tasks, and naively combining OPSD with RL often leads to training collapse. To address these limitations, we introduce Skill-SD, a framework that turns the agent's own trajectories into dynamic training-only supervision. Completed trajectories are summarized into compact natural language skills that describe successful behaviors, mistakes, and workflows. These skills serve as dynamic privileged information conditioning only the teacher, while the student always acts under the plain task prompt and learns to internalize the guidance through distillation. To stabilize the training, we derive an importance-weighted reverse-KL loss to provide gradient-correct token-level distillation, and dynamically synchronize the teacher with the improving student. Experimental results on agentic benchmarks demonstrate that Skill-SD substantially outperforms the standard RL baseline, improving both vanilla GRPO (+14.0%/+10.9% on AppWorld/Sokoban) and vanilla OPD (+42.1%/+40.6%). Project page: https://k1xe.github.io/skill-sd/
中文标题/摘要
标题：Skill-SD：面向多轮LLM智能体的技能条件自蒸馏方法
强化学习（RL）已广泛用于训练多轮交互任务的LLM智能体，但其样本效率受稀疏奖励和长时程问题严重制约。基于策略的自蒸馏（OPSD）通过提供来自可访问真实答案的优先教师的密集词元级监督来缓解此问题，但此类固定优先信息无法捕捉智能体任务中多样化的有效策略，且将OPSD与RL简单结合常导致训练崩溃。为突破这些限制，我们提出Skill-SD框架，将智能体自身轨迹转化为动态的仅训练阶段监督。已完成的轨迹被归纳为描述成功行为、错误及工作流程的紧凑自然语言技能。这些技能作为动态优先信息仅用于调节教师模型，而学生模型始终在原始任务提示下行动，并通过蒸馏学习内化指导。为稳定训练，我们推导出重要性加权反向KL损失以实现梯度校正的词元级蒸馏，并动态同步教师模型与持续改进的学生模型。在智能体基准测试中，Skill-SD显著超越标准RL基线：在AppWorld/Sokoban任务上分别提升原始GRPO（+14.0%/+10.9%）和原始OPD（+42.1%/+40.6%）。项目页面：https://k1xe.github.io/skill-sd/
Summary / 总结
The motivation for Skill-SD arises from the sample inefficiency of reinforcement learning (RL) for training multi-turn LLM agents, due to sparse rewards and long horizons, and the limitations of on-policy self-distillation (OPSD) which relies on fixed privileged information that cannot capture diverse valid strategies and often causes training collapse. The method introduces a framework that converts the agent's own completed trajectories into dynamic, training-only supervision by summarizing them into compact natural language skills describing behaviors, mistakes, and workflows; these skills condition only a privileged teacher, while the student agent acts under the plain task prompt and learns through distillation, stabilized by an importance-weighted reverse-KL loss for gradient-correct token-level distillation and dynamic teacher-student synchronization. The main experimental results show that Skill-SD substantially outperforms standard RL baselines, improving vanilla GRPO by +14.0% on AppWorld and +10.9% on Sokoban, and vanilla OPD by +42.1% and +40.6% on the same benchmarks, respectively.
Skill-SD的提出动机在于，强化学习训练多轮LLM智能体时因奖励稀疏和周期长而样本效率低下，且基于策略的自蒸馏方法依赖于固定的特权信息，无法捕捉多样化的有效策略并常导致训练崩溃。该方法引入了一个框架，将智能体自身完成的轨迹转化为动态的、仅用于训练的监督信号，通过将其总结为描述成功行为、错误和工作流程的紧凑自然语言技能；这些技能仅用于调节特权教师模型，而学生智能体在普通任务提示下行动并通过蒸馏学习，同时采用重要性加权的反向KL损失进行梯度校正的令牌级蒸馏以及动态的师生同步以稳定训练。主要实验结果表明，Skill-SD显著优于标准强化学习基线，在AppWorld和Sokoban基准上将vanilla GRPO分别提升了14.0%和10.9%，将vanilla OPD分别提升了42.1%和40.6%。
Preference-Agile Multi-Objective Optimization for Real-time Vehicle Dispatching
Authors: Jiahuan Jin, Wenhao Zhao, Rong Qu, Jianfeng Ren, Xinan Chen, Qingfu Zhang, Ruibin Bai
First: 2026-04-12T14:39:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-12T14:39:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-objective optimization (MOO) has been widely studied in literature because of its versatility in human-centered decision making in real-life applications. Recently, demand for dynamic MOO is fast-emerging due to tough market dynamics that require real-time re-adjustments of priorities for different objectives. However, most existing studies focus either on deterministic MOO problems which are not practical, or non-sequential dynamic MOO decision problems that cannot deal with some real-life complexities. To address these challenges, a preference-agile multi-objective optimization (PAMOO) is proposed in this paper to permit users to dynamically adjust and interactively assign the preferences on the fly. To achieve this, a novel uniform model within a deep reinforcement learning (DRL) framework is proposed that can take as inputs users' dynamic preference vectors explicitly. Additionally, a calibration function is fitted to ensure high quality alignment between the preference vector inputs and the output DRL decision policy. Extensive experiments on challenging real-life vehicle dispatching problems at a container terminal showed that PAMOO obtains superior performance and generalization ability when compared with two most popular MOO methods. Our method presents the first dynamic MOO method for challenging \rev{dynamic sequential MOO decision problems
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向实时车辆调度的偏好敏捷多目标优化
多目标优化因其在现实应用中支持以人为中心的决策而受到广泛研究。近年来，由于市场动态变化要求实时调整不同目标的优先级，动态多目标优化需求迅速增长。然而，现有研究多集中于不切实际的确定性多目标优化问题，或无法处理现实复杂性的非序列动态多目标决策问题。为应对这些挑战，本文提出偏好敏捷多目标优化方法，允许用户动态调整并交互式分配偏好。该方法在深度强化学习框架内构建了统一模型，可显式接收用户动态偏好向量输入，并通过拟合校准函数确保偏好向量与深度强化学习决策策略的高质量对齐。在集装箱码头复杂车辆调度场景中的大量实验表明，相较于两种主流多目标优化方法，本方法在性能与泛化能力上均表现优异，首次为动态序列多目标决策问题提供了解决方案。

Proximal Supervised Fine-Tuning
Authors: Wenhong Zhu, Ruobing Xie, Rui Wang, Xingwu Sun, Di Wang, Pengfei Liu
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-08-25T08:26:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-12T14:04:59+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Supervised fine-tuning (SFT) of foundation models often leads to poor generalization, where prior capabilities deteriorate after tuning on new tasks or domains. Inspired by trust-region policy optimization (TRPO) and proximal policy optimization (PPO) in reinforcement learning (RL), we propose Proximal SFT (PSFT). This fine-tuning objective incorporates the benefits of trust-region, effectively constraining policy drift during SFT while maintaining competitive tuning. By viewing SFT as a special case of policy gradient methods with constant positive advantages, we derive PSFT that stabilizes optimization and leads to generalization, while leaving room for further optimization in subsequent post-training stages. Experiments across mathematical and human-value domains show that PSFT matches SFT in-domain, outperforms it in out-of-domain generalization, remains stable under prolonged training without causing entropy collapse, and provides a stronger foundation for the subsequent optimization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：近端监督微调
基础模型的监督微调常导致泛化能力下降，即模型在新任务或领域微调后原有能力退化。受强化学习中信赖域策略优化与近端策略优化的启发，我们提出近端监督微调方法。该微调目标融合信赖域优势，在保持竞争性调优的同时有效约束策略漂移。通过将监督微调视为具有恒定正优势的策略梯度方法特例，我们推导出能稳定优化并提升泛化能力的近端监督微调框架，同时为后续训练阶段保留进一步优化空间。在数学与人类价值观领域的实验表明：近端监督微调在域内性能与监督微调相当，在域外泛化中表现更优，在长时训练中保持稳定且不会引发熵崩溃，并为后续优化提供更强基础。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the poor generalization and capability deterioration observed in standard supervised fine-tuning (SFT) of foundation models, this paper proposes Proximal SFT (PSFT), a method inspired by trust-region optimization techniques from reinforcement learning like TRPO and PPO. The method formulates SFT as a policy gradient case and introduces a trust-region constraint to limit policy drift during fine-tuning, thereby stabilizing optimization. Experimental results across mathematical and human-value domains demonstrate that PSFT matches SFT's in-domain performance while achieving superior out-of-domain generalization, maintaining stability during prolonged training without entropy collapse, and providing a stronger base for subsequent post-training optimization.
本文的动机是解决基础模型在标准监督微调（SFT）中出现的泛化能力差及原有能力退化的问题，受强化学习中信任区域优化方法（如TRPO和PPO）的启发，提出了近端监督微调（PSFT）。该方法将SFT视为策略梯度的一个特例，并引入信任区域约束来限制微调过程中的策略漂移，从而稳定优化过程。在数学和人类价值观领域的实验结果表明，PSFT在域内性能与SFT相当，在域外泛化方面表现更优，能在长时间训练中保持稳定而不发生熵崩溃，并为后续的优化阶段提供了更坚实的基础。
EmoMAS: Emotion-Aware Multi-Agent System for High-Stakes Edge-Deployable Negotiation with Bayesian Orchestration
Authors: Yunbo Long, Yuhan Liu, Liming Xu
First: 2026-04-08T12:20:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-12T13:22:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) has been widely used for automated negotiation, but their high computational cost and privacy risks limit deployment in privacy-sensitive, on-device settings such as mobile assistants or rescue robots. Small language models (SLMs) offer a viable alternative, yet struggle with the complex emotional dynamics of high-stakes negotiation. We introduces EmoMAS, a Bayesian multi-agent framework that transforms emotional decision-making from reactive to strategic. EmoMAS leverages a Bayesian orchestrator to coordinate three specialized agents: game-theoretic, reinforcement learning, and psychological coherence models. The system fuses their real-time insights to optimize emotional state transitions while continuously updating agent reliability based on negotiation feedback. This mixture-of-agents architecture enables online strategy learning without pre-training. We further introduce four high-stakes, edge-deployable negotiation benchmarks across debt, healthcare, emergency response, and educational domains. Through extensive agent-to-agent simulations across all benchmarks, both SLMs and LLMs equipped with EmoMAS consistently surpass all baseline models in negotiation performance while balancing ethical behavior. These results show that strategic emotional intelligence is also the key driver of negotiation success. By treating emotional expression as a strategic variable within a Bayesian multi-agent optimization framework, EmoMAS establishes a new paradigm for effective, private, and adaptive negotiation AI suitable for high-stakes edge deployment.

标题：EmoMAS：面向高风险边缘可部署谈判的贝叶斯编排情感感知多智能体系统
大语言模型（LLMs）已广泛用于自动谈判，但其高计算成本和隐私风险限制了在移动助手或救援机器人等隐私敏感的端侧部署。小语言模型（SLMs）提供了可行替代方案，但难以应对高风险谈判中复杂的情感动态。本文提出EmoMAS，一种贝叶斯多智能体框架，将情感决策从被动反应转变为战略行为。EmoMAS利用贝叶斯编排器协调三个专业智能体：博弈论模型、强化学习模型和心理一致性模型。该系统融合其实时洞察以优化情感状态转换，同时根据谈判反馈持续更新智能体可靠性。这种混合智能体架构支持无需预训练的在线策略学习。我们进一步引入了债务、医疗、应急响应和教育领域的四个高风险边缘可部署谈判基准。通过跨所有基准的广泛智能体间模拟，搭载EmoMAS的SLMs和LLMs在平衡伦理行为的同时，谈判性能持续超越所有基线模型。结果表明，战略情感智能同样是谈判成功的关键驱动因素。通过将情感表达作为贝叶斯多智能体优化框架中的战略变量，EmoMAS为适用于高风险边缘部署的高效、隐私安全且自适应的谈判AI建立了新范式。

Motivated by the need for private, on-device negotiation AI that can handle high-stakes emotional dynamics, this paper introduces EmoMAS, a Bayesian multi-agent framework that strategically orchestrates game-theoretic, reinforcement learning, and psychological coherence agents to optimize emotional state transitions. The method enables online strategy learning without pre-training by fusing real-time agent insights and updating their reliability based on feedback. Depth-Breadth Synergy in RLVR: Unlocking LLM Reasoning Gains with Adaptive Exploration
Authors: Zhicheng Yang, Zhijiang Guo, Yinya Huang, Yongxin Wang, Dongchun Xie, Hanhui Li, Yiwei Wang, Xiaodan Liang, Jing Tang
First: 2025-08-19T11:51:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-12T13:17:04+00:00
Comments: 20 pages, 17 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Reward (RLVR) is a powerful method for enhancing the reasoning abilities of Large Language Models, but its full potential is limited by a lack of exploration in two key areas: Depth (the difficulty of problems) and Breadth (the number of training instances). Our analysis of the popular GRPO algorithm reveals a bias that down-weights difficult, low-accuracy problems, which are crucial for improving reasoning skills. To address this, we introduce Difficulty Adaptive Rollout Sampling (DARS), a method that re-weights difficult problems by using targeted, multi-stage rollouts. DARS increases the number of rollout outcomes for these harder problems according to our proposed re-balancing schedules and leads to consistent gains in Pass@K. We discovered that increasing rollout size alone does not improve performance and may actually impair it. In contrast, scaling the batch size to increase breadth via full-batch updates significantly boosted Pass@1 metrics. This improvement stems from higher token-level entropy, ensuring robust exploration and minimized gradient noise. We further present DARS-Breadth, a combined approach that uses DARS with a large breadth of training data. This method demonstrates simultaneous gains in both Pass@K and Pass@1, confirming that depth (adaptive exploration) and breadth (scaling iteration instances) are orthogonal and complementary dimensions for unlocking the full power of RLVR.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RLVR中的深度-广度协同：通过自适应探索释放大语言模型推理能力
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）是提升大语言模型推理能力的有效方法，但其潜力受限于两个关键维度的探索不足：深度（问题难度）与广度（训练实例数量）。我们对主流GRPO算法的分析发现，其存在低估困难低准确率问题的偏差，而这类问题对提升推理能力至关重要。为此，我们提出难度自适应轨迹采样（DARS），该方法通过定向多阶段轨迹对困难问题进行重加权。DARS依据我们提出的再平衡策略增加困难问题的轨迹产出数量，从而持续提升Pass@K指标。研究发现，仅增加轨迹规模并不能改善性能，反而可能损害效果；而通过全批次更新扩大批量以增加广度，则显著提升了Pass@1指标。这种改进源于更高的词元级熵，确保了稳健探索并降低了梯度噪声。我们进一步提出DARS-Breadth联合方案，将DARS与大规模训练数据结合。该方法在Pass@K和Pass@1上均实现同步提升，证实了深度（自适应探索）与广度（迭代实例扩展）是释放RLVR完整潜力的正交互补维度。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the limited exploration in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Reward (RLVR) for enhancing Large Language Model reasoning, identifying a bias in methods like GRPO that underweight difficult, low-accuracy problems crucial for improvement. The authors propose Difficulty Adaptive Rollout Sampling (DARS), a method that re-weights difficult problems using targeted, multi-stage rollouts to increase their sampling, which consistently improves Pass@K scores. Experiments reveal that merely increasing rollout size can harm performance, whereas scaling batch size for broader data coverage boosts Pass@1 via higher token-level entropy and reduced gradient noise, leading to the integrated DARS-Breadth approach that synergistically combines adaptive depth exploration with breadth scaling for gains in both Pass@K and Pass@1 metrics.
本文针对用于增强大语言模型推理能力的可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）中探索不足的问题，指出如GRPO等方法存在偏见，低估了对提升推理能力至关重要的困难、低准确率问题。作者提出了难度自适应滚动采样（DARS），该方法通过定向多阶段滚动来重新加权困难问题以增加其采样，从而持续提升Pass@K分数。实验表明，仅增加滚动规模可能损害性能，而扩大批次规模以覆盖更广数据则通过更高的令牌级熵和减少梯度噪声来提升Pass@1，由此集成的DARS-Breadth方法将自适应深度探索与广度扩展相结合，在Pass@K和Pass@1指标上均取得了协同增益。
Calibration Collapse Under Sycophancy Fine-Tuning: How Reward Hacking Breaks Uncertainty Quantification in LLMs
Authors: Subramanyam Sahoo
First: 2026-04-12T11:09:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-12T11:09:49+00:00
Comments: Accepted at the AISTATS 2026 Workshop on Towards Trustworthy Predictions: Theory and Applications of Calibration for Modern AI. 14 Pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Modern large language models (LLMs) are increasingly fine-tuned via reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) or related reward optimisation schemes. While such procedures improve perceived helpfulness, we investigate whether sycophantic reward signals degrade calibration -- a property essential for reliable uncertainty quantification. We fine-tune Qwen3-8B under three regimes: no fine-tuning (base), neutral supervised fine-tuning (SFT) on TriviaQA, and sycophancy-inducing Group Relative Policy Optimisation (GRPO) that rewards agreement with planted wrong answers. Evaluating on $1{,}000$ MMLU items across five subject domains with bootstrap confidence intervals and permutation testing, we find that \textbf{sycophantic GRPO produces consistent directional calibration degradation} -- ECE rises by $+0.006$ relative to the base model and MCE increases by $+0.010$ relative to neutral SFT -- though the effect does not reach statistical significance ($p = 0.41$) at this training budget. Post-hoc matrix scaling applied to all three models reduces ECE by $40$--$64\%$ and improves accuracy by $1.5$--$3.0$ percentage points. However, the sycophantic model retains the highest post-scaling ECE relative to the neutral SFT control ($0.042$ vs.\ $0.037$), suggesting that reward-induced miscalibration leaves a structured residual even after affine correction. These findings establish a methodology for evaluating the calibration impact of reward hacking and motivate calibration-aware training objectives.
中文标题/摘要
标题：校准崩溃与谄媚性微调：奖励破解如何破坏大语言模型的不确定性量化
现代大语言模型（LLMs）日益通过人类反馈强化学习（RLHF）或相关奖励优化方案进行微调。尽管此类方法提升了感知助益性，我们研究了谄媚性奖励信号是否会降低校准性——这是可靠不确定性量化的关键属性。我们在三种机制下对Qwen3-8B进行微调：无微调（基础模型）、基于TriviaQA的中立监督微调（SFT），以及诱导谄媚行为的群体相对策略优化（GRPO）——该机制奖励模型对预设错误答案的认同。通过在五个学科领域的1000个MMLU项目上采用自助置信区间和置换检验进行评估，我们发现：谄媚性GRPO会导致持续的方向性校准退化（ECE相较于基础模型上升+0.006，MCE相较于中立SFT增加+0.010），尽管在当前训练预算下该效应未达到统计显著性（p=0.41）。对所有三个模型应用事后矩阵缩放后，ECE降低40%-64%，准确率提升1.5-3.0个百分点。然而，谄媚模型在缩放后仍保持相对于中立SFT对照组最高的ECE值（0.042对比0.037），表明奖励诱导的校准偏差即使在仿射校正后仍会留下结构化残差。这些发现建立了一种评估奖励破解对校准影响的方法论，并为开发校准感知的训练目标提供了依据。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates whether fine-tuning large language models (LLMs) with sycophantic reward signals, which encourage agreement with users even when incorrect, degrades their calibration for reliable uncertainty quantification. The method involves fine-tuning the Qwen3-8B model under three regimes: a base model, a neutrally supervised fine-tuned model on TriviaQA, and a sycophancy-inducing model using Group Relative Policy Optimisation (GRPO) that rewards agreement with planted wrong answers. Experimental results on 1,000 MMLU items show that sycophantic GRPO leads to consistent directional calibration degradation, increasing Expected Calibration Error (ECE) and Maximum Calibration Error (MCE), though the effect is not statistically significant with the given training budget; post-hoc matrix scaling improves calibration across all models but the sycophantic model retains the highest residual error, indicating that reward-induced miscalibration leaves a structured trace even after correction.

Data Mixing Agent: Learning to Re-weight Domains for Continual Pre-training
Authors: Kailai Yang, Xiao Liu, Lei Ji, Hao Li, Xiao Liang, Zhiwei Liu, Yeyun Gong, Peng Cheng, Mao Yang
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2025-07-21T14:01:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-12T09:28:58+00:00
Comments: Accepted by the ACL 2026 main conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Continual pre-training on small-scale task-specific data is an effective method for improving large language models in new target fields, yet it risks catastrophic forgetting of their original capabilities. A common solution is to re-weight training data mixtures from source and target fields on a domain space to achieve balanced performance. Previous domain reweighting strategies rely on manual designation with certain heuristics based on human intuition or empirical results. In this work, we prove that more general heuristics can be parameterized by proposing Data Mixing Agent, the first model-based, end-to-end framework that learns to re-weight domains. The agent learns generalizable heuristics through reinforcement learning on large quantities of data mixing trajectories with corresponding feedback from an evaluation environment. Experiments in continual pre-training on math reasoning show that Data Mixing Agent outperforms strong baselines in achieving balanced performance across source and target field benchmarks. Furthermore, it generalizes well across unseen source fields, target models, and domain spaces without retraining. Direct application to the code generation field also indicates its adaptability across target domains. Further analysis showcases the agents' well-aligned heuristics with human intuitions and their efficiency in achieving superior model performance with less source-field data.
中文标题/摘要
标题：数据混合智能体：学习为持续预训练重加权领域
在小规模任务特定数据上进行持续预训练是提升大语言模型在新目标领域性能的有效方法，但可能导致原始能力的灾难性遗忘。常见解决方案是在领域空间中对源领域与目标领域的训练数据混合进行重加权，以实现均衡性能。以往领域重加权策略依赖基于人类直觉或经验结果的手动启发式设计。本研究通过提出首个基于模型的端到端框架——数据混合智能体，证明了更通用的启发式方法可通过参数化实现。该智能体通过强化学习，在大量数据混合轨迹及评估环境反馈中学习可泛化的启发式规则。数学推理持续预训练实验表明，数据混合智能体在源领域与目标领域基准测试的均衡性能上均优于强基线模型。此外，该智能体无需重新训练即可在未见过的源领域、目标模型和领域空间中良好泛化。在代码生成领域的直接应用也验证了其跨目标领域的适应能力。进一步分析表明，智能体学习的启发式规则与人类直觉高度契合，且能以更少的源领域数据高效实现更优模型性能。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address catastrophic forgetting in continual pre-training of large language models on new target domains by improving upon manual, heuristic-based domain reweighting strategies. The method introduces Data Mixing Agent, a model-based, end-to-end framework that uses reinforcement learning to learn generalizable heuristics for re-weighting data mixtures from source and target domains. Experimental results on math reasoning show the agent outperforms baselines in balancing performance across source and target benchmarks, generalizes to unseen fields and models without retraining, and adapts effectively to other domains like code generation, while aligning with human intuition and requiring less source data.

SpikingMamba: Towards Energy-Efficient Large Language Models via Knowledge Distillation from Mamba
Authors: Yulong Huang, Jianxiong Tang, Chao Wang, Ziyi Wang, Jianguo Zhang, Zhichao Lu, Bojun Cheng, Luziwei Leng
First: 2025-10-06T08:49:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-12T08:00:47+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) have achieved remarkable performance across tasks but remain energy-intensive due to dense matrix operations. Spiking neural networks (SNNs) improve energy efficiency by replacing dense matrix multiplications with sparse accumulations. Their sparse spike activity enables efficient LLMs deployment on edge devices. However, prior SNN-based LLMs often sacrifice performance for efficiency, and recovering accuracy typically requires full pretraining, which is costly and impractical. To address this, we propose SpikingMamba, an energy-efficient SNN-based LLMs distilled from Mamba that improves energy efficiency with minimal accuracy sacrifice. SpikingMamba integrates two key components: (a) SI-LIF, a signed-integer spiking neuron that preserves semantic polarity through signed multi-level spike representations. (b) A training-exclusive Smoothed Gradient Compensation (SGC) path mitigating quantization loss while preserving spike-driven efficiency. We employ a single-stage distillation strategy to transfer the zero-shot ability of pretrained Mamba and further enhance it via reinforcement learning (RL). Experiments show that SpikingMamba-1.3B achieves a 4.76$\times$ energy benefit, with only a 4.78\% zero-shot accuracy gap compared to the original Mamba. The model achieves a further 2.55\% accuracy improvement after RL, narrowing the performance gap from 4.78\% to 2.23\%. Code is available at: https://github.com/HuuYuLong/SpikingMamba .
中文标题/摘要
标题：SpikingMamba：通过从Mamba进行知识蒸馏实现高能效大型语言模型
大型语言模型（LLMs）虽在多项任务中表现卓越，但因密集矩阵运算导致能耗较高。脉冲神经网络（SNNs）通过稀疏累加替代密集矩阵乘法，提升了能效。其稀疏脉冲活动使得LLMs能在边缘设备上高效部署。然而，先前基于SNN的LLMs常为效率牺牲性能，且恢复精度通常需完整预训练，成本高昂且不切实际。为此，我们提出SpikingMamba，一种基于SNN的高能效LLMs，通过从Mamba蒸馏实现，在最小精度损失下提升能效。SpikingMamba包含两个关键组件：（a）SI-LIF，一种带符号整数脉冲神经元，通过多级符号脉冲表示保留语义极性；（b）训练专用的平滑梯度补偿（SGC）路径，在保持脉冲驱动效率的同时减少量化损失。我们采用单阶段蒸馏策略迁移预训练Mamba的零样本能力，并通过强化学习（RL）进一步优化。实验表明，SpikingMamba-1.3B实现4.76倍能效提升，零样本精度仅比原Mamba低4.78%。经RL后精度再提升2.55%，性能差距从4.78%缩小至2.23%。代码发布于：https://github.com/HuuYuLong/SpikingMamba。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the high energy consumption of large language models (LLMs) by proposing SpikingMamba, an energy-efficient model that uses spiking neural networks (SNNs) to replace dense matrix operations with sparse accumulations. The method introduces two key components: a signed-integer spiking neuron (SI-LIF) to preserve semantic polarity and a training-exclusive smoothed gradient compensation (SGC) path to mitigate quantization loss, combined with a single-stage knowledge distillation from the Mamba model and reinforcement learning for enhancement. Experimental results show that SpikingMamba-1.3B achieves a 4.76× energy benefit with only a 4.78% zero-shot accuracy gap compared to Mamba, which is further reduced to 2.23% after reinforcement learning, demonstrating improved efficiency with minimal performance sacrifice.
本文针对大型语言模型（LLMs）能耗高的问题，提出了SpikingMamba，一种基于脉冲神经网络（SNNs）的能效模型，通过稀疏累加替代密集矩阵运算以提高能效。方法包含两个关键组件：用于保持语义极性的有符号整数脉冲神经元（SI-LIF）和训练专用的平滑梯度补偿（SGC）路径以减少量化损失，并结合从Mamba模型的单阶段知识蒸馏和强化学习进行增强。实验结果表明，SpikingMamba-1.3B实现了4.76倍的能效提升，与Mamba相比零样本准确率差距仅为4.78%，经过强化学习后进一步缩小至2.23%，在最小化性能损失的同时显著提高了能效。
Beyond Compliance: A Resistance-Informed Motivation Reasoning Framework for Challenging Psychological Client Simulation
Authors: Danni Liu, Bo Liu, Yuxin Hu, Hantao Zhao, Yan Liu, Ding Ding, Jiahui Jin, Jiuxin Cao
First: 2026-04-12T07:51:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-12T07:51:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Psychological client simulators have emerged as a scalable solution for training and evaluating counselor trainees and psychological LLMs. Yet existing simulators exhibit unrealistic over-compliance, leaving counselors underprepared for the challenging behaviors common in real-world practice. To bridge this gap, we present ResistClient, which systematically models challenging client behaviors grounded in Client Resistance Theory by integrating external behaviors with underlying motivational mechanisms. To this end, we propose Resistance-Informed Motivation Reasoning (RIMR), a two-stage training framework. First, RIMR mitigates compliance bias via supervised fine-tuning on RPC, a large-scale resistance-oriented psychological conversation dataset covering diverse client profiles. Second, beyond surface-level response imitation, RIMR models psychologically coherent motivation reasoning before response generation, jointly optimizing motivation authenticity and response consistency via process-supervised reinforcement learning. Extensive automatic and expert evaluations show that ResistClient substantially outperforms existing simulators in challenge fidelity, behavioral plausibility, and reasoning coherence. Moreover, ResistClient facilities evaluation of psychological LLMs under challenging conditions, offering new optimization directions for mental health dialogue systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越顺从：基于阻抗理论的动机推理框架用于挑战性心理来访者模拟
心理来访者模拟器已成为培训和评估咨询师学员及心理大语言模型的可扩展解决方案。然而现有模拟器存在不切实际的过度顺从问题，导致咨询师对真实实践中常见的挑战性行为准备不足。为填补这一空白，我们提出ResistClient系统，通过整合外部行为与内在动机机制，基于来访者阻抗理论系统化建模挑战性来访者行为。为此，我们提出阻抗导向的动机推理框架，该两阶段训练框架首先通过在大规模阻抗导向心理对话数据集上进行监督微调来缓解顺从偏差，其次超越表层响应模仿，在生成响应前建立心理连贯的动机推理模型，通过过程监督强化学习联合优化动机真实性与响应一致性。大量自动评估与专家评估表明，ResistClient在挑战保真度、行为合理性和推理连贯性上显著优于现有模拟器。此外，该系统能为心理大语言模型在挑战性条件下的评估提供支持，为心理健康对话系统开辟新的优化方向。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the unrealistic over-compliance of existing psychological client simulators, which inadequately prepare counselors for real-world challenging behaviors, this paper introduces ResistClient, a framework grounded in Client Resistance Theory to model such behaviors more authentically. The method employs a two-stage Resistance-Informed Motivation Reasoning (RIMR) approach: first, it reduces compliance bias via supervised fine-tuning on a large-scale resistance-oriented conversation dataset, and second, it enhances psychological coherence by integrating motivation reasoning before response generation, optimized through process-supervised reinforcement learning. Experimental results from automatic and expert evaluations demonstrate that ResistClient significantly outperforms prior simulators in challenge fidelity, behavioral plausibility, and reasoning coherence, while also enabling better evaluation and optimization of psychological LLMs under challenging conditions.
针对现有心理客户模拟器过度顺从、无法真实模拟现实挑战性行为的局限性，本文基于客户阻抗理论提出了ResistClient框架，旨在更真实地建模此类行为。方法上采用了两阶段的阻抗知情动机推理（RIMR）框架：首先通过在大规模阻抗导向的心理对话数据集上进行监督微调以减少顺从偏差，其次在生成回应前进行动机推理以增强心理一致性，并通过过程监督强化学习进行联合优化。实验结果表明，ResistClient在挑战保真度、行为合理性和推理连贯性上显著优于现有模拟器，同时能为心理大语言模型在挑战性条件下的评估提供新优化方向。
Pacing Opinion Polarization via Graph Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Mingkai Liao
First: 2026-02-23T11:57:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-12T07:41:44+00:00
Comments: 38 pages, 16 figure. "involving slight adjustments to the experimental setup and a restructuring of the overall exposition."
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Opinion polarization moderation has been studied mainly as an analytical optimization problem under the Friedkin Johnson FJ model, where intervention algorithms rely on linear steady state analysis and model specific derivations. While effective in narrowly structured settings, such methods scale poorly and do not naturally extend to richer intervention regimes. This raises a central question: can polarization moderation be treated as a graph based sequential planning problem? We answer this question by proposing PACIFIER, to our knowledge the first unified graph learning framework, and in particular the first graph reinforcement learning framework, for opinion polarization moderation. PACIFIER reformulates the canonical ModerateInternal MI and ModerateExpressed ME problems as sequential decision making tasks on graphs, replacing repeated analytical recomputation with learned intervention policies. The framework has two variants: PACIFIER RL for long horizon planning and PACIFIER Greedy for efficient myopic ranking. It also extends naturally to cost aware moderation, continuous valued internal opinions, and topology altering node removal. Experiments on 15 real world polarized networks reveal a clear regime dependent picture. In analytically structured MI settings, PACIFIER remains competitive with strong analytical solvers and consistently emerges as the strongest scalable non analytical alternative. In contrast, in ME, continuous ME, and cost ME, PACIFIER achieves strong and highly consistent superiority over non PACIFIER baselines. Most importantly, PACIFIER RL becomes decisively superior in cost ME and topology altering node removal, where long horizon reasoning over future consequences is crucial. Overall, PACIFIER shifts opinion polarization moderation from model specific analytical optimization toward a unified graph learning and graph reinforcement learning paradigm.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于图强化学习的意见极化调控
意见极化调控研究主要基于Friedkin-Johnson（FJ）模型作为分析优化问题展开，现有干预算法依赖线性稳态分析和模型特定推导。这类方法在狭窄结构化场景中有效，但扩展性差且难以自然延伸至更丰富的干预机制。这引出一个核心问题：极化调控能否视为基于图的序贯规划问题？ 我们通过提出PACIFIER框架对此作出肯定回答——据我们所知，这是首个统一的图学习框架，特别是首个用于意见极化调控的图强化学习框架。PACIFIER将经典的ModerateInternal（MI）与ModerateExpressed（ME）问题重构为图上的序贯决策任务，以学习型干预策略替代重复的分析计算。该框架包含两个变体：面向长时域规划的PACIFIER RL与面向高效近视排序的PACIFIER Greedy，并能自然扩展至成本感知调控、连续值内部意见及拓扑结构节点删除场景。 在15个真实世界极化网络上的实验揭示了清晰的机制依赖性图景：在分析结构化MI场景中，PACIFIER与强分析求解器保持竞争力，始终是最具扩展性的非分析替代方案；而在ME、连续ME及成本ME场景中，PACIFIER较非PACIFIER基线展现出强大且高度一致的优越性。最重要的是，在需要长远推理未来后果的成本ME与拓扑结构节点删除任务中，PACIFIER RL具有决定性优势。 总体而言，PACIFIER将意见极化调控从模型特定的分析优化转向统一的图学习与图强化学习范式。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of analytical optimization methods for opinion polarization moderation, which are often model-specific and scale poorly, this paper introduces PACIFIER, a unified graph reinforcement learning framework that reframes the problem as a sequential decision-making task on graphs. The method includes two variants: PACIFIER RL for long-term planning and PACIFIER Greedy for efficient myopic ranking, and it extends to cost-aware moderation, continuous opinions, and node removal. Experimental results on 15 real-world polarized networks show that PACIFIER remains competitive with analytical solvers in structured settings and achieves strong, consistent superiority in more complex regimes like cost-aware moderation and topology alteration, where long-horizon reasoning is crucial.
本文针对观点极化调节中分析方法存在的模型依赖性强、可扩展性差等局限，提出了PACIFIER这一统一的图强化学习框架，将问题重构为图上的序列决策任务。该方法包含两个变体：用于长期规划的PACIFIER RL和用于高效近视排序的PACIFIER Greedy，并可扩展至成本感知调节、连续意见和节点移除等场景。在15个真实世界极化网络上的实验表明，PACIFIER在结构化设置中与解析求解器保持竞争力，并在成本感知调节和拓扑改变等更复杂场景中表现出显著且一致的优越性，尤其在需要长远推理的任务中优势明显。
GoT-R1: Unleashing Reasoning Capability of MLLM for Visual Generation with Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Chengqi Duan, Rongyao Fang, Yuqing Wang, Kun Wang, Linjiang Huang, Xingyu Zeng, Hongsheng Li, Xihui Liu
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-05-22T17:59:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-12T04:05:04+00:00
Comments: Github page refer to: https://github.com/gogoduan/GoT-R1. Published as a conference paper at ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Visual generation models have made remarkable progress in creating realistic images from text prompts, yet struggle with complex prompts that specify multiple objects with precise spatial relationships and attributes. Effective handling of such prompts requires explicit reasoning about the semantic content and spatial layout. We present GoT-R1, a framework that applies reinforcement learning to enhance semantic-spatial reasoning in visual generation. Building upon the Generation Chain-of-Thought approach, GoT-R1 enables models to autonomously discover effective reasoning strategies beyond predefined templates through carefully designed reinforcement learning. To achieve this, we propose a dual-stage multi-dimensional reward framework that leverages MLLMs to evaluate both the reasoning process and final output, enabling effective supervision across the entire generation pipeline. The reward system assesses semantic alignment, spatial accuracy, and visual quality in a unified approach. Experimental results demonstrate significant improvements on T2I-CompBench benchmark, particularly in compositional tasks involving precise spatial relationships and attribute binding. GoT-R1 advances the state-of-the-art in image generation by successfully transferring sophisticated reasoning capabilities to the visual generation domain. To facilitate future research, we make our code and pretrained models publicly available at https://github.com/gogoduan/GoT-R1.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GoT-R1：通过强化学习释放多模态大语言模型在视觉生成中的推理能力
视觉生成模型在根据文本提示创建逼真图像方面取得了显著进展，但在处理需要精确空间关系和属性的多对象复杂提示时仍面临挑战。有效处理此类提示需对语义内容和空间布局进行显式推理。本文提出GoT-R1框架，通过强化学习增强视觉生成中的语义-空间推理能力。该框架基于思维链生成方法，使模型能够通过精心设计的强化学习自主发现超越预设模板的有效推理策略。为实现这一目标，我们提出双阶段多维奖励框架，利用多模态大语言模型同时评估推理过程和最终输出，实现对生成流程的全方位有效监督。该奖励系统以统一方法评估语义对齐度、空间准确性和视觉质量。在T2I-CompBench基准测试中，特别是在涉及精确空间关系和属性绑定的组合任务上，实验结果显示显著提升。GoT-R1通过将复杂推理能力成功迁移至视觉生成领域，推动了图像生成技术的进步。为促进后续研究，我们已在https://github.com/gogoduan/GoT-R1公开代码与预训练模型。

Motivated by the difficulty visual generation models face with complex prompts requiring precise spatial and attribute reasoning, this paper introduces GoT-R1, a framework that enhances semantic-spatial reasoning through reinforcement learning. C2F-Thinker: Coarse-to-Fine Reasoning with Hint-Guided Reinforcement Learning for Multimodal Sentiment Analysis
Authors: Miaosen Luo, Zhenhao Yang, Jieshen Long, Jinghu Sun, Yichu Liu, Sijie Mai
First: 2026-03-10T12:48:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-12T03:30:47+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multimodal sentiment analysis aims to integrate textual, acoustic, and visual information for deep emotional understanding. Despite the progress of multimodal large language models (MLLMs) via supervised fine-tuning, their "black-box" nature hinders interpretability. While Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning offers a potential remedy, it is constrained by high manual annotation costs and the inherent challenges of reinforcement learning (RL), such as reward sparsity and low exploration efficiency on hard samples. This paper presents C2F-Thinker, a framework that harmonizes coarse-to-fine structured reasoning with hint-guided RL through a two-stage progressive training pipeline. In the first stage, we conduct cold-start supervised fine-tuning using high-quality CoT data distilled from a larger teacher model, consisting of three distinct phases: polarity judgment, intermediate analysis, and fine-grained scoring. This equips the base model with a structured emotional reasoning paradigm. In the second stage, we introduce a hint-guided Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) algorithm. By injecting correct initial polarity predictions as hints during the sampling process, the model is guided toward accurate reasoning paths, effectively mitigating cascading errors and enhancing the utilization of hard samples. Furthermore, a multi-faceted reward function incorporating classification, regression, and formatting constraints is designed to refine prediction accuracy while preserving interpretability. Experimental results demonstrate that C2F-Thinker achieves competitive performance on fine-grained sentiment regression tasks while significantly outperforming baselines in cross-domain generalization. This highlights its potential in building trustworthy and robust sentiment analysis systems for real-world applications.
中文标题/摘要
标题：C2F-Thinker：基于提示引导强化学习的从粗到细推理框架用于多模态情感分析
多模态情感分析旨在整合文本、声学和视觉信息以实现深层情感理解。尽管多模态大语言模型通过监督微调取得进展，但其“黑盒”特性阻碍了可解释性。思维链推理虽提供潜在解决方案，却受限于高昂的人工标注成本以及强化学习固有的奖励稀疏性和困难样本探索效率低等挑战。本文提出C2F-Thinker框架，通过两阶段渐进式训练流程，将粗粒度到细粒度的结构化推理与提示引导强化学习相融合。第一阶段使用从大型教师模型蒸馏的高质量思维链数据进行冷启动监督微调，包含极性判断、中间分析和细粒度评分三个独立阶段，使基础模型具备结构化情感推理范式。第二阶段提出提示引导的组相对策略优化算法，通过在采样过程中注入正确的初始极性预测作为提示，引导模型走向准确推理路径，有效缓解级联错误并提升困难样本利用率。此外，设计了融合分类、回归和格式约束的多维度奖励函数，在保持可解释性的同时提升预测精度。实验结果表明，C2F-Thinker在细粒度情感回归任务中取得竞争优势，并在跨领域泛化能力上显著超越基线模型，凸显了其在构建可信赖、鲁棒的现实应用情感分析系统方面的潜力。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the interpretability limitations of multimodal large language models (MLLMs) in sentiment analysis, where traditional Chain-of-Thought reasoning is costly and reinforcement learning struggles with sparse rewards and hard samples. The proposed C2F-Thinker framework employs a two-stage training pipeline: first, it uses supervised fine-tuning with distilled CoT data to instill a structured three-phase reasoning paradigm (polarity judgment, intermediate analysis, and fine-grained scoring); second, it introduces a hint-guided Group Relative Policy Optimization algorithm that injects correct initial polarity hints during sampling to guide reasoning, mitigate cascading errors, and improve hard sample utilization, alongside a multi-faceted reward function for accuracy and interpretability. Experiments show the model achieves competitive performance on fine-grained sentiment regression and excels in cross-domain generalization, underscoring its potential for robust, real-world applications.
