Safety Guarantees in Zero-Shot Reinforcement Learning for Cascade Dynamical Systems
Authors: Shima Rabiei, Sandipan Mishra, Santiago Paternain
First: 2026-04-12T02:53:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-12T02:53:52+00:00
Comments: 8 pages, 2 figures; submitted to IEEE for possible publication
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper considers the problem of zero-shot safety guarantees for cascade dynamical systems. These are systems where a subset of the states (the inner states) affects the dynamics of the remaining states (the outer states) but not vice-versa. We define safety as remaining on a set deemed safe for all times with high probability. We propose to train a safe RL policy on a reduced-order model, which ignores the dynamics of the inner states, but it treats it as an action that influences the outer state. Thus, reducing the complexity of the training. When deployed in the full system the trained policy is combined with a low-level controller whose task is to track the reference provided by the RL policy. Our main theoretical contribution is a bound on the safe probability in the full-order system. In particular, we establish the interplay between the probability of remaining safe after the zero-shot deployment and the quality of the tracking of the inner states. We validate our theoretical findings on a quadrotor navigation task, demonstrating that the preservation of the safety guarantees is tied to the bandwidth and tracking capabilities of the low-level controller.
中文标题/摘要
标题：级联动态系统零样本强化学习中的安全保证
本文研究级联动态系统的零样本安全保证问题。这类系统的部分状态（内部状态）会影响其余状态（外部状态）的动态特性，反之则不成立。我们将安全性定义为以高概率始终保持在预设安全集合内。我们提出在降阶模型上训练安全强化学习策略，该模型忽略内部状态的动态特性，将其视为影响外部状态的动作输入，从而降低训练复杂度。在完整系统中部署时，训练后的策略将与底层控制器结合，该控制器的任务是跟踪强化学习策略提供的参考轨迹。我们的主要理论贡献是给出了完整系统安全概率的边界条件，特别阐明了零样本部署后保持安全的概率与内部状态跟踪精度之间的相互作用关系。我们在四旋翼飞行器导航任务中验证了理论结果，证明安全保证的保持程度与底层控制器的带宽及跟踪能力密切相关。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of ensuring safety in zero-shot reinforcement learning for cascade dynamical systems, where inner states influence outer states but not vice versa. The motivation is to provide probabilistic safety guarantees when deploying a policy trained on a simplified model. The method involves training a safe RL policy on a reduced-order model that treats inner states as actions, thereby lowering training complexity, and then combining it with a low-level tracking controller for full-system deployment. The main theoretical result is a bound on the safe probability in the full-order system, linking safety preservation to the tracking quality of the inner states. Experimental validation on a quadrotor navigation task confirms that safety guarantees depend on the bandwidth and tracking performance of the low-level controller.
本文研究了级联动力系统中零样本强化学习的安全保障问题，其中内部状态影响外部状态但反之不成立。动机是在部署基于简化模型训练的策略时提供概率性安全保证。方法包括在降阶模型上训练安全RL策略，将内部状态视为动作以降低训练复杂度，然后结合低级跟踪控制器进行全系统部署。主要理论成果是给出了全阶系统中安全概率的界限，将安全保持与内部状态的跟踪质量联系起来。在四旋翼导航任务上的实验验证表明，安全保障取决于低级控制器的带宽和跟踪能力。
A Queueing-Theoretic Framework for Dynamic Attack Surfaces: Data-Integrated Risk Analysis and Adaptive Defense
Authors: Jihyeon Yun, Abdullah Yasin Etcibasi, Ming Shi, C. Emre Koksal
First: 2026-04-12T02:52:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-12T02:52:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We develop a queueing-theoretic framework to model the temporal evolution of cyber-attack surfaces, where the number of active vulnerabilities is represented as the backlog of a queue. Vulnerabilities arrive as they are discovered or created, and leave the system when they are patched or successfully exploited. Building on this model, we study how automation affects attack and defense dynamics by introducing an AI amplification factor that scales arrival, exploit, and patching rates. Our analysis shows that even symmetric automation can increase the rate of successful exploits. We validate the model using vulnerability data collected from an open source software supply chain and show that it closely matches real-world attack surface dynamics. Empirical results reveal heavy-tailed patching times, which we prove induce long-range dependence in vulnerability backlog and help explain persistent cyber risk. Utilizing our queueing abstraction for the attack surface, we develop a systematic approach for cyber risk mitigation. We formulate the dynamic defense problem as a constrained Markov decision process with resource-budget and switching-cost constraints, and develop a reinforcement learning (RL) algorithm that achieves provably near-optimal regret. Numerical experiments validate the approach and demonstrate that our adaptive RL-based defense policies significantly reduce successful exploits and mitigate heavy-tail queue events. Using trace-driven experiments on the ARVO dataset, we show that the proposed RL-based defense policy reduces the average number of active vulnerabilities in a software supply chain by over 90% compared to existing defense practices, without increasing the overall maintenance budget. Our results allow defenders to quantify cumulative exposure risk under long-range dependent attack dynamics and to design adaptive defense strategies with provable efficiency.
中文标题/摘要
标题：动态攻击面的排队论框架：数据集成风险分析与自适应防御
我们开发了一个排队论框架来建模网络攻击面的时间演化，其中活跃漏洞数量被表示为队列积压。漏洞随着被发现或创建而到达，并在被修补或成功利用后离开系统。基于此模型，我们通过引入一个放大到达、利用和修补速率的AI放大因子，研究自动化如何影响攻击与防御动态。分析表明，即使对称自动化也会增加成功利用的速率。我们使用从开源软件供应链收集的漏洞数据验证模型，并证明其与现实世界攻击面动态高度吻合。实证结果揭示了重尾修补时间，我们证明这会引发漏洞积压的长程依赖性，并有助于解释持续的网络风险。利用攻击面的排队抽象，我们开发了一种系统性的网络风险缓解方法。将动态防御问题建模为具有资源预算和切换成本约束的约束马尔可夫决策过程，并设计了一种强化学习算法，可实现可证明的近似最优遗憾。数值实验验证了该方法，并表明我们基于强化学习的自适应防御策略显著减少了成功利用并缓解了重尾队列事件。通过在ARVO数据集上进行追踪驱动实验，我们证明所提出的基于强化学习的防御策略相比现有防御实践，在不增加总体维护预算的情况下，将软件供应链中的平均活跃漏洞数量降低了90%以上。我们的研究使防御者能够量化长程依赖攻击动态下的累积暴露风险，并设计具有可证明效率的自适应防御策略。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to model the dynamic nature of cyber-attack surfaces, this paper develops a queueing-theoretic framework where active vulnerabilities are treated as a queue backlog, with arrivals from discoveries and departures from patching or exploitation. The method incorporates an AI amplification factor to analyze automation's impact on attack and defense dynamics, and formulates dynamic defense as a constrained Markov decision process, solved via a reinforcement learning algorithm. Experimental results, validated on open-source software supply chain data, show that even symmetric automation increases exploit rates, reveal heavy-tailed patching times leading to long-range dependence in risk, and demonstrate that the proposed RL-based defense reduces active vulnerabilities by over 90% without extra budget.
本文旨在建模网络攻击面的动态演化，其动机源于需要量化持续的网络风险。方法上，提出了一个排队论框架，将活跃漏洞视为队列积压，并引入AI放大因子来分析自动化对攻防动态的影响，进而将动态防御问题构建为带约束的马尔可夫决策过程，并通过强化学习算法求解。主要实验结果基于开源软件供应链数据验证，表明即使对称的自动化也会增加漏洞利用率，揭示了重尾修补时间导致风险的长期依赖性，并且所提出的基于强化学习的防御策略在不增加预算的情况下，将活跃漏洞平均数量降低了90%以上。
Reinforcement Learning for Intensity Control: An Application to Choice-Based Network Revenue Management
Authors: Huiling Meng, Ningyuan Chen, Xuefeng Gao
First: 2024-06-08T05:27:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-12T00:40:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Intensity control is a class of continuous-time dynamic optimization problems with many important applications in Operations Research including queueing and revenue management. In this study, we propose a practical continuous-time reinforcement learning framework for intensity control using choice-based network revenue management as a case study, which is a classical problem in revenue management that features a large state space, a large action space, and a continuous time horizon. We show that by leveraging the event-driven structure of the problem and the inherent discretization of sample paths created by the state-jump times, a defining feature of intensity control, one does not need to discretize the time horizon in advance. We adapt discrete-time Monte Carlo and temporal difference learning algorithms for policy evaluation to continuous time and develop policy-gradient-based actor-critic algorithms for event-driven intensity control. Through a comprehensive numerical study, we evaluate the proposed approach against various state-of-the-art benchmarks, demonstrating its overall superior performance and effective scalability to large-scale problems. Notably, compared to discretization-based reinforcement learning methods, our continuous-time approach delivers significantly superior performance while maintaining comparable computational efficiency. This advantage is particularly pronounced in highly non-stationary environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习在强度控制中的应用：基于选择的网络收益管理案例研究
强度控制是一类连续时间动态优化问题，在运筹学的排队论和收益管理等领域具有重要应用。本研究以基于选择的网络收益管理这一经典问题为案例，提出了一个实用的连续时间强化学习框架。该问题具有状态空间大、动作空间大、时间连续的特点。我们证明，通过利用问题的事件驱动结构以及状态跳变时间（强度控制的定义特征）产生的样本路径固有离散化，无需预先离散化时间范围。我们将离散时间的蒙特卡洛法和时序差分学习策略评估算法适配到连续时间，并开发了基于策略梯度的事件驱动强度控制执行者-评论者算法。通过全面的数值研究，我们将所提方法与多种先进基准进行比较，证明其整体优越性能及对大规模问题的有效扩展性。值得注意的是，与基于离散化的强化学习方法相比，我们的连续时间方法在保持相当计算效率的同时，性能显著更优，这一优势在高度非平稳环境中尤为明显。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to address complex continuous-time dynamic optimization problems in operations research, such as choice-based network revenue management which involves large state and action spaces over continuous time, this paper proposes a practical continuous-time reinforcement learning framework for intensity control. The method leverages the event-driven structure and state-jump times inherent in intensity control to avoid pre-discretization of the time horizon, adapting Monte Carlo and temporal difference learning for policy evaluation and developing policy-gradient-based actor-critic algorithms for event-driven control. Experimental results from a comprehensive numerical study show that the approach outperforms state-of-the-art benchmarks, offering superior performance and scalability, especially in non-stationary environments, while maintaining computational efficiency comparable to discretization-based methods.
本研究针对运筹学中如基于选择的网络收益管理等连续时间动态优化问题，这些问题具有大状态空间、大动作空间和连续时间的特点，提出了一种实用的连续时间强化学习框架用于强度控制。方法利用强度控制中事件驱动结构和状态跳跃时间的固有特性，避免了预先离散化时间轴，并改编了蒙特卡洛和时间差分学习算法进行策略评估，开发了基于策略梯度的行动者-评论者算法用于事件驱动控制。综合数值实验结果表明，该方法在多种先进基准测试中表现优异，展现出卓越的性能和可扩展性，尤其在非平稳环境中优势明显，同时保持了与离散化方法相当的计算效率。
Semantic-Space Exploration and Exploitation in RLVR for LLM Reasoning
Authors: Fanding Huang, Guanbo Huang, Xiao Fan, Yi He, Xiao Liang, Xiao Chen, Qinting Jiang, Faisal Nadeem Khan, Jingyan Jiang, Zhi Wang
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2025-09-28T11:14:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-11T20:06:38+00:00
Comments: Accepted as an ACL 2026 Findings paper
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) for LLM reasoning is often framed as balancing exploration and exploitation in action space, typically operationalized with token-level proxies (e.g., output entropy or confidence). We argue that this apparent trade-off is largely a measurement artifact: token-level statistics reflect next-token uncertainty rather than how reasoning progresses over multi-token semantic structures. We therefore study exploration and exploitation in the hidden-state space of response trajectories. We use Effective Rank (ER) to quantify representational exploration and introduce its temporal derivatives, Effective Rank Velocity (ERV) and Effective Rank Acceleration (ERA), to characterize exploitative refinement dynamics. Empirically and theoretically, ER and ERV exhibit near-zero correlation in semantic space, suggesting the two capacities can be improved simultaneously. Motivated by this, we propose Velocity-Exploiting Rank Learning (VERL), which shapes the RL advantage with an auxiliary signal derived from ER/ERV and uses the more stable ERA as a meta-control variable to adaptively balance the incentives. Across multiple base models, RL algorithms, and reasoning benchmarks, VERL yields consistent improvements, including large gains on challenging tasks (e.g., 21.4\% in Gaokao 2024).
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向大语言模型推理的RLVR中语义空间的探索与利用
面向大语言模型推理的可验证奖励强化学习常被视作动作空间中探索与利用的权衡问题，通常通过词元级代理指标（如输出熵或置信度）实现。我们认为这种表面权衡主要是测量假象：词元级统计量反映的是下一词元的不确定性，而非推理在多词元语义结构上的推进过程。因此，我们研究响应轨迹隐状态空间中的探索与利用机制。采用有效秩量化表征探索，并引入其时间导数——有效秩速度与有效秩加速度——刻画利用性精炼动态。实证与理论分析表明，语义空间中有效秩与有效秩速度呈近零相关性，提示两种能力可同步提升。基于此，我们提出速度利用秩学习算法，通过有效秩/有效秩速度衍生的辅助信号塑造强化学习优势函数，并采用更稳定的有效秩加速度作为元控制变量自适应平衡激励权重。在多种基模型、强化学习算法与推理基准测试中，该算法均取得稳定提升，在挑战性任务上表现尤为显著（如2024年高考题提升21.4%）。
Summary / 总结
The paper challenges the conventional view of balancing exploration and exploitation in token-level action spaces for Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) in LLM reasoning, arguing it is a measurement artifact that fails to capture multi-token semantic progress. Instead, it proposes studying these dynamics in the hidden-state space of response trajectories, using Effective Rank (ER) to quantify exploration and introducing its temporal derivatives, Effective Rank Velocity (ERV) and Effective Rank Acceleration (ERA), to characterize exploitative refinement. The method reveals near-zero correlation between ER and ERV in semantic space, indicating these capacities can be improved simultaneously, leading to the Velocity-Exploiting Rank Learning (VERL) approach, which shapes RL advantages with ER/ERV signals and uses ERA for adaptive balancing. Experimental results across models, algorithms, and benchmarks show consistent improvements, including significant gains on challenging tasks like a 21.4% increase on Gaokao 2024.
本文对大型语言模型推理中可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）在词元级动作空间平衡探索与利用的传统观点提出挑战，认为这是一种测量假象，无法捕捉多词元语义进展。相反，它提出在响应轨迹的隐藏状态空间中研究这些动态，使用有效秩（ER）量化探索，并引入其时间导数——有效秩速度（ERV）和有效秩加速度（ERA）——来表征利用性细化。该方法揭示了语义空间中ER与ERV近乎零相关，表明这两种能力可同时提升，从而提出了速度利用秩学习（VERL）方法，该方法利用ER/ERV信号塑造RL优势，并使用ERA进行自适应平衡。在多个基础模型、算法和基准测试上的实验结果显示了一致的性能提升，包括在高考2024等挑战性任务上实现21.4%的显著增益。
